Endzabeni yesihloko sema-AM, Ikhomishini ikhetse I-Welsh Parliament Members noma ema-WMP, kepha sincomo se-MWP sitfole kusekelwa kakhulu ngesikhatsi kucociswana nesive.
Ema-AMs shengatsi aphakamisa letinye tincomo, kepha lomshikashika bekufika esivumelwaneni kungabangela uMphatsi Lophetse, Elin Jones, inhloko, kantsi kubhekeke kutsi abhale imitsetfo ngaletingucuko esikhatsini semaviki lambalwa.
Imitsetfo kuletingucuko itawufaka ekhatsi letinye tingucuko tenchubo yekusebenta kwendlu yabayesikhulu, lokufaka ekhatsi imitsetfo yekukhipha ema-AM nendlela yekwakhiwa kwekusebentisana kwemakomiti.

“Emabhara akasesiwo emagumbi lekuhlalwa kuwo emphakatsini, lapho bantfu baya khona njalonjalo.”
Ngemasontfo-ke wona kumkhatsata kutsi lemali yekutsengisa imphahla angeke ihlale sikhatsi lesidze njengoba baphatsi babhekile, “futsi esikhatsini lesingaba sifishane noma emva kwesikhatsi atawubuyela lapho acala khona”.
Sikhundla semasontfo, sekangeta kuloko, singatsatfwa takhiwo tetindlu letihlangene letigcwele tinhlobonhlobo tebantfu labangeke basite tindzawo letivikelwe kuleyo mimango.
“Linyenti lebantfu labatsenga tindlu letihlangene kuletakhiwo litoba bantfu labamhlophe,” washo kanjalo, “ngako kutophangisa lilanga lamasontfo atovalwa siphetfo ngoba akunokwenteka kutsi linyenti lalabantfu labatawungena kuletindlu letihlangene babe ngemalunga alamasontfo.”
Emasontfo omabili akhiwa ngemabandla ebantfu lamamhlophe ngaphambi kwakutsi i-Harlem ibe lidolobha lelikhulu lalabamnyama - i-Metropolitan Community ngemnyaka wa-1870, ne-St. Martins iminyaka lelishumi emva kwaloko.
Libandla lekucala lalabamhlophe lemaWeseli laphuma kuleyondzawo ngeminyaka yabo-1930.
Libandla lalabamnyama lebelinelisotfo edvute kwalapho ngilo lelatsatsa lesakhiwo.
I-St. Martin’s yatsatfwa libandla lalabamnyama ngaphasi kwa-Rev. John Howard Johnson, lowahola umkhankaso wekudvuba kwebatsengisi ku-125th Street, sitaladi lesikhulu sekutsengiselana e-Harlem, lowamelana nekucashwa noma kutfutfukiswa kwalabamnyama.
Umlilo lowabhedvuka nga-1939 washiya lesakhiwo sonakele kakhulu, kodvwa kwatsi lapho emalunga epherishi ya-Father Johnson enta tinhlelo tekuphindze avuse lelisontfo, asungula umsebenti we-khariloni.

Tinhlelo te-Sainsbury’s tingenela imakethe yemikhicito yebuhle e-UK
I-Sainsbury’s itsatsa etulu i-Boots, ne-Superdrug kanye ne-Debenhams ngemizila yemikhicito yebuhle legcwele basiti lababochwepheshe.
Njengencenye yemfutfo lonemandla wekungenela lemakethe yemikhicito yebuhle yase-UK lengu-£2.8bn, lechubeka njalo ngekundlondlobala ngesikhatsi lapho kutsengiswa kwetefashini kanye netintfo tasendlini kubuyela emuva, lemizila yemikhicito yebuhle itawulingwa etitolo letingu-11 etindzaweni letehlukene eveni lonkhe tiphindze tiyiswe kuletinye titolo emnyakeni lotako nangabe kunesiciniseko sekutsi iyaphumelela.
Lokuhlanyelwa kwetimali kulemikhicito yebuhle ifika ngesikhatsi lapho emasuphamakethe atfungatsa tindlela tekusebentisa sikhala semashelufa lake atsatselwa tinyatselo temtsetfo ngema-TV, ema-microwave kanye nemphadla yasendlini.
I-Sainsbury’s itsite itawuyiphindza kabili imikhicito yayo yebuhle leyitsengisako kuze kufike emikhicitweni lengu-3,000, lekufaka ekhatsi tinhlobo letifana ne-Revlon, Essie, Tweezerman kanye ne-Dr. I-PawPaw kwekucala.
Tinhlobo letehlukene temphahla yaka-L’Oreal, Maybelline kanye ne-Burt's Bees nato titawutfola sikhala lesengetiwe ngetindzawo letineluphawu letifana naleto letitfolakala etitolo taka-Boots.
Isuphamakethe nayo icalisa kabusha tinhlobo letehlukene tekwekutimonyonga taka-Boutique kuze kutsi linyenti lemikhicito ihambisane nalabadla tibhidvo kuphela - intfo leya ngekukhula kufunwa batsengi labasebasha.
Ngetulu kwaloko, i- Fragrance Shop, letsengisa emakha itobe ilinga tivumelwane etitolo letimbili taka-Sainsbury’s, sekucala sakhona savulwa e-Croydon, eningizimu ne-London evikini leliphelile, kantsi sesibili sivulwa e-Selly Oak, e-Birmingham, esikhatsini lesitako lonyaka.
Kutsenga nge-intanethi kanye netingucuko tekutsenga kudla lokungematsantana lamancane etitolo letincane malanga onkhe kusho kutsi emasuphamakethe kubita kutsi afake umfutfo lomkhulu wekuheha bantfu kutsi baye kuwo.
Mike Coupe, longungcongcoshe lomkhulu waka-Sainsbury’s, utsite letindzawo tekutsengisa titoya ngekukhula kubukeka nekufanana netitolo letitsengisa konkhe ngesikhatsi loluchungechunge lwesuphamakethe lutama kulwa ne-Aldi kanye ne-Lidi labatsengisa ngemali lehlisiwe ngekwengeta tinsita kanye nalokungasiko kudla.
I-Sainsbury's beyifaka tindzawo tekutsengisa taka-Argos emakhulwini etitolo yaphindze yangenisa ema-Habitats lambalwa kusukela yatsenga loluchungechunge lwetitolo eminyakeni lemibili leyedlulile, lokungiko letsi yandlondlobalisa emagrosa latsengisiwe kwaphindze kwenyusa intalo yalokutsengiwe.
Imitamo yalesuphamakethe yangaphambili kwekuvusetela ematiko ayo emikhicito yebuhle kanye nemakhemisi yagcina yehlulekile.
I-Sainsbury's yalinga kuhlanganyela ne-Boots ngasekucaleni kweminyaka yabo-2000, kepha lokuhlangana kwaphela kulandzela kungavumelani ngekutsi batawuhlukaniselana kanjani imali lengene ngesitolo sekhemisi emasuphamakethe ayo.
Lelisu lelisha lefika emva kwekutsi i-Sainsbury's itsengisele i-Celesio, longumnikati weluchungechunge lwe-Lloyds Pharmacy, ibhizinisi yemakhemisi langu-281, ngemali lengu-£125m, eminyakeni lemitsatfu leyedlulile.
Itsite i-Lloyds itawudlala indzima kuloluhlelo, ngekwengeta tinhlobo letehlukene temikhicito yekunakekela sikhumba lesezingeni lelisetulu letifaka ekhatsi i-Roche-Posay kanye ne-Vichy etitolo letine.
Paul Mills-Hicks, longumcondzisi waka-Sainsbury's kutekutsengiselana, watsi: “Sesigucule kubukeka nekuvakala kwemizila yetfu yemikhicito yebuhle kuze kutfutfukiseke indzawo levumako yemakhasimende etfu.
Siphindze sahlanyela timali kubalingani labakhetsekile ekuceceshweni, labatawuba sedvutane kuniketa teluleko.
Letinhlobo letehlukene temikhicito leneluphawu lwetfu tentelwe kuhlangabetana netidzingo tetfu tonkhe nendzawo yetfu lehehako kantsi letindzawo letivumako tisho kutsi sesiyindzawo yekuphela lefanele imikhicito yebuhle nalebukana ngco nendlela lendzala yekutsenga.”

Mr. Joko uphindze ubukene nekucindzeteleka lokubangwa kungevani kwemacembu e-Indonesia, lapho emalunga elinyenti lemaSulumane avumele kusebentisa luhlobo lwenkholo yabo lengahambisani netingucuko.
Bantfu labangetulu kwenkhulungwane babulewe kwaphindze kwatsi emashumi etinkhulungwane basuswa emakhaya abo ngesikhatsi kulwa benkholo ya-Khrestu kanye nema-Sulumane etitaladini, basebentisa bocelemba, butjoki, kanye lanetinye tikhali letilimatako.
Bukela: Daniel Sturridge we-Liverpool ufake ligoli lelijulile lekulinganisa nababukene ne-Chelsea
Daniel Sturridge usindzise i-Liverpool ekulahlekelweni yi-Premier League ku-Chelsea ngeligoli lemzuzu waka-89 ngeMgcibelo e-Stanford Bridge e-London.
Sturridge waniketwa ibhola lephuma ku-Xherdan Shaqirin ngesikhatsi angemayadi langu-30 kusukela kumapali e-Chelsea nelicembu lakhe lilandzela ngemuva nga 1-0.
Wachilitela ibhola ngasencene sakhe ngaphambi kwekuvulela ligoli alicondzise ngasekugcineni kwelipali.
Lomtamo weligoli waphakama waya etulu kwelibhokisi ngesikhatsi liwelela ngasekoneni lelisetulu ngasekudla enethini.
Ekugcineni lelibhola lawela ngetulu kwa-Kepa Arrizabalaga lobekazuba lahlala enethini.
“Kwakungumtamo wekufinyelela esikhaleni, nekutfola ibhola futsi badlali labafana na-Shaq badlala balichubele embili ngalokusemandleni abo njalo, ngako ngatama kutidalela sikhatsi lesidze lesenele,” kusho Sturridge atjela i-LiverpoolFC.com.
Ngabona Kante eta alitsintsa kanye wangacitsi sikhatsi acabanga ngalo wavele walidubula epalini.”
I-Chelsea yahamba embili nga 1-0 ekhatsi nemdlalo emva kwekutfola ligoli ngemzuzu waka-25 livela kusihlabani sase-Belgium lesingu-Eden Hazard.
Umshayi wemagoli welicembu lema-Blues wakhahlela ibhola ngesitsendze wayibuyisela ku-Mateo Kovacic, ngaphambi kwekutsi aligucugucule ngasemkhatsini wenkhundla bese ugijimela ngaseluhlangotsi lwe-Liverpool.
Kovacic washeshe waliniketa-aphindze-ahambe ngasekhatsi nenkhundla.
Wase uvutsela libhola lelihle kakhulu, lelaholela kutsi Hazard alifake ebhokisini.
Hazard wagijima washiya labavimba emuva walicedzela ngasekugcineni kwelipali walifaka enethini ngelunyawo lwangasencene waledlulisa ku-Alisson Becker welicembu le-Liverpool.
I-Liverpool ibhekene ne-Napoli esigabeni seticheme ku-Champions League nga 3 p.m. ngaLesitsatfu e-Stadio San Paolo e-Naples, e-Italy.
I-Chelsea ibukene ne-Videoton ku-UEFA Europa League nga 3 p.m. ngaLesine e-London.
Sibalo salabafile kutsunami yase-Indonesia senyukela ku-832
Sibalo salabafile esigamekweni sekutamatama kwemhlaba kanye netsunami sesenyukele ku-832, kusho i-ejensi yetimo letimbi yelive ekuseni ngeLisontfo.
Kubikwa kutsi bantfu labaningi bebavaleleke ngephasi kwetibi tetakhiwo letawa ngesikhatsi sekutamatama kwemhlaba lokwakunemandla lalinganiselwa ku-7.5 lokwenteka ngaLesihlanu nalokwacala emagagasi ledlula ema-fithi langu-20, kusho Sutopo Purwo Nugroho lokhulumela i-ejensi atjela umhlangano webetindzaba.
Lidolobha lase-Palu, lelinebantfu labangetulu kwa-380,000, lajikijelwa yinkhukhuma leyadalwa kuwa kwetakhiwo.
Emaphoyisa abophe indvodza leneminyaka lengu-32, ngetinsolo letilandzela kubulawa kwemfati lowagwazwa waze wafa
Kucaliswe luphenyo lwelicala lekubulala kulandzela kutsi kutfolakale sidvumbu semfati e-Birkenhead, e-Merseyside ekuseni kwanamuhla.
Lomuntfu loneminyaka lengu-44 budzala watfolakala nga 7.55 ekuseni anemanceba ekugwazwa e-Grayson Mews ku-John Street, kwaboshwa indvodza leneminyaka lengu-32 ngekusolwa kutsi ingumbulali.
Emaphoyisa ancuse bantfu bendzawo lababona noma labeva lokutsite kutsi bativete.
Umseshi longu-Inspector Brian O'Hagan utsite: ‘Loluphenyo lusesetigabeni tekucala kepha ngingacela kunoma ngubani lobekasedvutane ne-John Street e- Birkenhead lowabona nome weva lokutsite lokusolekako kutsi asitsintse.
Ngingaphindze ngicele kunome ngubani, ikakhulu bashayeli bematekisi, lekungahle kukhona lebakutsebula ngembili kwetimoto lokungumlandvo wesehlakalo kutsi basitsintse ngoba kungenteka kutsi babe nelwati lolumcoka eluphenyweni lwetfu.’
Lokhulumela emaphoyisa uvumile kutsi lomfati lowatfolakala wasendzaweni yase-Birkenhead nekutsi utfolakele ngekhatsi kwemuti.
Emini yantsambama namuhla bangani lebakholwa kutsi bayamati umufi bafika endzaweni yesehlakalo kutobuta imibuto yekutsi watfolakala kuphi ekuseni.
Luphenyo lusachubeka njengoba emaphoyisa atsi asachubeka nekwatisa tihlobo talohlaselwe wabulawa.
Umshayeli wetekisi lohlala e-Grayson Mews usandza kutama kubuyela eflethini yakhe kepha watjelwa ngemaphoyisa kutsi kute umuntfu lovumelekile kungena noma kuphuma kulesakhiwo.
Uvele wancunywa umlomo nakeva ngalesehlakalo.
Bahlali sebatjelwa kutsi kusetawuba sikhatsi lesingema-awa ngaphambi kwekuvunyelwa kutsi babuyele ngekhatsi.
Sisebenti semaphoyisa sevakala sitjela lenye indvodza kutsi yonkhe lendzawo seyitsatfwa njengendzawo yesehlakalo.
Lomunye umfati wafika kulendzawo akhala tinyembeti.
Asho aphindzaphindza kutsi ‘maye kuyesabeka”.
Nga 2pm tincola letimbili temaphoyisa betingekhatsi kwendzawo levalelwe kunalenye incola ngaphandle nje kwalendzawo.
Lindlazana lemaphoyise belime ngaphandle kwendzawo levalelwe ibuka lokwentekako kulamaflethi.
Nome ngubani lonelwati lolutsite uyacelwa kutsi atsintse DM @MerPolCC, ashayele 101 noma atsintse ema-Crimestoppers ku-0800 555 111 angatatisi kutsi ungubani, asebentise ilogi 247 yamhlaka 30 kuNyoni.
Sitfombe Sephalamende sa-Cromwell sigucuke saba sehlakalo sesikhumbuto ngemsindvo ‘wekubhala kabusha umlandvo’
Kudzingiswa kwaso ngungaba tibongo temtsetfo kulokubhubhisa lokufana nekwe-Thalibani kwetitfombe letiningi temihambo netenkholo yaseNgilandi lowentiwa balandzeli bakhe labangema-Phurithi labatentisako.
Kepha-ke leSosayethi ya-Cromwell yachaza umbono weMnu. Crick “njengebuphukuphuku” kanye “nemtamo wekubhala kabusha umlandvo.”
John Goldsmith, longusihlalo weSosayethi YaCromwell, watsi: “Kwakumele kwenteke kulesikhatsi semphikiswano ngekususwa kwetitfombe kutsi sitfombe sa-Oliver Cromwell lesingaphandle kweSigodlo sase-Westminister sibe ngulesibukwako.
Kubulawa kwetitfombe nemifanekiso yemphi yasekhaya yemaNgisi akuzange kulawulwe noma kwentiwe ngu-Cromwell.
Mhlawumbe Cromwell longasuye angentiwa umhlatjelo wetento tababemkhulu wakhe Thomas lowaphila eminyakeni lelikhulu leyedlulile.
Umbukiso lomkhulu wa-Sir William Hamo Thorneycroft wekubonisa Cromwell usibonakaliso semcondvo weminyaka yemakhulu langu-19 futsi uyincenye yesitfombe semibhalo yemlandvo lelabaningi bakholwa kutsi kusafanele akhunjulwe.
Mnu. Goldsmith watjela i-Sunday Telegraph kutsi: “Cromwell utsatfwa bantfu labaningi, mhlawumbe ikakhulu eminyakeni yemakhulu langu-19 kunanamuhla, njengemvikeli wephalamende ekucindzekeni kwangaphandle, le ngekwendzaba yakhe kungebukhosi.
Kutsi loko kungumbiko loliciniso leliphelele kuyindzaba yemphikiswano yemlandvo lesachubeka.
Lokwatiwako kutsi umbango wasekhatsi neminyaka yemakhulu langu-17 nguwo locondzise kutfutfukiswa kwesive setfu lokwalandzela, naye Cromwell ungulomunye lomelele lelunye luhlangotsi lalowomkhatsi.
Loko lakwenta kwaphumelela njengeMvikeli weNkhosi kufanelwe kukhunjulwa neku hlonishwa.
Ingulube Ibulala Umlimi WaseShayina
Umlimi uhlaselwe wabulawa yingulube emakethe yaseShayina leseningizimu-nshonalanga, ngekusho kwemibiko yetindzaba kuleyondzawo.
Lendvodza, leyatiwa ngesibongo sayo saka-”Yuan,” itfolakele ifile ilimele umtsambo lomkhulu wengati, igcwele ingati eceleni kwesibaya setingulube emakethe lese-Liupanshui esifundzeni sase-Guizhou, kusho umbiko we-South China Norning Post wangelisontfo.
Umfuyi wetingulube ulungiselela kujova tingulube endzaweni yekufuya tingulube mhlaka-30 kuNkhwekhweti, 2005 eSifundzeni se-Xining yase-Qinghai, eShayina.
Kubikwa kutsi bekahambe nemzala wakhe basuka esifundzeni sase-Yunnan lebakhelene naso ngaLesitsatfu bayotsengisa tingulube letingu-15 emakethe.
Ngekusa lokulandzelako umzala wakhe wamtfola afile, futsi watfola kutsi umnyango wesibaya setingulube lesisedvutane nalapho uvuliwe.
Wabika kutsi ngekhatsi kwalesibaya bekunengulube lenkhulu lendvuna lebeyigcwele ingati emlonyeni wayo.
Lohlola tidvumbu wavuma kutsi lengulube lebenesisindvo lesingu 550 wemaphawundi yamhlasela yamgicita lomlimi waze wafa, ngekusho kwembiko.
“Imilente yemzala wami beyigcwele ingati futsi ilimele,” kusho umzala wakhe lobekatiwa ngesibongo saka “Wu”, emagama akhe ashiwo betindzaba i-Guiyang Evening News.
Emakhamera lakhombisa lokwenteka abonisa Yuan angena emakethe nga-4.40 am ngaLesine ayokondla tingulube takhe.
Sidvumbu sakhe satfolakala emva kweli-awa.
Lesilwane lesabulala lendvodza sasingasiso sa-Yuan noma umzala wakhe.
Umphatsi wemakethe watjela betindzaba te-Evening News kutsi lengulube beyivalelwe kutsi ingahlaseli lomunye umuntfu, ngesikhatsi emaphoyisa acokelela bufakazi kuleyondzawo yesehlakalo.
Umndeni waka-Yuan kanye nalabaphetse imakethe kubikwa kutsi basakhulumisana kutsi kube nesincephetelo salokufa.
Nome kungakavami nje, tigameko tetingulube letihlasela bantfu setike tabikwa ngaphambili.
Ngemnyaka wa-2016, ingulube yahlasela umfati kanye nendvodza yakhe eplazini labo e-Massachusetts, yashiya lendvodza ilimele kabi.
Eminyakeni lelishumi lengaphambili, ingulube lenesisindvo lesingu 650 wemaphawundi yabetsela umlimi wase-Wales esigulumbeni sakhe waze walanyulelwa kutsi umkakhe asicoshe ngekusetfusa lesilwane.
Kulandzela kutsi umlimi wase-Origon adliwe tingulube takhe ngemnyaka wa-2012, lomunye webalimi base-Manitoba watjela i-CBC News kutsi akukavami kutsi tingulube tibe nelulaka, kepha kunambitsa ingati kungaba “sisusa” saloko.”
“Tisuke tidlala nje.
Titsandza kufufutsa, nekuhlola tintfo ... atisuki tiphumele kuyolimata.
Kufanele nje kutsi utinike inhlonipho lefanele,” ngekusho kwakhe.
Imisalela ye-Hurricane Rosa iletsa timvula letimatima letisabalele e-US leseningizimu-nshonalanga
Njengoba kuhloliwe, i-Hurricane Rosa iya ngekuphelelwa ngemandla isahamba emantini lapholile elugwini lolusenyakatfo ne-Mexico.
Noko, Rosa utawuletsa timvula letinetikhukhula kuyo yonkhe inyakatfo ye-Mexico kanye naseningizimu lesenshonalanga ne-U.S. kulamalanga letako.
Rosa waba nemimoya lenemandla lenelitubane lelingu-85 mph, lokuSivinguvungu Sesigaba 1, kusukela nga 5 a.m. NgeLisontfo ngesikhatsi sasemphumalanga, futsi wabonakala emamayela langu-385 eningizimu lesenshonalanga ne- Punta Eugenia, e-Mexico.
Kubhekeke kutsi Rosa abheke ngasenyakatfo ngeLisontfo.
Kusenjalo, umhosha wemoya sewucale kwakheka elwandlekati i-Pacific Ocean futsi uhamba ubheke emphumalanga yelugu i-West Coast yase-U.S. Ngesikhatsi Rosa asasondzela epheninsula ye-Baja e-California ngeMsombuluko njengelitulu lelinemandla, utocala afuce umoya lonemswakama awubhekise enyakatfo uyongena eningizimu lesenshonalanga ne-U.S.
Rosa utawuletsa imvula lengafika kuma-intji langu-10 kuletinye tincenye tase-Mexico ngeMsombuluko.
Bese-ke, umoya lonemswakama wangasenkhabeni yelive lohlangana nalomhosha lotako utawudala timvula letinemandla letisabalele eNingizimu-nshonalanga kulamalanga letako.
Kuleyo ndzawo, timvula letingema-intji langu 1 kuya ku-4 titawubanga tikhukhula letinemandla tesikhashana, nekudzilika kwemhlaba lokungahle kube khona ehlane.
Umoya lomatima longasenkhabeni yelive utawubanga lizinga letimvula lelingasuka ngu-2 kuya ku-3 wema-intji ngeli-awa etindzaweni letikhetsiwe, ikakhulu etindzaweni letiseningizimu ne-Nevada kanye ne-Arizona.
Timvula letingafika ku-2 kuya ku-3 wema-intji tibhekekile etindzaweni letiseNingizimu-nshonalanga, ikakhulu etindzaweni letiningi tase-Arizona.
Kungahle kube khona tikhukhula letinemandla tesikhashana letitawugucula simo masinyane nje ngenca yesimo sekusakateka kwemvula letingasenkhabeni yelive.
Akusiwo umcondvo lomuhle kudzabula ehlane ngetinyawo ngalesikhatsi lesibi setimvula letingasenkhabeni yelive.
Timvula letimatima tingabanga kutsi emawa abe yimifula lenemandla kantsi nekudvuma kwelitulu kungaletsa imimoya lenemandla nekubhunya kwetintfuli.
Lomhosha wemoya lotako uyawuletsa imvula lenemandla kuleto tindzawo letiyincenye yelugu lwa-California LeseNingizimu.
Timvula letingaba ngetulu kwesigamu se-intji tingefika, lokungabanga tikhukhula letingatseni nekushelela kwemigwaco.
Loku kutawuba kucala kwesikhatsi semvula kuleyo ndzawo.
Kutawuba khona imvula lena tikhawu letawucala kufika e-Arizona ngekuhamba kwesikhatsi ngeLisontfo nasekuseni ngeMsombuluko, ngaphambi kwekutsi imvula yenabele etindzaweni letiningi ngeMsombuluko nangaLesibili.
Imvula lenemandla itosabalala ne-Four Corners ngaLesibili ichubeke kuze kube nguLesitsatfu.
Inyanga yeMphala ingahle ibe nemazinga ekushisa lagucuka kakhulu kulo lonkhe lase-U.S. ngesikhatsi i-Arctic iya ngekuphola, kepha tindzawo letingasenkhabeni yelive titawuhlala tifutfumele.
Kulesinye sikhatsi loku kuholela ekugucukeni lokubabatekako kwemazinga ekushisa etindzaweni letihlalelene.
Kunesibonelo lesikhulu sekugucuka lokugcamile kwemazinga ekushisa lokwehlukene enkhabeni ye-U.S. ngeLisontfo.
Kunemehluko lolinganiselwa ku-20 digrisi welizinga lekushisa emkhatsini we-Kansas City, ne-Missouri, kanye ne-Omaha, e-Nebraska, kanye nasemkhatsini we St. Louis ne-Des Moines, e-Iowa.
Kulamalanga lambalwa letako, sivuvu sasehlobo sitawutama kuphindze sikhule futsi sandze.
Tindzawo letiningi letisenkhabeni nasemphumalanga ne-U.S. kubhekeke kutsi ticale ngekufutfumala lokunemazinga langaba kuma-80s kwenyanga yeMphala kusukela Ematsafeni LaseNingizimu nakuletinye tincenye teNyakatfo-mphumalanga.
Lizinga lekushisa e-New York lingafika ku-80 digrisi ngaLesibili, lokungacishe kube ngema-digrisi langu-10 ngetulu kwalojwayelekile.
Tinhlola tesikhatsi lesidze tibonisa ematfuba emazinga ekushisa lasetulu kunalajwayelekile etindzaweni letisemphumalanga ne-U.S. encenyeni yekucala yenyanga ye-Mphala.
Bantfu labatigidzi letingetulu kwa-20 babukela kutekwa kwelicala la-Brett Kavanaugh
Bantfu labangetulu kwetigidzi letingu-20 babukela bufakazi lobushubile bangaLesine balokhetfwe Yinkantolo Lenkhulu, Brett Kavanaugh, kanye na-Christine Blasey Ford, umfati lowambeka licala lekumhlukubeta ngekwasecasini, lekuvakala kutsi kwenteka ngeminyaka yabo-1980, emisakatweni yamabonakudze lesitfupha.
Kusenjalo, kujamelana ngakutepolitiki kwachubeka, ngesikhatsi basakati baphatamisa kusakata lokujwayelekile kwetingucuko tamuva tangaLesihlanu: lekusivumelwane lesasichutjwa ngu-Sen Jeff Flake wase-Arizona kutsi i-FBI yente luphenyo lwemacala lweliviki.
Ford watjela Likomidi Letemtsetfo Wesinethi kutsi ucinisekise ngalokuphelele kutsi Kavanaugh wamdvonsa ngesihluku adzakiwe futsi watama kumkhumula timphahla takhe ephathini yesikolwa lesiphakeme.
Ngesikhatsi aniketa bufakazi lobunzulu, Kavanaugh watsi ucinisekise ngalokuphelele nga-100 phesenti kutsi loko akuzange kwenteke.
Kungenteka kutsi bantfu labangetulu kwetigidzi letingu-20.4 lababikwa ngu-Nielsen ngaLesihlanu balibukela lelicala.
Lenkampani beyibala tibukeli letijwayelekile ku-CBS, ABC, CNN, neShaneli ye-Fox News kanye ne-MSNBC.
Tibalo talamanye emashaneli lebekabonisa lelicala atizange tisheshe titfolakale, lekufaka ekhatsi i-PBS, C-SPAN kanye ne-Fox Business Network.
Futsi-ke Nielsen uvamise kuba nebulukhuni bekukala sibalo sebantfu lababukela emahhofisini.
Uma sikubuka ngalenye indlela, lobungako bebabukeli kufananiswa nebemdlalo webhola wekwehlulekisana noma i-Academy Awards.
I-Fox News Channel, lenalabanemcondvo losekela kakhulu kubekwa Kavanaugh esikhundleni, yaholela ekutsini emashaneli abe netibukeli letilinganiselwa etigidzini letingu-5.69 tebabukeli kulelicala lelatsatsa lilanga lonkhe, sekusho Nielsen.
I-ABC yalandzela ngebabukeli labatigidzi letingu-3.26.
I-CBS yaba netigidzi letingu-3.1, i-NBC yona yaba netigidzi letingu-2.94, ne-MSNBC tigidzi letingu-2.89 kantsi i-CNN yona yaba netigidzi letingu-2.52, kusho Nielsen.
Umdlandla wachubeka kuhlala uphakeme emva kwalelicala.
Flake waba seshashalazini kulesigameko sangaLesihlanu.
Emva kwekutsi lihhofisi lema-Republican likhiphe sitatimende sekutsi litoncoma kukhetsa Kavanaugh, wabanjwa kuma-khamera e-CNN kanye ne-CBS ngaLesihlanu atsetsiswa bashuci ngesikhatsi atama kugibela likheshi limyisa ecaleni leLikomidi Lemtsetfo.
Wema abhekise emehlo akhe phasi imizuzu lembalwa ngesikhatsi avinjelwa, aboniswa bukhoma emsakatweni we-CNN.
“Ngime la embikwakho,” kusho lomunye umfati.
“Ngabe ucabanga kutsi bekakhuluma liciniso yini esiveni?
Watjelwa kutsi, “unemandla ngesikhatsi bafati labaningi bangenamandla.””
Flake watsi lihhofisi lakhe likhiphe sitatimende waphindze watsi, sekusele kancane kuvaleke likheshi, utawuphindze abe nalokunye langakusho ecaleni embikwelikomidi.
Emashaneli lasakata ngetintsambo nangemoya onkhe bekabonisa bukhoma kuma-awa ngekuhamba kwesikhatsi, ngesikhatsi Likomidi Lemtsetfo kumele livotele kuchubela embili kukhetfwa kwa-Kavanaugh abe lilunga le-Sinethi leliphelele.
Kepha Flake watsi loko angakwenta ngesivumelwane sekutsi i-FBI ingabuketa emacala latfweswe lokhetselwe liviki lelitako, lebekugcugcutelwa lindlanzana lema-Democrats.
Flake wagculiseka ngenhlanye ngetinkhulumo nemngani wakhe, Sen. Chris Coons, wema-Democrat.
Emva kwekukhulumisana na-Coons nalamanye emalunga esinethi emva kwaloko, Flake wenta sincumo.
Kukhetsa kwa-Flake kwaba nemandla, ngoba kwakunebufakazi kutsi ema-Republicans angeke abe nemavoti ekuphasisa kukhetfwa kwa-Kavanaugh ngaphandle kweluphenyo.
Mengameli Trump sewuvule luphenyo lwe-FBI ngemacala latfweswe Kavanaugh.
Ndvunankhulu wase-Brithani PM May usola baceki ngeku-’dlala ipolitiki’ ngendzaba ye-Brexit
Ndvunankhulu Theresa May wasola labagceka luhlelo lwakhe lwekuphuma enhlanganweni i-European Union ngekutsi “badlala ipolitiki” ngelikusasa lelive lase-Brithani nekutsi bentela phasi lokufunwa sive ngesikhatsi acocisana nebeliphephandzaba i-Sunday Times.

Kudutjulwa kwa-Wayde Sims Emaphoyisa abopha umsolwa Dyteon Simpson ekufeni kwemdlali e-LSU
Emaphoyisa abophe umsolwa ekudutjulwaneni lokwaphuma nemphefumulo wa-Wayde Sims, umdlali we-basketball e-LSU loneminyaka lengu-20 budzala.
Dyteon Simpson, naye loneminyaka lengu-20, uboshiwe wafakwa ejele ngelicala lekubulala kwesigaba sesibili, ngekusho kwe-Baton Rouge Police Department.
Bemtfetfo bakhiphe i-vidiyo yekubukana emehlweni kwa-Sims kanye na-Simpson, kantsi emaphoyisa atsi Sims walahlekelwa tibuko takhe kuleyomphi.
Letibuko tatfolwa ngemaphoyisa endzaweni yaleso sehlakalo kwatsi natihlolwa tatfolakala tine-DNA ya-Simpson, kusho umbiko we-WAFB lencike ku-CBS.
Emva kwekutsi emaphoyisa abute Simpson imibuto, emaphoyisa atsi wavuma kutsi wamdubula wambulala Waude.

Bososayensi labahlatiya simo semhlaba sebabone kukhula kwalokunyakata kwalesikhafula-mlilo lesisime endzaweni lengemamayela langu-45 (72 wemakhilometre) ngaseningizimu-mphumalanga yenhlokodolobha kusukela ngesikhatsi kutamatama kwemhlaba lokunesikali lesingu-7.1 kwanyakatisa inkhaba ye-Mexico ngenyanga yeNyoni nga-2017.

Bantfu labasitfupha baboshiwe e-Barcelona ngeMgcibelo kulandzela kutsi babhikishi labasekela inkhululeko babambana etulu nemaphoyisa etiphitsiphitsi, nangesikhatsi tinkhulungwane tebantfu tingenela imishuco lababangisana nayo njengesikhumbuto selivoti lase-Catalonia lekumisa kwehlukaniswa kwemacembu.
Sicuku salabasekela kwehlukana lesasitivale buso nalesancandvwa ngemaphoyise etiphitsiphitsi sabajikijela ngemacandza nangapende loyimphuphu, lokwadala emafu lamnyama elutfuli etitaladini lebetivame kuba netivakashi letinyenti.

Bavoti labanyenti kakhulu bakhetsa kutfola inkhululeko noma nje sibalo salabavota sasiphasi ngenca yekutsi labo labaphambene nekuyekelela bavele badvuba kuyovota.
Ngekusho kwetiphatsimandla te-Catalonia bantfu labacishe babe yinkhulungwane balimala emnyakeni lophelile kulandzela kutsi emaphoyisa atame kumisa kutsi kuvota kuchubeke etindzaweni tekuvota kuso sonkhe sifundza kuloko kubambana ngetihlutfu lokwakukhona.
Emacembu lasekela inkhululeko abekanekise enkanjini busuku bonkhe bangaLesihlanu kuvimbela umshuco wekusekela umbutfo webaphoyisa elive.
Lowo mshuco wachubeka kepha kwabita kutsi basebentise lenye indlela.
Narcis Termes, loneminyaka lengu-68, nalongusomagezi lowangenela umbhikisho walabasekela kwehlukaniswa akanye nemkakhe, watsi sewuphelelwe litsemba lekutsi i-Catalonia ingaba nematfuba ekutfola inkhululeko.
“Umnyaka lophelile ube ngumnyaka wetikhatsi tekuphila kahle kakhulu.
Ngabona batali bami bakhala tinyembeti tenjabulo ngoba bakhone kuvota kepha-ke nyalo sekume konkhe,” asho sekangeta.
Nakube baphumelela bancoba ngekuphuma ngeseligundvwane elukhetfweni lwesifundza ngenyanga ya-Ngongoni lephalile, emacembu ase-Catalonia lasekela inkhululeko abe nebulukhuni bekuchubeka nemfutfo wawo lonyaka ekubeni labanye bebaholi bawo labahamba embili batidzingisa bona noma bativalela ngesikhatsi balindzele kutsetfwa kwelicala lendzima lebayidlala ekuhleleni i-referendamu lokwalandzelwa kumenyetelwa kwenkhululeko.
Joan Puig, longumakhenikha loneminyaka lengu-42 budzala lobekatsatsa titfombe talombhikisho ngelucingo lwakhe ngenhloso yekusekela emaphoyisa, utsite lokucabana bekubhebheteliswa betembangave kumacembu omabili.
“Simo sesiya ngekushuba kakhulu,” kusho yena.
Kutsite ngeMgcibelo, Oriol Junqueras, longulomunye webaholi bema-Catalan lebebagciniwe ngaphambi kwekutekiswa licala kusukela kulomnyaka lophelile, wamemetela kutsi utongenela lukhetfo lwePhalamende yase-Europe kulomnyako lotako.
“Kungenela lolukhetfo lwase-Europe kuyindlela lekahle kakhulu yekujivata kuyekelelwa kwemagugu embuso wentsandvo yeliningi kanye nekucindzetelwa lesikubonile kuhulumende wase-Spain,” washo njalo.

Menga ukhahlela libhola lelaniketa i-Livingston kuncoba ema-Rangers nga 1-0
Ligoli lekucala Dolly Menga lalishayela i-Livingston labanika kuncoba umdlalo
I-Livingston leyaphakanyiswa yamangalisa licembu i-Rangers ngekuvalela Steven Gerrard ekwehlulweni kwakhe kwesibili emidlalweni lengu-18 njengamenenja we-klabhu i-Ibrox.
Libhola lelakhahlelwa ngu-Dolly Menga latibonakalisa livula umkhatsi ngesikhatsi licembu la-Gary Holt lilingana na-Hibernian endzaweni yesibili.
Licembu la-Gerrard lisele lingenakuncoba ekuhambeni kule-Premiership kulesikhatsi sanyalo semidlalo kantsi libukene ne-Hearts leholako nalabayilandzela ngemaphuzu lasiphohlongo, ngeLisontfo lelitako.
Kuze kube nguleso sikhatsi, i-Rangers itokwemukela i-Rapid Vienna ku-Europa League ngaLesine.
Ngalesikhatsi, i-Livingston ichubeka nekungehlulwa kwayo kulesigaba emidlalweni lesitfupha, na-Holt loyinhloko yebaceceshi usamelwe kutsi eve kwehlulwa seloku atsatsa sikhundla sa-Kenny Miler kulenyanga lephelile.
I-Livingston iphutselwa ngematfuba ekudlala netivakashi
Licembu la-Holt besekukudzala kufanele lihambe embili ngaphambi kwekushaya ligoli, kucondzisa kwalo kubangele i-Rangers tinkinga.
Scott Robinson waphunyula kepha wacekela phasi umfutfo wakhe ngaphambi kwekushaya ligoli, kwatsi Alan Lithgow wase ukhona kucondzisa umfutfo wakhe kabanti kulandzela kutsi antjuze ahlangabeta libhola lenhloko la-Craig Halhett embikwemapali.
Labemukela tivakashi banetiseka kutsi bayekele i-Rangers idlale embikwabo, ngekwati kutsi bangahle bahluphe letivakashi ngetikhatsi letitsite.
Langena kanjalo-ke leligoli lelimcoka lekuncoba.
I-Rangers yavumela ligoli lelingavinjwa kwatsi i-Livingston yasebenta kuvula umkhatsi, bo-Declan Gallagher ana-Robinson bahlangana kulungisela Menga, lowavele walitsintsa wase ushaya ligoli asekhatsi nelibhokisi.
Kulesosigaba, i-Rangers beyisolo iyiphetse ibhola kepha yatfola kutsi badlali basekhaya labavimba emuva abangeneki kantsi na-Liam Kelly lovimba emagoli wakhatsateka kakhulu.
Kwachubeka kanjalo nasesigamini sesibili semdlalo, noma nje Alfredo Morelos aphocelela kuvinjwa kweligoli lelashaywa ngu-Kelly.
Scott Pittman wavinjelwa tinyawo ta-Allan McGregor lovimbela i-Rangers emagoli, kwatsi Lithgow waphazamisa lelinye lisu lemdlalo we-Livingston.
Kwaba nekuphambana kwebhola lokuningi ebhokisini le-Livingston lekamane akhweshiswa nje, kantsi emaphenalthi lamabili lebekafunwa - kulandzela insayeya ya-Halkett yekuntjintja Glenn Middleton, kanye nalenye yekubamba ibhola ngesandla - adluliswa nje.
‘Kuyamangalisa kakhulu’ ngaku-Livingston - kusho labahlatiyako.
Alasdair Lamont we-BBC Scotland Enkhundleni ye-Tonny Macaroni
Umdlalo lowamangalisa kakhulu lowaba nemphumela lomuhle ku-Livingston.
Kumuntfu nje, bebatihlabani, letatichubeka njalo kwenta lokukhulu kunalokubhekekile kulendlela leya embili.
Indlela yabo yekudlala kanye nekutiphatsa kwabo akukagucuki seloku babuyela ekundizeni kwabo, kepha-ke tibongo kumele tedluliselwe ku-Holt ngendlela lekalibumbe ngakhona lelicembu kusukela ekufikeni kwakhe.
Bekanetihlabani letiningi.
Kapteni welicembu, Halkett, bekatimisele, atilungiselela kuvimba lokusezingeni lelisetulu, kantsi Menga abeloku angabaniki bo-Connor Goldson na-Joe Worrall litfuba lekuphumula.
I-Rangers yona, noko, beyinesikhebesi selugcozi.
Njengoba bebakahle kakhulu ngaphasi kwesandla sa-Gerrard, bebasilela kancane kuleyo migangatfo.
Libhola labo lekugcina belintengantenga - bakhona kuvulela kudlalela ngasekhaya kanye nje - kantsi-ke loku kwayivula emehlo i-Rangers, leyatikhandza isekhatsi neluhlu lwemaphuzu.

Hurricane Rosa Usongela I-Phoenix, ne-Las Vegas, Salt Lake City Ngetikhukhula Letinemandla (Tindzawo Letinesomiso Tingahle Tisitakale)
Akukavami kutsi umoya lowehlelako longasenkhabeni yemhlaba uhlasele i-Arizona, kepha-ke loku kungahle kwenteke makusuka liviki lelitako njengoba umfutfo losele wa-Hurricane Rosa udzabula i-Desert Southwest, aletsa bungoti betikhukhula letinemandla.
I-National Weather Service seyikhiphe secwayiso lesibhekiswe enshonalanga ne-Arizona kuya ngaseningizimu nemphumalanga Nevada, neningizimu-mphumalanga ne-California kanye ne-Utah, lekufaka ekhatsi emadolobha i-Phoenix, Flagstuff, Las Vegas, kanye ne-Salt Lake City, sekugadza tikhukhula letinemandla ngeMsombuluko nangaLesibili.
Kubhekeke kutsi Rosa atsatse indlela lecondzile ledlula e-Phoenix ngaLesibili, afike nemvula ngeMsombuluko.
I-National Weather Service yase-Phoenix iphawule nge-thwithi kutsi “tiphepho tangasenkhabeni yemhlaba letilishumi tibelesele ngesivunguvungu sangasenkhabeni yemhlaba noma simo sekwehla kwemoya libanga lelingengci emamayela langu-200 ngaphandle kwe-Phoenix kusukela nga-1950!
Katrina (ngemnyaka wa-1967) naye bekasiphepho lebesingemamayela langengci ku-40 nemncele we-AZ.”
Emamodeli e-National Hurricane Center akamuva ahlongota imvula lengema-intji langu-2 kuya ku-4, kuphindze kube nema-intji lafika ku-6 e-Mogollon Rim yase-Arizona.
Letinye tindzawo te-Desert Southwest letifaka ekhatsi inkhaba ye-Rockies kanye ne-Great Basin tingahle titfole ema-intji 1 kuya ku-2, naletinye tindzawo lapho imvula ingafika ku-4 wema-intji.
Kuleto tindzawo letingekho engotini yetikhukhula letinemandla, imvula leta na-Rosa ingahle ibe sibusiso njengoba lesifundza sihlaselwe somiso.
Noma tikhukhula tiletsa kukhatsateka kakhulu, lenye yalemvula ingahle isite njengoba Iningizimu-nshonalanga ibukene nesimo sesomiso kwanyalo.
Ngekusho kwe-U.S. Drought Monitor, incenye ye-Arizona lengetudlwana kancane kwa-40 wemaphesenti ibukene nesomiso lesikhulu, lekusigaba sesibili, ngekwembiko we-weather.com
Kwekucala, indlela ya-Hurricane Rosa iholela ekudzilikeni kwemhlaba etindzaweni letehlukene tepheninsula ye-Baja California e-Mexico.
Rosa, lobelesele ngemandla etikhukhula ngeLisontfo ekuseni nemimoya lehhusha litubane lelingemamayela langu-85 ngeli-awa, ingemamayela langu-385 ngaseningizimu ne-Punta Eugenia, e-Mexico ibheke enyakatfo ahamba emamayela langu-12 ngeli-awa.
Lesiphepho sihlangabetana nemanti lapholile elwandlekati i-Pacific bese siphela emandla.
Ngako kubhekeke kutsi sifike ngemandla etiphepho tangasenkhabeni yemhlaba e-Mexico emini yantsambama noma ngeMsombuluko.
Imvula lesabalele netincenye te-Mexico ingahle ibe nemandla, lokungabanga ingoti lenkhulu yetikhukhula.
“Imvula lefika ku-3 kuya ku-6 wema-intji ibhekeke kusukela e-Baja California kuya enyakatfo-nshonalanga ne-Sonora, lengahle ifike ku-10 wema-intji,” kubika i-weather.com
Rosa utawubese ubheka enyakatfo adzabule e-Mexico njengesiphepho sangasenkhabeni yemhlaba ngaphambi kwekufika emnceleni we-Arizona etikhatsini tasekuseni kakhulu ngaLesibili njengemoya lowehlako, lotawubese uhamba ukhuphuke udzabule e-Arizona wedlulele eningizimu ye-Utah ebusuku bangaLesibili.
“Ingoti lenkhulu lebhekeke ku-Rosa noma tinsalela takhe yimvula lematima kakhulu e-Baja California, nasenyakatfo-nshonalanga, kanye ne-U.S. Desert Southhwest,” kusho i-National Hurricane Center.
Letimvula tibhekeke kuletsa tikhukhula letinemandla letisongela imphilo netibi ehlane, kanye nekudzilika kwemhlaba etindzaweni letinetintsaba.

“Angigijimi nje, kepha ngigijima kakhulu,” washo njalo.

I-U.S. kufanele iphindze kabili timali te-A.I.
Njengoba kuphisheka kwe-China ngekuhlakanipha kwabongcondvomshina (AI) kwandza, i-U.S. kufanele iphindze kabili linani lemali leyicitsa kutelucwaningo kuloluhlangotsi, kusho Kai-Fu Lee longumhlanyeli wetimali nalosebenta tekuhlakanipha kwabongcondvomshina, loke wasebentela i-Google, ne-Microsoftt kanye ne-Apple.
Lamagama afika kulandzela kutsi tincenye letehlukene tahulumende we-U.S. tikhiphe timemetelo nge-AI, noma nje i-U.S. ingenalo lisu lelisemtsetfweni le-AI.
Kusenjalo, i-China icalise luhlelo lwayo kulomnyaka lophelile: ihlose nguhamba embili ngekuba ku-No.1 ekwenteni tingucuko letinsha ku-AI kungakapheli umnyaka wa-2030.
“Kuphindza kabili liphakelo lelucwaningo nge-AI kungaba sicalo lesikahle, kwatise kutsi lamanye emave asemuva kakhulu kune-U.S., futsi sibuke embili kulomunye umhlahlandlela ku-AI.
Kuphindza kabili timali letikhishwako kungahle kuphindze kabili nematfuba ekutsi imphumelelo lenkhulu ku-AI lelandzelako itawuba se-U.S., kusho Lee atjela i-CNBC engcocweni lebekhona kuleliviki.
Lee, lobhale incwadi yakhe letsi “AI Superpowers”: I-China, Silicon Valley and New World Order” leshicilelwe kulenyanga ngu-Houghton Miffin Harcourt, losikhulu lesiphetse (CEO) se-Sinovation Ventures, lekungiyo lehlanyele timali kulenye yetinkampani te-AI letisembili kakhulu e-China, Face++.
Ngeminyaka yabo-1980, ase-Carnegie Mellon, wasebenta eluhlelweni lwe-AI lolwehlula umdlali lobekwa embili kakhulu kunabo bonkhe we-American Othello, kantsi emva kwesikhatsi waba sikhulu se-Microsoft Research futsi angumengameli weligatja le-Google e-China.
Lee wakuvuma kucudzelana kwahulumende we-U.S. kutebuchwepheshe njengensayeya i- Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency's Robotics Challenge futsi wabuta kutsi lolandzelako utawuba nini, kuze akhone kucoka basunguli bemibono labatolandzela.
Bacwaningi base-U.S. kuvamise kutsi kufanele kutsi basebente matima kuze batfole kuphiwa timali nguhulumende, kusho Lee.
“Akusiyo i-China lesemuka baholi bemfundvo; tinkampani letinkhulu,” kusho Lee.
I-Facebook, ne-Google naletinye tinkampani tebuchwepheshe leticashe labakhanyiselwe kakhulu labavela emayunivesithi kutosebenta ku-AI kuleminyaka ledlulile.
Lee utsite tingucuko kutemigomo yekungeniswa kwebantfu eveni nato tingayisita i-U.S. kutfutfukisa imitamo yayo ku-AI.
“Ngicabanga kutsi emakhadi emvume yekuhlala kulelive kufanele aniketwe labaneticu te-PhD ku-AI,” kusho yena.
Libandla i-State Council yase-China ikhiphe luhlelo lwayo lolubitwa i-Next Generation Artificial Intelligence Development Plan ngenyanga yaKholwane 2017.
Inhlangano lebitwa nge-National Natural Science Foundation yase-China iniketa timali kubantfu labasetikhungwini temfundvo ngendlela lefana naleyo ye-National Science Foundation naletinye tinhlangano tahulumende letipha bacwaningi base-U.S. timali, kepha-ke lizinga lemsebenti wemfundvo liphasi e-China, kusho Lee.
Ngasekucaleni kwalomnyaka, i-U.S. Defense Department yacamba sikhungo lesitsiwa yi-Joint Artficial Intelligence Center, lekucondvwe kutsi isebentise kubambisana kwemikhakha kanye netifundziswa, futsi sakhiwo semahhofisi amengameli, i-White House, imemetele kubunjwa kwe-Select Committee on Artificial Intelligence.
Futsi kuyona lenyanga DARPA umemetele kuhlanyelwa kwemali lengu-$2 bhiliyoni emsebentini lomusha lobitwa nge-AI Next
Kantsi-ke i-NSF yona, kwanyalo ihlanyela imali lengetulu kwetigidzi leti-$100 ngemnyaka umunye kutekucwaninga nge-AI.
Kusenjalo, tinhlelo temtsetfo we-U.S. letafuna kucamba ikhomishani letsiwa yi-National Security Commission on Artificial intelligence atikaboni kunyakata kwekusebenta etinyangeni letedlulile.

Licembu lasekhaya labuya, noko, kwatsi ngesikhatsi Struan Hutchinson anikwa iyelokhadi ngekusukela Climo angenabhola, alisusa emgceni wephenalthi, Macpherson watsintsa phasi ngasemuva kwesihenco se-Ayr lebeyita ngemandla.

‘Lwandle ngelwetfu’: I-Bolivia lekakwe ngulamanye emave yetsemba kutsi inkantolo itophindze ivule indlela leya e-Pacific
Bagwedli bemkhumbi bagadza indlunkhulu yemikhumbi yemphi e-La Paz.
Takhiwo tesive tindizisa umjeka leluhlata njengelwandle.
Tikhungo temikhumbi yemphi kusukela e-Lake Titicaca kuya e-Amazon tigcwele ticubulo letitsi: “Lwandle ngelwetfu ngekwemtsetfo.”
Kuphindze silutfole kungumsebenti.”
Kuyo yonkhe i-Bolivia lekulive lelikakwe ngulamanye emave, sikhumbuto setindzawo letingaselwandle letatsatfwa yi-Chile embangweni wemnotfo ngeminya yesenshuri yaka-19 leyedlula lapho kwacitseka khona ingati, sisakhanya kahle engcondvweni - njengesifiso sekuphindze bahambe eLwandlekati lwe-Pacific.
Lawo matsemba ephakeme kakhulu emva kwemashumi eminyaka, esikhatsini lapho i-Bolivia imele sijubo senkantolo yemhlaba yebulungiswa (ICJ) mhla ka-1 kuMphala sekuphele iminyaka lesihlanu kusetjentwa lendzaba.
“I-Bolivia isenawo umfutfo, umoya wekubumbana nekuthula, futsi ibheke umphumela lebabuke kutsi utohamba kahle,” kusho Roberto Calzadilla, sikhulu lesimele live lase-Bolivia.
Takhamuti tase-Bolivia titobe tibuka lesijubo se-ICJ kubomabonakudze kulo lonkhe live, ngelitsemba lekutsi lenkantolo i-The Hague itawuvumelana nekusho kwe-Bolivia kutsi - emva kwemashumi eminyaka etinkhulumo - i-Chile iphocelelekile kukhulumisana kufika esivumelwaneni sekuniketa i-Bolivia sikhala sayo sekufinyelela elwandle.
Evo Morales, longumengameli wemdzabu lokhuluma kahle wase-Bolivia - nalobukene nemphi yemphikiswano yekuphindze akhetfwe emnyakeni lotako - naye usibuke ngalabovu lesijubo sangeMsombuluko.
“Sesisondzele kakhulu ekubuyeleni eLwandlekati Lwe-Pacific,” asho afunga ngasekupheleni kweNgci.
Kepha labanye bahlatiyi bakholwa kutsi inkantolo ingahle ingakhiphi sijubo lesisekela i-Bolivia - nekutsi kuncane lokungagucuka uma ingenta njalo.
Lelibandla le-UN lelise-Netherlands alinawo emandla ekujuba imikhawulo yelive lase-Chile, futsi ishito kutsi ayinowukhipha umphumela wetinkhulumo letingahle tibanjwe.
Lokutsi lesijubo se-ICJ sifike sekuphele tinyanga letisitfupha nje kuphela kuphetfwe tinkhulumo kukhombisa kutsi lendzaba “beyingasiyo lematima,” sekusho Paz Zarate, loyingcweti yemtsetfo wemave.
Esikhundleni sekutsi ichubekise tinjongo tase-Bolivia, leminyaka lemine leyedlulile iyibuyisele emuva.
“Ludzaba lwekufinyelela elwandle selutseftwe ngendlovu yangena ngumbuso we-Bolivia lokhona,” kusho Zarate.
Tinkhulumo ta-Morales letinemphi ekhatsi seticedze konkhe kumtsakaselela kwetakhamiti tase-Chile, abeka umbono wakhe.
Kutobakhona sikhatsi lapho i-Bolivia ne-Chile batawuchubeka bakhulumisane, kepha kutawuba matima kakhulu kutsi babambe tinkhulumo emva kwaloku.
Lamave lamabili akashintjanisi emancusa kusukela nga-1962.
Lowake waba ngumengameli, Eduardo Rodríguez, lomelele i-Bolivia e-The Hague, uwuphikile umcondvo wekutsi lesijubo senkantolo sisheshise ngendlela lengakavami.
Lilanga langeMsombuluko litawuletsela i-Bolivia “litfuba lelingakavami lekuvula sikhatsi lesisha sebudlelwane ne-Chile” kanye nelitfuba “lekucedza sikhatsi lesesiminyaka lengu-139 yekungavumelani ngaloko lebangakuzuza bobabili,” kusho yena.
Calzadilla naye waphika kutsi Morales - losengulomunye wabomengameli base-Latin America labadvume kakhulu - bekasebentisa lendzaba yemanti elwandle njengeludvondvolo kutepolitiki.
“I-Bolivia ayiyuze iyekele lilungelo layo lekutfola indlela yekifinyelela eLwandlekati Lwe-Pacific,” sekangeta.

Tikolwa tase-Scotland letitimele tihlala tinemlandvo welizinga leliphakeme kutemfundvo, futsi loku kuchubeke njalo nangemnyaka wa-2018 lobe nemiphumela lebabatekako, lokuciniswa kuphela yimphumelelo yemuntfu ngamunye nekwawonkhewonkhe kutemidlalo, tebuciko, temculo kanye nalokunye lokwentiwa ngummango.
Njengoba kunebafundzi labangetulu kwa-30,000 e-Scotland, letikolwa letimelelwe libandla i-The Scottish Council of Independent Schools (SCIS), tenta konkhe lokusemandleni kwetfula tinsita letisezingeni lelisetulu kubafundzi bato kanye nebatali.
Tikolwa letitimele tihlose kulungiselela bafundzi bato kuchubeka nemfumdvo lephakeme, imisebenti lebatikhetsela yona kanye nekutsatsa indzawo yabo njengetakhamiti temhlaba wonkhe.
Njegemkhakha wemfundvo longaticambela futsi wetfule luhlelo lwesikolwa lowuntentele lona, sibona tilwini tamanje tichubeka tiba tifundvo letidvumile naletifiswako letingakhetfwa etikolweni.
Nelson Mandela watsi: “Uma ukhuluma nendvodza ngelulwimi laluvako, loko kuya enhloko yakhe.
Uma ukhuluma naye ngelulwimi lwakhe loko kuya enhlitiyweni yakhe.
Loku kusikhumbuto lesinemandla kakhulu sekutsi asikwati kutsi sitsembele elulwimini lwesiNgisi uma sifuna kwakha buhlobo nekwetsembana nebantfu labachamuka kulamanye emave.
Lokuphuma embikweni wemiphumela yalonyaka lesatsandza kukhishwa, singabona kutsi tilwimi tisetulu eluhlwini lwetifundvo kunanatelwe kutsi lizinga lekuphumelela leliphakeme kakhulu lisetikolweni letitimele.
Incenye lengu-68 phesenti yanawuhlanganisa ndzawonye bafundzi labafundze tilwimi tangaphandle itfole sigaba A Lesiphakeme.
Tibalo leticokelelwe etikolweni letingu-74 letingemalunga e-SCIS tibonisa kutsi 72 phesenti webafundzi baphumelele sigaba A Lesiphakeme, kantsi 72-phesenti walabo labafundze si-Jalimani, 69 phesenti walabo labafundze si-Frentji kanye na 63 phesenti walabafundze si-Spanish nabo baphemelele ngesigaba A.
Loku kukhombisa kutsi tikolwa letitimele e-Scotland tisekela tilwimi talamanye emave njengemakhono labalulekile lekungangabateki wutsi bantfwana nalabasha batawadzinga kusasa.
Tilwimi nyalo, njengesifundvo lebangasikhetsa, tibonwa tisesigabeni lesilingana netifundvo tesayensi (STEM - sayensi, tebuchwepheshe, tebunjiniyela kanye ne-mathematics) eluhlelwini lwetikolwa letitimele nakuletinye.
Luphandvo lolwentiwe yi-UK Commission for Employment and Skills ngemnyaka wa-2014 lwatfola kutsi kuleto tizatfu letashiwo bacashi ngemzukuzuku wekugcwalisa tikhala, 17 phesenti wato bekachazwa ngekutsi uhambisana nekungabikho kwemakhono etilwimi.
Kungako kuya ngekwandza kutsi emakhono etilwimi aphocelelwe kuze kutsi bantfu labasha balungiselwe imisebenti yakusasa.
Njengoba ematfuba ekusebenta lafuna tilwimi aya ngekwandza, lamakhono abalulekile emhlabeni jikelele.
Ngekungabuki kutsi umuntfu ukhetsa muphi umsebenti, nangabe ufundze lulwimi lwesibili, batawuba ncono kunalabanye kusasa ngekuba nemakhono emphilo yabo yonkhe njengalawa.
Kwati kukhulumisana ngco nebantfu labaphuma kulamanye emave kutawuvele kumbeke embili emncintiswaneni umuntfu lokhuluma tilwimi letiningi.
Ngekusho kweluvo lwe-YouGov lwalabadzala labangetulu kwa-4,000 e-UK ngemnyaka wa-2013, labangu 75 phesenti bebangakhoni kukhuluma kahle lulwimi lwangaphandle ngalokwenele kutsi bangacocisana ngalo, kwatsi si-Frentji saba kuphela kwelulwimi lolwalukhulunywa bantfu labangu-15 phesenti.
Kungako kuhlanyela ekufundziseni tilwimi nyalo kumcoka kubantfwana banamuhla.
Kuba netilwimi letiningi, ikakhulu leto temave emnotfo losatfutfuka, kutawuhlomisa bantfwana ngematfuba lamahle ekutfola imisebenti lekhanyako.
Ngekhatsi kwe-Scotaland, sikolwa ngasinye siyehluka etilwimini labatifundzisako.
Tikolwa letibalwako titawubukana netilwimi tamanje letivamile, kantsi letinye titawufundzisa tilwimi lekubonakala kutsi tibalulekile e-UK nakubukwa embili ku-2020, njenge-Mandarin noma si-Japhane.
Kuloko lokufiswa ngumntfwanakho, kutawuhlala kukhona tilwimi letimbalwa langakhetsa kuto ngekhatsi kwetikolwa letitimele, letinabothishela labaceceshekile kuloluhlangotsi.
Tikolwa letitimele e-Scotland titimisele kuniketa simo sekufundza lesitawulolonga bantfwana sibahlomise ngemakhono ladzingeka kutsi baphumelele, kungabukwa kutsi likusasa liphetseni.
Angeke kuphikwe kulesikhatsi, kulesimo sebhizinisi lehlanganisa umhlaba wonkhe, kutsi tilwimi tichubeke kubaluleka kakhulu kwentele likusasa lelive, ngako loku kufanele kuboniswe kutemfundvo.
Ngempela, kufanele kutsi tilwimi tamanje tibonwe njenge “makhono ekuchumana mhlaba wonkhe”.
Tikolwa letitimele titawuchubeka kuniketa ematfuba ekukhetsa, kwehlukana kanye nekwenyusa lizinga kubantfu labasha e-Scotland.
Il faut bien le faire.
John Edward ungumcondzisi we-Scottish Council of Independent Schools.
LeBron utawenta i-Lakers ivele kwekucala ngeLisontfo e-San Diego
Kumela LeBron James kutsi ahlanganise sicalo sakhe se-Los Angeles Lakers sekuya ngasekupheleni kubalandzeli bakhe.
Umceceshi we-Lakers, Luke Walton, sewumemetele kutsi James utawudlala emdlalweni wekuvula sendvulela sesikhatsi semidlalo abukane ne-Denver e-San Diego ngeLisontfo.
Kepha-ke kutsi mingaki imizuzu latawuyidlala kusetawumiswa.
“Imizuzu itawuba ngetulu kwamunye nangaphasi kwa-48,” kusho Walton kuwebsaythi lesemtsetfweni ye-Lakers.
Umbiki we-Lakers, Mike Trudell, ufake ku-Tweeter kutsi James angahle adlale imizuzu lefinciwe.
Kulandzela kutilolonga ngasekucaleni kwaleliviki, James wabutwa ngemalungiselelo akhe ngeluhla lwetikhatsi temidlalo lesitfupha yekudlala kwe-Lakers ngaphambi kwekucalisa kwesizini.
Angidzingi imidlalo ngaphambi kwesizini kuze ngilungele kulesigaba semsebenti wami,” kusho yena.
Sikhatsi Serali Ya-Trump E-West Virginia, YouTube Channel
Mengameli Donald Trump ucalisa siyaluyalu semarali emkhankaso namuhla ebusuku e-Wheeling, e-West Virginia.
Yirali ya-Trump yekucala kulasihlanu lahlelelwe liviki lelitako, lekufaka ekhatsi kuma etindzaweni letinebungani letifaka ekhatsi i-Tennessee kanye ne-Mississippi.
Njengoba livoti lekushicilela kucoka kwakhe kwekugcwalisa sikhala lesivuleke Enkantolo Lenkhulu limisiwe, Trump uhlose kukhulisa kusekelwa ngesikhatsi lesitako selukhetfo lwasekhatsi lethemu njengoba ema-Republicans asengotini yekulahlekelwa kubusa i-Congress ngesikhatsi sekukhetsa ngenyanga yeLweti.
Ngusiphi sikhatsi serali ya-Trump namuhla ebusuku futsi wenta njani kuyibukela ku-intanehti?
Irali ya-Trump yase-Wheeling, e-West Virginia imiselwe 7 p.m. ET kusihlwa, tingu-29 kuNyoni, 2018.
Ungayibukela irali ya-Trump yase-West Virginia ku-intanethi ngentasi usebentise kubukela kukhoma ku-YouTube.
Trump angahle akhulume ngendzaba yekulalelwa kuleliviki ngalocokelwe Inkantolo Lenkhulu, Brett Kavanaugh, leyashuba kakhulu ngetinsolo tekungatiphatsi kahle ngasecansini, njengoba kunekumiswa kwelivoti lekushicilela le-Sinethi sikhatsi lesingaba liviki ngesikhatsi i-FBI isaphenya.
Kepha inhloso lenkhulu yalesiyaluyalu semarali kusita ema-Repablican labhekene nelukhetfo lolumatima ngeLweti kutsi abuyise umfutfo.
Ngako umkhankaso waMengameli Trump utsite lamarali lasihlanu kuleliviki lelitako ahlose “kufaka emandla kumavolontiya kanye nebalandzeli njengoba ema-Republican atama kuvikela nekukhulisa bunyenti lebanabo kuSinethi kanye neNdlu Yebameleli,” ngekusho kwe-Reuters.
“Kulawula i-Congress kubaluleke kakhulu kuloluhlelo lwamengameli lwekuhambela tifundza letiningi ngalokusemandleni sisabheke esikhatsini semkhankaso lesiphitsitelako,” kusho lokhulumela umkhankaso wa-Trump longafunanga kutisho ligama, atjela baka-reuters.
Njengoba imiselwe kuya enkhundleni i-Wesbanco Arena lese-Wheeling, irali yanamuhla kusihlwa ingaletsa balandzeli labaphuma e “Ohio nase-Pennsylvania iphindze itfole kuboniswa emisakatweni yase-Pittsburgh,” ngekusho kwebetindzaba i-West Virginia Metro News.
NgeMgcibelo kutaba kwesibili kulenyanga lephelile kutsi Trump avakashele e-West Virginia, sifundza lasiwina ngemaphuzu langemaphesenti langetulu kwa-40 nga-2016.
Trump utama kulekelela locokelwe i-Republican Senate e-West Virginia, Patrick Morrisey, losemuva ngemavoti eluvo.
“Akusiyo inkhomba lekahle kuMorrisey kutsi kuze kute mengameli kutotama kumphakamisa emavotini eluvo,” kusho Simon Haeder, sosayensi yepolitiki eYunivesithi YaseWest Virginia, ngekusho kwa-Reuters.
I-Ryder Cup 2018: Licembu i-Team USA likhombisa ligcabo lekulwa kuze ematsemba aphile kuya kumasingili angeLisontfo
Kulandzela emaseshini lamatsatfu angenhlanye, ema-foursomes angeMgcibelo emini yantsambama kungahle kube ngilokudzingwa ngule-Ryder Cup.
Iphendulamu yemfutfo lojikajikako ngumcondvo wemidlalo locanjiwe kepha lowo badlali labawukholelwa ngempela, futsi kwedlula emncintiswaneni lofana nalena
Kepha-ke sebangatsi lomfutfo ukuphi nyalo?
“Bebasolo bahamba embili ngemaphuzu lasitfupha kepha nyalo semane, ngako sesitfwele loko njengemfutfo lomncane mhlawumbe,” kusho Jordan Spieth asahamba kancane kwalelolanga.
Phela i-Europe inesandla lesingetulu, isembili ngemaphuzu lamane kantsi kusesele lalishumi nambili.
I-Americans, njengoba Spieth asho, umoya uyabavumela futsi banalokuningi lokungabakhutsata, lokungafani neluhlobo lwa-Spieth na-Justin Thomas labadlala kanyekanye lilanga lonkhe futsi ngamunye batichenya ngemaphuzu lamatsatfu kulamane

Loko kumemeta lokukhulu kwekujabula kwaya ngekukhula ngekuchubeka kwemlente wakhe, afaka phasi iphuthi lebalulekile kutsatsa umdlalo webune be-all-square ngesikhatsi yena na-Thomas bebaphasi ngamabili emva kwalamabili.
Iphothi yakhe leyabaphemelelisa kulomdlalo nga-15 wahlangabetwa kumemeta lokufanako, kweluhlobo lolukutjela kutsi ukholwa kutsi licembu i-Americans alikaphumi kuloku.
“Kumele kutsi ushone phasi ucabange ngemdlalo wakho locondzene nawo,” kusho Spieth.
Ngiloko kuphela lesekushiywe ngulabadlali ngamunye.
Timbobo letingu-18 kubeka luphawu.
Badlalilekungibo bodvwa labanemaphuzu langetulu kwa-Spieth na-Thomas kulamalanga lamabili laphelile bo-Frencesco Molinari na-Tommy Fleetwood, indzaba lengaphikiswa yendzebe ye-Ryder Cup.

I-”Moliwood” bekungibo bodvwa lababili labangakafaki ibhogi ngeMgcibelo emva kwemini, kepha nabo bagwema emabhogi ngeMgcibelo ekuseni, ngaLesihlanu emva kwemini nemfica lesemuva ngaLesihlanu ekuseni.
Lowo mgamu, nendlela emandla abo agijima ngakhona kuya nekubuya kulesihlwele kugcizelela kutsi labadlali bekwehlulwa ngeLisontfo, bese kubate labanye badlali labadvumile kucedzela kuncoba lokungenteka kwe-Europe ngekushona kwelilanga e-Le Golf National kuna-Fleetwood noma Molinari.
Lekungaba ncono bobabili ngasikhatsi sinye etimbotjeni letehlukene.
Kepha-ke, kusengakabi sikhatsi sekukhuluma ngebucwaticwati be-Europe.
Bo-Bubba Watson na-Webb Simpson benta umsebenti lomfisha nga-Sergio Garcia, lichawe lemabhola lamane asekuseni, ngesikhatsi baboshelwa na-Alex Noren.

I-Europe idlale ncono njengelicembu kuze kube manje futsi ihamba embili kakhulu basaya elangeni lekugcina kepha leseshini yema-foursomes iphindze yakhombisa kutsi i-Team USA inawo emandla alemphi lelabanye, ikakhulu Stateside, bebanekungabata.
I-Euorpe ihamba embili nga-10-6 elangeni lemancamu le-Ryder Cup
I-Europe itawuba nesandla lesingetulu lesihle kakhulu kusayiwa elangeni lemancamu le-Ryder Cup kulandzela kuphumelela emidlalweni kuma-fourballs nema-foursomes bahamba embili nga-10-6 kune-United States.
Laba lababili, bo-Tommy Fleetwood bana-Francesco Molinari, bebanelugcozi lwekuhola kuphumelela kabili kuna-Tiger Woods lowaba nebumatima kulingana nabo kuze kube ngunyalo e-Le Golf National kumaphuzu lamane.
Luhlangotsi lwase-Europe lwa-Thomas Bjorn, lufuna kugcina indzebe leyabalahlekela e-Hazeltine eminyakeni lemibili leyedlulile, lwahamba embili luncoba luhlangotsi lwema-Merikha kuma-fourballs asekuseni, ancoba loluchunge lwemdlalo nga-3-1.
I-U.S. yakhombisa kuzabalaza kuma-foursomes, ancoba emidlalweni lemibili, kepha abavumanga kwehlulwa.
Luhlangotsi lwa-Jim Furk ludzinga emaphuzu lasiphohlongo emidlalweni yemasingili langu-12 angeLisontfo kuze bagcine lendzebe.
Fleetwood uyirukhi yekucala yase-Europe kuwina emaphuzu lamane ngekulandzelana, kwatsi yena ana-Molonari bacopha “Moliwood” kulandzela imphelasontfo lehlasimulako, ngibo kuphela lababili labatfole emaphuzu lamane emidlalweni yabo lemine yekuvula emlandvweni we-Ryder Cup.
Sebancobe bo-Woods na-Patrick Reed kuma-fourballs base bachubeka babambene kahle kakhulu kuyohlula Woods lobesaphelelwe ngumoya na-Bryson Dechambeau wase-Merikha ngekuncoba lokukhulu kakhulu nga-5 na 4.
Woods, lowatidvonsa emidlalweni lemibili ngeMgcibelo, wabonisa emazwibela ekudlala kahle kepha nyalo sewulahlekelwe yimidlalo lengu-19 kulengu-29 yakhe kuma-fouralls nema-foursomes kanye nalasikhombisa iladzelana.
Justin Rose, sekatfole kuphumulela ema-fourballs asekuseni, wabuyela kuyohlanganyela na-Henrik Stenson kuma-foursomes wayohlula nga 2&1 bo-Dustin Johnson na-Brooks Koepa - lababalelwa endzaweni yekucala neyesitsatfu emhlabeni.
I-Europe ayizange itfole lebeyikufuna noko ngelilanga lebeliphole kamnandzi ngaseningizimu-nshonalanga ne-Paris.
Behluli labakhulu labancoba katsatfu, Jordan Spieth bana-Justin Thomas babuke kubekela ema-Merikha luphawu lwekubekisa ngemaphuzu lamabili ngeMgcibelo.
Batfola kuphumelela nga-2&1 kuletibukwako behlula Jon Rahm na-Ian Pouter wase-Spain kuma-fourballs baphindze babuyela muva kuyohlula Poulter na-Roy Mcllroy 4&3 kuma-foursomes kulandzela kulahlekelwa imigodzi lemibili.
Kukabili kuphela emlandvweni we-Ryder Cup lapho licembu libuya nekwehlulwa ngemaphuzu lamane kumasingili, noma njengalabayiphetse luhlangotsi lwaka-Furyk ludzinga kuphela kulinganisa kuze bagcinne indzebe.
Kepha-ke, kulandzela kuba besibili emalanga lamabili, kuphindzisela kwangeLisontfo kubukeka shengatsi kungetulu kwemandla abo.
I-North Korea itsi ‘cha’ ngekubeka phasi tikhali ngekwayo ngaphandle kwekutsemba
Indvuna yetangaphandle e-North Korea itjele Mhlabuhlangene ngeMgcibelo kutsi kuchubeka nekunklinya kujulisa kungaletsembi live le-United States futsi kute indlela lelive lelingayekela ngakhona tikhali tayo tenyukliya ngekwalo kulesimo lesinje.
Ri Yong Ho utjele Ingcungcuthela Yemhlaba, i-General Assembly, yemnyaka kutsi i-North Korea seyitsetse “tinyatselo leticatsa telucolo” emnyakeni lodlulile, njengekumisa kuvivinywa kwenyukliya netikhali temamisayli, kuchacha takhiwo tendzawo yekuvivinyela inyukliya, kanye nekutibophelela kungandzisi tikhayi tenyukliya netebuchwepheshe bayo inyukliya.
“Kepha-ke, asiboni tento letifana naleto e-U.S.,” kusho yena.
“Ngaphandle kwekutsi kube nekwetsemba i-U.S., ngeke sibe neligunya letekuphepha kwelive letfu futsi nangabe simo sinje ngeke kwenteke kutsi sibeke phasi tikhali ngekwetfu kucala.”
Kutsite Ri nakananatela kukhonona lokufananako kwase-North Korea ngekutsi i-Washington ivimbele indlela “yekucala kancane” kususa tikhali tenyukliya lapho i-North Korea ingavuzelwa tinyatselo tayo, inkhulumo yakhe ibonakale igcamile ngekutsi ayikwalanga nje kubeka phasi tikhali tenyukliya njengoba Pyongyang enta ngaphambili.
Ri bekacondzise enkhulumeni leyashiwo ngu-Kim Jong Un ahlangene na-Donald Trump emhlanganweni wabo wekucala emkhatsini namengameli we-U.S.wangaleso sikhatsi nemholi wase-North Korea e-Singapore ngeNhlaba mhla ka-1, ngesikhatsi Kim atibophelela kusebentela “kuyekela tikhali tenyukliya letisepeninsula ye-Korea” kantsi trump yena watsembisa kucinisekisa kuphepha kwe-North Korea.
I-North Korea beyifuna kuphetfwa ngendlela imphi i-53 Korea War yanga-1950, kepha i-United States itsite Pyongyang kumele ayekele tikhali tenyukliya kucala.
I-Washington iphindze yala imiyalelo yekucekisa kutsi emave emhlaba ashubise kunklinya i-North Korea.
“I-U.S. iyaphikelela ngekutsi “akubekwe phasi tikhali tenyukliya kucala” iphindze ikhulise lizinga lekucindzetela ngekunklinya kuphumelelisa inhloso yabo ngendlela lephocelelako, kanye nekwala “kumemetela kucedvwa kwemphi,”” kusho Ri.
“Lokubuka tintfo ngendlela yekutsi kusinklinya kungasigucisa ngemadvolo kuliphupho nje lebantfu labangati lutfo ngatsi.
Kepha inkinga kutsi lokuchubeka nekusinklinya kujulisa kungetsembi kwetfu.”
Ri akazange akhulume ngemicabango yemhlangano wesibili emkhatsini wa-Kim na-Trump lowaphawulwa ngulomholi we-U.S. ngasekucaleni kweliviki.
Esikhundleni saloko indvuna iphawule ngemihlangano lemitsatfu emkhatsini wa-Kim nemholi we-South Korea, Moon Jae-in, kuletinyanga letisihlanu letedlulile waphindze wengeta kutsi: “Kube lolohlanganyela kuloludzaba lwekuyekelwa kwetikhali tenyukliya bekuyi-South Korea hhayi i-U.S., ngabe kuyekela kwetikhali tenyukliya akukafiki kulesigaba sekungayi embili.”
Noma kunjalo, kuvakala kwenkhulumo ya-Ri kwehluka kakhulu kunasemnyakeni lophelile, ngesikhatsi atjela i-U.N. Genaral Assembly kutsi kubhekisa emarokhethi ase-North korea enkhabeni ye-U.S. kutokwenteka kulandzela kutsi “Mnu. Mengameli Lomubi” Trump abite Kim nge “ndvodza yemarokhethi” lecondze kutibulala.
Kulomnyaka kaMhlabuhlangene, Trump, lekunguye kulomnyaka lophelile wasonga ku “bhidlita acotfule” i-North Korea, wabhumbela tibongo ku-Kim ngesibindzi sakhe sekutsatsa tinyatselo tekubeka phasi tikhali, kepha watsi kuningi lokusamele kwentiwe nekunklinya kume ngemumo ize i-North korea iyekele tikhali tenyukliya.
Kutsite ngaLesitsatfu, Trump watsi akanako kubekisa sikhatsi saloku, asho kutsi “Uma kutsatsa iminyaka lemibili, lemitsatfu noma tinyanga letihlanu - akunandzaba.”
I-China ne-Russia baphawula kutsi libandla i-U.N. Security Council ifanele kuvuza Pyongyang ngetinyatselo letitsetfwe.
Kodvwa-ke, i-U.S. Secretary of State mike Pompeo utjele i-U.N. Security Council ngaLesine kutsi: “Kuciniswa kwekunkliya kwe-Security Council kumele kuchubeke ngemandla nangekungaphazami kuze sibone kuphetsa kwekuyekela tikhali tenyukliya ngalokuphelele nalokucinisekisiwe.
I-Security Council ikhulise kunklinya i-North Korea ngaphandle kwekuphikisana kusukela nga-2006 ngenhloso yekuhisha kufakwa kwetimali etinhlelweni ta-Pyongyang tenyukliya nemamisayli lavutsa umlilo.
Pompeo uhlangene na-Ri eceleni kwengcungcuthela i-U.N. General Assembly waphindze emva kwaloko watsi utawuvakashela Pyongyang futsi ngenyanga lelandzelako kulungiselela umhlangano wesibili.
Pompeo sewuvakashele e-North Korea katsatfu kulomnyaka, kepha luhambo lwakhe lwekugcina aluhambanga kahle.
Washiya Pyongyang ngaKholwane atsi kube nenchubekela embili, kwatsi kungapheli ema-awa lamangaki i-North Korea yamhlambalata ngekwenta “timfuno letifanane yetigebengu.”
I-North Korea itibophelele emhlanganweni na-Moon kulenyanga kutochacha takhiwo temamisayli kanye nesakhiwo senyukliya uma live le-Merikha itsatsa “tinyatselo letifananako.”
Utsite Kim umtjele kutsi “letinyatselo letifananako” lebekatifuna titicinisekiso tekuphepha Trump latibophelela ngato e-Singapore, nekuchubekela kubuyisela budlelwane ne-Washington esimeni lesifanele.
Bafundzi base-Harvard batsatsa sifundvo sekutfola kuphumula ngalokwenele
Sifundvo lesisha eyunivesithi lebitwa nge-Harvard University seyente kutsi bonkhe bafundzi bemabanga laphasi batfole kulala kakhulu ngenhloso yekuncandza kwandza kwemkhuba wekufundza ngekusitwa yikhafeyni ‘busuku bonkhe.’
Lomunye umfundzisi utfole kutsi bafundzi kuleyunivesithi lehamba embili emhlabeni abati lutfo mayelana netintfo tekucala ekutiphatseni kanye nekutinakekela.
Charles Czeisler, longuphrofesa wekulapha tekulala e-Harvard Medical School naloyingcweti e-Brigham and Women's Hospital, ucambe sifundvo lakholwa kutsi sekucala seluhlobo lwaso e-U.S.
Wakhutsateka kucala lesifundvo kulandzela kwetfula inkhulumo ngemphumela wekungatfoli kulala kahle ekufundzeni.
‘Ekupheleni kwayo lenye intfombatana yeta kimi yatsi: ‘Kuya ngani kutsi ngitjelwe loku nyalo sengenta umnyaka wekugcina?’
Watsi kute lowake wamtjela ngekutsi kulala kubaluleke ngani - lokungimangalisile,’ atjela beliphephandzaba i-The Telegraph.
Lesifundvo lesetfulwa kwekucala lonyaka, sichazela bafundzi tintfo letidzingekako ngekutsi imikhuba lemihle yekulala isita kanjani kuphumelela ekufundzeni nasemidlalweni, kanye nasekwenteni kuphila kwabo kube ncono.
Paul Barreira, longuphrofesa wetengcondvo e-Harvard Medical School nalongumcondzisi wetinsika kutemphilo kuleyunivesithi, utsite iyunivesithi incume kucalisa lesifundvo kulandzela kutsi itfole kutsi bafundzi abatfoli kulala ngalokwenele evikini.
Lesifundvo lesitsatsa li-awa sisebentisa tindlela temisebenti leyenta nihlanganyele.
Kulenye incenye kunesitfombe selikamelo lekulalisa bantfu labaningi, lapho bafundzi bafacata tinkomishi telikhofi, emakhethini, kwekutishukumisa kanye netincwadzi bese batjelwa ngemitselela yekhafeyni nekukhanya, nekutsi kwenta kahle kutemidlalo kungabangwa nemtselela lomubi wekungalali ngalokwenele, nangekubaluleka kweluhlelo lwesikhatsi sekulala.
Kulenye futsi incenye, bahlanganyeli kulesifundvo batjelwa ngekutsi kungatfoli kulala kahle losekutsetse sikhatsi lesidze kungakhulisa bungoti bekuhlaseleka kwenhlitiyo, kufa kwemitsambo, nekudzangala kanye nemdlavuza.
Umbalave wemabala aleyunivesithi, lonetinkinobho letitsintsekako, wona ubese ubakhutsata kutsi bacabange ngeluhlelo lwabo lwemalanga onkhe.
‘Siyati kutsi angeke sigucule kutiphatsa kwebafundzi ngaleso sikhatsi.
Kepha siyakholwa kutsi banelilungelo lekwati - njengoba nawe unelilungelo lekwati imitselela yekukhetsa kubhema sikilidi emphilweni,’ sekwengeta Phrofesa Czeisler.
Umkhuba wekutichenya ngeku “dvonsa busuku konkhe” usekhona, kusho yena, angeta ngekutsi buchwepheshe bamanje nekukhula njalo kwekutfweseka kwebafundzi kusho kungatfoli kulala lokwenele kuyinkinga lekhulako.
Kucinisekisa kutsi utfola kulala kahle ngalokwenele, kufanele kube ‘sikhali lesifihlekile’ semfundzi sekuncandza kukhatsateka, kukhatsala kanye nekungaphumuli, kusho yena - ngisho nekukhulisa sisindzo semtimba, njengoba kungalali ngalokwenele kuncisha ingcondvo, kubente bahlale balambile.
Raymond So, loneminyaka lengu-19 budzala wase-California lofundzela ibhayoloji lephatselene nalokutsakiwe nekwemtimba, nguye lowasita lophrofesa kucamba nekuhlanganisa lesifundvo, kulandzela kutsi naye ahlanganyele kulelinye lemaklasi akhe ngesikhatsi enta umnyaka wakhe wekucala e-Harvard.
Utsite lesifundvo simvule emehlo lokwamkhutsata kutsi alwele kutsi lesifundvo setfulwe kuwo onkhe emabala aleyunivesithi.
Sinyatselo lesiladzelako, ngekwetsemba, sekutsi kucelwe bonkhe bafundzi bemabanga lasetulu kutsi bente luhlelo lolufana nalolu ngaphambi kwekutsi bangenele tifundzo kuleyunivesithi lencintisanako.
Phrof. Czeisler uncome kutsi bafundzi bafanele bacuphe i-alamu lebakhumbuta nasekusikhatsi sekuyolala, nangekutsi bavuke nini, futsi bahlale bati ngemitselela lemibi ye ‘kukhanya lokuluhlata’ lokukhishwa tikrini tekhompyutha nekukhanya kwe-LED, lokungaphazamisa sigci semtimba endleleni, kuholele etinkingeni tekulala.
Livingston 1-0 Rangers: Ligoli la-Menga lijika phasi bafana ba-Gerrard
I-Rangers I-Rangers ihlushwe kushaywa tidvubuti temdlalo welilanga bahambile ngesikhatsi kushaya kwa-Menga kwavimbetela luhlangotsi lwa-Gerrard lolungahlangani kwehlulwa nga 1-0 e-Livingston.
Luhlangotsi lwe-Ibrox belugadze kubhalisa kuphulela kwalo kwekucala endleleni yabo kusukela ngekuncoba kwabo nga 4-1 ngeNdlovana e-St Johnstone, kepha licembu la-Gary Holt libetse Gerrard kwesibili emidlalweni lengu-18 angumphatsi yashiya luhlangotsi lwakhe ngemaphuzu lasiphohlongo ngemuva kwe-Hearts ye-Ladbrokes Premiership leyeduka.
Menga wadubula sekusele imizuzu lesikhombisa kuphele sigamu sekucala nekuhleliswa kwe-Rangers kushoda ngelugcozi akuzange kubukeke shengatsi kuyalinganisa.
Njengaloku i-Rangers yehlela endzaweni yesitfupha, i-Livingston ikhuphukela kuyesitsatfu kantsi ingemuva kwe-Hibernian ngemehluko wemagoli.
Futsi kwakungekho lokusengayikhatsata i-Rangers kulandzela kutsi somugca longu-Calum spence adzinge kulashelwa silondza enhloko emva kujikijelwa ngesilimato lekubonakala kutsi sachamuka ngaseluhlangitsini lwasekuhambeni.
Gerrard wenta tingucuko letisiphohlongo kuloluhlangotsi lokwedlula ngelihubo ku-Ayr tabangenisa ku-Betfred Cup ngaphambi kwemancamu.
Holt yena, ngakulolunye luhlangotsi, wahamba naleyo Livi 11 leyemuka i-Hearts liphuzu evikini leliphelile futsi bekatayitsakasela indela lesipani sakhe lesicecesheke kahle yacindzetela ngakhona titsa tabo kuwo onkhe emajika.
Kungahle kube i-Rangers yabusa ngesikhatsi ibhola ibe ngakubo kepha i-Livinston yenta lokuningi ngelibhola leyaba nalo.
Bekufanele ngabe bafaka ligoli sekuphele imizuzu lemibili nje kungeniwe enkhundleni kwatsi kukhishwa kwa-Menga kwekucala kwatfumela Scott Pitman wangena ngeligoli la-Allan McGregor kepha lomdlali wasekhatsi wadvonsa litfuba lakhe lelikhulu.
Libhola lelingavinjwa la-Keaghan Jacobs lelimatima lase litfola kapteni Craig Halkett kepha umvimbi wakhe Alan Litgow wakhona kulihlaba epalini lelisemuva.
I-Rangers yakhona kutfola kulawula kepha kwabukeka kunelitsemba ngetulu kwekutsi bayakholwa ngemdlalo wabo babesitsatfu kumancamu.
Alfredo Morelos wativela acinisekisile kutsi bekufanele atfole iphenalthi nakuphela siganyana sesine njengoba yena na-Steven Lawless bashayisana kodvwa rafela Steven Thomson waphakamisela lomdlali wase-Colombia indvwangu.
I-Rangers yakhona kungenisa emagoli lamabili nje esiwombeni sekucala kodvwa umvimbi wemagoli we-Ibrox Liam Kelly akahlushwanga kakhulu libhola lenhloko la-Lassana Coulibaly nekukhahlela kwa-Ovie Ejaria.
Njengoba ligoli lekuvula ngemzuzu waka-34 kungahle kube laphambana nemdlalo, kute longa phika kutsi belibafanelwe kulelihlumela lodvwa.
I-Rangers yaphindze yehluleka kubukana nalekumiswe ngu-Jacobs
Scott Arfield akazange aphindzisele ngesikhatsi Declan Gallagher angenisa libhola ku-Scott Robinson, lowakutsatsa kalula kukhetsa Menga abese ulicedzela kalula.
Gerrard wasukuma ngesikhatsi selikhefu washintjanisa Coulibaly na-Ryan Kent futsi lolushintjo lwacishe lwaletsa umphumela ngesikhatsi lomdlali waseluphikweni ashaya Morelos kepha Kelly lowenta letibukwako wagijima ngasecaleni lakhe wayovimba.
Kepha i-Livingston yachubeka kugwinya tihambi batenta badlala ngendlela lebajabulisa bona, bo-Lithgow na-Halkett bavutsela emabhola lamadze alandzelana.
Luhlangotsi lwa-Holt lungahle lube lwachubeka nekuhola kwabo ngasemaphetselweni emdlalo kepha McGregor wema kahle wamuka Jacobs ngaphambi kwekutsi Lithgow wafayela libholi lenhloko lisuka ekoneni.
Glenn Middleton we-Rangers lowangena emkhatsini wasebentisa iphenalthi ngesikhatsi aphica Jacobs kepha Thomson wabuka eceleni.
I-Almanaki: Umcambi we-Geiger Counter
Nyalo-ke lipheji leliphuma ku-Almanaki ye “Sunday Morning” yetfu: Mhla ka-30 kuNyoni, 1882, eminyakeni lengu-136 leyadlula ngalelilanga lanamuhla, futsi SIBALA ... lelilanga ingcweti yakusasa kutefiziksi Johannes Wilhelm “Hans” Geiger watalwa e-Germany.
Geiger wasungula indlela yekubona nekukala kukhishwa kwemisebe legijima ngelitubane lelkhulu, lusungulo lolwagcina luholela kudivaysi leyatiwa nge-Geiger Counter.
Njengemgogodla wesayensi kusukela lapho, i-Geiger Counter nayo yaba ngumgogodla wemkhuba lodvumile, njengalifilimu i “Bells of Coronado,” la-1950 lelalibukisa labo lebekubonakala shengatsi bangeke babe bososayensi Roy Rogers na-Dale Evans:
Yenabakitsi: “Ngabe yini kona loku?”
Rogers: “Yi-Geiger Counter, lesetjentiswa kutfola emaminerali lakhipha imisebe legijima ngelitibane lelikhulu lafana ne-uranium.
Mawulalela ngema-iyefoni, ungayiva imisindvo yema-athomu lakhishwa kushukuma kwawo kumaminerali.”
Evans: “Asitsi, sekuvele kuyachuma!
“Hans” Geiger wafa ngemnyaka wa-1945, sekusele emalanga lambalwa abe neminyaka lengu-63.
Kepha loku lakusungula lokuneligama lakhe kusachubeka kuyaphila.
Umjovo lomusha wemdlavuza ungafundzisa emasotja emtimba ‘kubona’ emaseli lamabi
Umjovo lomusha wemdlavuza ungafundzisa emasotja emtimba ‘kubona’ emaseli lamabi futsi uwabulale.
Umjovo wekugoma ufundzisa emasotja emtimba kubekisa emaseli lamabi njengencenye yekwelapha
Indlela yekwenta loku isebentisa kukhipha emaseli lasanemandla ekuvikela kumuntfu logulako, bese ayaguculwa e-lab
Babese ‘babona’ iprotheyni levamile kulamanye emaseli emdlavuza bese baphindze bawajove
Umjovo losalingwa ubonisa imiphumela lenika litsemba kubantfu labagulako labanetinhlobo letitsite temdlavuza.
Lomunye umfati lolashwe ngalomjovo, lofundzisa emasotja emtimba kubekisa emaseli lamabi, wabona umdlavuza wakhe unyamalala sikhatsi lesingetulu kwetinyanga letingu-18.
Indlela yekwenta isebentisa kukhipha emaseli kumuntfu logulako, aguculwe elabhorathri kuze akhone ‘kubona’ iphrotheyni lebitwa nge-HER2 levamile kuleminye imidlavuza, bese lamaseli aphindze ajoviwa emtimbeni.
Phrofesa Jay Berzofsky, we-US National Cancer Institute e-Bethesda, e-Maryland, usho njalo. “Imiphumela yetfu isitjela kutsi sinemjovo lotsembisa kusebenta.”
I-HER2 “ichuba kukhula kwetinhlobo lelimbalwa temdlavuza.” lokufaka ekhatsi yemabele, yesibeletho, yemaphaphu kanye neyematfumbu lamakhulu, kuchaza Phrof. Berzofsky.
Linye indlela lecishe ifane nale yekutsatsa emaseli kumuntfu logulako bese “afundziswa” kutsi awacondvwa kanjani emaseli, isebentile ekwelapheni luhlobo lolutsite lwemdlavuza wematsambo.

Bangicaphatile!
Base baphindze batsi ngiselubishini,” kusho yena, ngekusho kweMhloli we-Washington.

Ukhululekile.
Natsi kanjalo.” sekangeta.

Ngicabanga kutsi empeleni loko kungulomunye wemibuto lemikhulu kulesikhatsi setfu - sikugucula kanjani loko?
Ngoba kuyakhanya kutsi kukhona lokuhambe kabi kulabasha betfu.’

HIV/Aids: I-China ibika kwenyuka nga-14% kwetehlakalo letisha
I-China imemetele kwenyuka nga-14% kwesibalo setakhamiti letiphila ne-HIV ne-Aids.
Bantfu labangetulu kwa-820,000 kulelive bayatsintseka, kusho labasebenta temphilo.
Kubikwe tehlakalo letisha letilinganiselwa ku-40,000 esigamini sesibili kuletine semnyaka wa-2018 kuphela.
Liningi letehlakalo letisha tivele ngekulalana, lokusho ingucuko kunasesikhatsini lesedlulile.
Ngekwemlandvo, i-HIV yandza ngekushesha etindzaweni letiningi tase-China njengemphumela wengati lengenwe nguleligciwane lefakwe kubantfu.
Kepha-ke sibalo sebantfu labasuleleka nge-HIV ngalendlela beseyinciphe yacishe yangabikho, kusho baphatsi betemphilo e-China engcungcutheleni lesesifundzeni se-Yunnan.
Umnyaka ngemnyaka, noko, sibalo salabo labaphila ne-HIV ne-Aids e-China senyuke ngebantfu labangu-100,000.
Kwesulelana nge-HIV ngekwebucansi kuyindzaba lesematseni emphakatsini webantfu beluhlobo lwe-LGBT e-China.
Buhlobo bebulili lobufanako kwentiwa kwangabi licala e-China nga-1997, kepha kubandlululwa kwebantfu beluhlobo lwe-LGBT kutsiwa kuyandlondlobala.
Ngenca yemagugu emphilo langavumelani kakhulu netingucuko, luphandvo lolwehlukene lulinganisele kutsi emandvodza langu 70-90% lalalana nalamanye emadvodza atawugcina atsetse bafati.
Lokuningi kwalokusulelana kwetifo kuchamuka ngekungabikho kwetivikelo tasecansini letenele kulokuhlobana.
Kusukela nga 2003, hulumende we-China utsembise kutfolakala kwemitsi yekwelapha i-HIV nguwonkhewonkhe njengemitamo yekucatulula loludzaba.

Kubuketwa Kwekubuya Futsi Kwa-Johny English - bucili bebuhloli ba-Rowan Atkinson lobunganikwa emandla
Sekuyinjwayelo nyalo kubuka lokugcamile kunoma nguliphi lifilimu lelisha lelitsintsa i-Brithani nalelibonakala lisebentiseka ekuvuseteleni lefrantjaysi yebucili bekhomedi ya-Johny English - lelacala emuva nga 2003 na-Johny English labuya futsi nga 2011 na-Johny English Reborn.
Kambe lokutilinganisa lokufaka-lulwimi-esihlatsini endzabeni yekutsi sivele sitibi kangako kube litfuba lelisha lekutsengisa ngaphandle?
Noma kunjalo, lomehlo-makhulu, nebuso lobuyirabha nalongati lutfo, Johny English sewube nayo ilayisense yakhe yekuhlanganisa tintfo tivusetelwe kwesibili - leligama lakhe libonisa kakhulu kunalokunye kutsi ungulodalelwe inhlekisa lebanti leyentelwe tindzawo letingakhulumi siNgisi letingayi emasinema.
Phela vele uyi-ejenti yangasese lelibele lotsi noma kutishaya kwakhe lokuyincaba kwenta kukhatikhati, utfole lokuncane kwa-Clouseau, imbijana ya Mnu. Bean kanye nekutihlaza kwalomlisa lofaka inothi yinye yengoma leyingcikitsi ye-Chariots of Fire emkhosini wekuvula ema-Olimphiki ase-London anga-2012.
Uphindze ancike kwasekucaleni kumhambi nendvodza yemfihlo yemave Atkinson lowake wadlala sikhangiso se-TV se-Barclaycard, washiya siphitsiphitsi ekuvukeni kwakhe.
Kukhona umzuzu munye noma lemibili lemnandzi kulokuvakasha kwa-JE.
Ngangitsandza ngesikhatsi Johny English asondzela endizeni lenelusiba emhlane agcoke isudu yemphi yaleto tikhatsi naleto tinsiba talendiza titishaya esigcokweni sakhe sensimbi.
Siphiwo sa-Atkinson sekuhlekisa sikhangisiwe, kepha lamahlaya avakala angenamandla futsi angakadzingeki, ikakhulu nangabe emagama emafilimu “langahlekisi” lanjenge 007 ne-Mission Impossible wona asafaka emahlaya njengesitsako.
Lelihlaya livakala shengatsi lentelwe bantfwana esikhundleni sebantfu labadzala, futsi kimi lombukiso wa-Johny English walokungahambi kahle awubonisi kuba nengcondvo yekucamba nekubuka intfo yinye njengekwekuhlekisa kumuvi lethulile ya-Atkinson angumlingisi wa-Bean.

Kantsi loko kusho Johny English cobo lwakhe logcwele tiphosiso, nyalo losacashwe njengemphatsi wesikolwa kulenye indzawo lehamba embili, kepha loniketa tifundvo letingakabhalwa ndzawo tekutsi ungaba ngumuntfu losebenta afihlekile kanjani: kunalokuhlekisako kuloku, njengoba English ane-akhademi yetinhloli ku-School of Rock-type .

Kusenjalo, ndvunankhulu usengotini yekuwela emlingweni walotsandvwako nalosigwili sethekhi lotsi yena angatisombulula tinkinga tetimphi tase-Britain temakhomputha: soni lesingu-Jason Volta, losalingiswa ngu-Jake Lacy.
Bo-English na-Bough bacalisa luhambo lwabo loludze lwemajika laphakeme langenangcondvo: bagcoke njengaboweta, balumeka umlilo e-restorenti ye-French; badala inyakanyaka batibhacise eskebheni sa-Volta; futsi English ususa incushuncushu ngesikhatsi atama kusebentisa i-headset kubona lokungekhatsi kwendlu ya-Volta.

Yini Umkhosi we-Global Citizen futsi Kukhona Yini Lokwentile Kwehlisa Bumphofu?
NgaloMgcibelo i-New York itawube yemukela tivakashi teMkhosi we-Global Citizen, umcimbi lowenteka kanye ngemnyaka loneludvwendvwe lwetihlabani letibabatekako tenta letibukwako kanye nemishini lebabateka ngalokunjalo; kucedza bumphofu emhlabeni.
Njengoba sewuneminyaka lesikhombisa, loMkhosi we-Global Citizen utawubona emakhulu etinkhulungwane tebantfu tiphelela e-Baleni Lelikhulu le-Central Park bangetutijabulisa kuphela ngalokwentiwa baculi labanjenga-Janet Jackson, Cardi B na Shawn Mendes, kepha nekutocwashiswa ngemgomo longiwo walomcimbi wekucedza bumphofu lobesabekako kungakapheli umnyaka wa-2030.
LoMkhosi we-Global Citizen, lowacala nga-2012, uchubekisa i-Global Poverty Project, licembu lelimele emave ngelitsemba lekucedza bumphofu ngekukhulisa sibalo sebantfu labalwa nabo.
Kuze utfole lithikithi lamahhala lekungena kulomcimbi (ngaphandle nangabe uyafuna kukhokhela lithikithi letitatanyiswa (VIP)), batsameli bekhonsathi kwakufanele bacedze luhla lwemisebenti letsite, noma “tento” letinjenge kuvolontiya, batfumele iimeyili kumholi lotsite wemhlaba, bashaye lucingo noma ngutiphi letinye tindlela letinekusita kucwashisa ngemgomo wekucedza bumphofu.
Kodvwa i-Global Citizen iphumelele kanganani njengoba sekusele iminyaka leli-12 kufeza lomgomo?
Ngabe lomcondvo wekuvuza bantfu ngekhonsathi lengakhokhelwa iyindlela lengiyo yini yekukhutsata bantfu kufuna kutsi kusetjentwe, noma nje ngulesinye sento lekutsiwa yi “clicktivism” - bantfu beva shengatsi benta umehluko weliciniso ngekusayina sicelo se-intanethi noma batfumele ithwithi.
Kusukela nga-2011, i-Global Citizen itsi sekubikwe “tento” letingetulu kwetigidzi leti-19 letiphuma kubalandzeli bayo, uchuba kubukwa kwemigomo leminingi lehlukene.
Itsi letento tisitile kuphumuta baholi bemhlaba kumemetela tibopho netinchubomgomo lelingaliswa nemali netigidzigidzi leti-$37 lebekelwe kutsintsa timphilo tetigidzigidzi leti-2.25 tebantfu ngemnyaka wa 2030.
Ngasekucaleni kwa-2018, lelicembu lakhomba tibopho letinge-390 netimemetelo letisukela etentweni tabo, lokungenani imali letigidzigidzi leti-$10 wato seyivele ikhishiwe noma icociwe.
Lelicembu lilinganisela kutsi letimali letitfolakele setibe nemtselela locondzene nebantfu labacishe babe tigidzi leti-649 emhlabeni wonkhe.
Letinye taletibopho letigcamile tifaka ekhatsi luhlelo lolunendlunkhulu e-U.K., lolubitwa nge-The Power of Nutrition, lokulubanjiswano lwalabahlanyela timali nebetfuli bemsebenti labatimisele “kusita banfwana kutsi bakhule ngalokuphelele,” lokutsembisa kuniketa i-Rwanda tigidzi leti-$35 kusita ekucedzeni kungondlengi kahle kwebantfu kulelolive kulandzela kutsi kutfolakale emathwithi langetulu kwa-4,700 laphuma ku-Global Citizen.
Ngelusito loluphuma kuhulumende wase-U.K., banikeli betimali, bohulumende bemhlaba, kanye nema-Global Citizen lafana nawe, singenta kutsi lokungabikho bebulungisa bekungondleki kwebantfu kutenhlalakahle kube yi-footnote emlandvweni,” kusho lincusa le-The Power of Nutrition, Tracey Ullman, atjela sicuku ngesikhatsi sekhonsati e-London ngenyanga yaMabasa nga 2018.
Lelicembu laphindze latsi emva kwekutsi tento letingetulu kwa-5,000 tentiwa kucela i-U.K. kutsi ikhulise kondliwa kwebantfwana nabonina, hulumende wamemetela kuniketwa kwemali yephrojekthi, i-Power of Nutrition, letawufinyelela etigidzini letisihlanu sebafati kanye nebantfwana ngekungenelela ngetondlo.
Kuphendvula lomunye wemibuto levame kubutwa (FAQs) kuwebsaythi ubuta lotsi “yini lekwenta kutsi ucabange kutsi singabucedza bumphofu lobedlulele?”
I-Global Citizen yatsi: “Kutoba yindlela lendze nalematima - kulesinye sikhatsi sitakuwa siphindze sehluleke.
Kepha, njengemzabalazo lomkhulu wemalungelo eluntfu kanye nekungavumelani-nahulumende welubandlululo lokusembikwetfu, sitawuphumelela, ngoba sinemandla lamakhulu masibumbene.
