Waboshwa futsi wabekwa licala lesehlakalo sebudlova basekhaya ngeMsombuluko ebusku
"Loku indvodzana yami lehlangabetana nako, loku lahlangabetana nako nakabuya, ngiyevelana naleminye imindeni leva tinkiyankiya te-PTSD nekulimala kwalamanye emasotja etfu labauya nako," watjela tetsamelilwati kurali yaDonald Trump eTulsa, eOklahoma.
Palin wabita kuboshwa kwakhe ngekutsi "yindlovu lesendlini" waphindze futsi watsi ngendvodzana yakhe naletitinye tigayigayi, "babuya behlukile kancane, babuya bacinile, babuya batibuka kutsi kukhona yini kuhlonipheka mayelana naloko emasotja nemphi yasemoyeni, kanye nawo onkhe emalunga etembutfo wemphi, lakunike lelive."
Waboshwa ngeMsombuluko eWasilla,e-Alaska, waphindze futsi wabekwa licala letebudlova basekhaya labente kulomunye make, afaka lunyawo lwengulube embikweni webudlova basekhaya kanye nekuphatsa silimato adzakiwe, ngekuya kwaDan Bennett, lokhulumela Litiko Letemaphoyisa laseWasilla.

"Kukhoseliswa kwalabo labashiya emakhaya abo emaveni abo ngobe bayahlushwa noma bayesaba mayelana nebuhlanga, tenkholo, buve, noma bulunga ecenjini lelitsite letanhlalonoma umbono wetepolitiki," kwasho Sessions esimemetelwei sakhe senchubomgomo sangeNhlaba mhla ti- 11.

Lincusa laseMelika lisola Ishayina 'ngebuhonga' lobune'tikhangiso letifakana umoya weluchuku'
Ngemuva kweliviki liphephandzaba lelisemtsetfweni laseShayina likhiphe sikhangiso lesitsetse emkahasi lamane ephepheni le-U.S.lawonkhe malanga tinzuzo tekuhwebelana teMelika neShayina, lincusa laseMelika eShayina lasola iBeijing ngekusebentisa liphephandzaba laseMelika kubhebhekisa inkhulumo lenemtselela wemoya weluchuku.
Imelika Mengameli Donald Trump ngaLesitsatfu lowendlulile ubhekise kusengeto seChina Daily lesikhokhelwako kuDes Moines Register - liphephandzaba lesifundza saselowa lelitsengwa kakhulu - ngemuva kwekusola Ishayina ngekufuna kufaka imphumulo ngeLweti mhla ti-6 elukhetfweni lwelibandla leMelika, licala Ishayina leliphikako.
Letinsolo taTrump tekutsi iBeijing beyetama kufaka imphulo elukhetfweni lweMelika kwenta naku tikhulu te-Melika letakutjela i-Reuters kutsi sigaba lesisha kumkhankhaso lobhebhetselwa yiWashington kutsi kucindzetelwe Ishayina
Nanoma-nje kuyintfo leyetayelekile kutsi imibuso yente tikhangiso letikhutsata tekuhwebelana, iBeijing neWashington kwamanje asesemphini lechubekako yetekuhwebelana lebente kutsi bakhokhisane umtselo emphahleni labayitsenga lomunye kulomunye.
Ematharifu ekuphindzisela kweShayina ekucaleni kwemphi yetekuhwebelana bekentelwe kushaya labatsengisa imphahla bayitsengisele letinye tifundza njengelowa, sifundza lesitsengisela kakhulu Ishayina lesesekela Licembu laTrump leRepublican, kusho tingcweti taseMelika neteShayina.
Terry Branstad, lincusa laseMelika leliseShayina kanye naloyo bekayindvuna yaselowa, sifundza lesitsengisela kakhulu Ishayina imikhicito yetekulima, utsite iBeijing ilimete basebenti baseMelika, balimi kanye nemabhizinisi.
Ishayina, Branstad wabhala emkhakheni wemibono kuDes Moines Register yangeLisontfo, "manje seyiphindza kabili buhonga nekuchuba tikhangiso tenkhulumo lenemtselela weluchuku kutetindzaba tetfu letikhululekile."
"Ekwendluliseni umoya weluchuku wayo, Ishayina itingenisa esikweni leMelika lekukhuluma ngekukhululeka netindzaba letikhululekile ngekufaka sikhangiso lesikhokhelwako ku-Des Moines Register," kwabhala Branstad.
"Kucatsanisa, esitendini setindzaba esitaladini lapha eBeijing, utawutfola emavi lambalwa lanemibono leyehlukene futsi angeke uyibone imibono yekutilahla ematsambo yebantfu baseShayina labangaba nayo endleni yemnotfo waseShayina lobahluphako, nakubukwa kutsi betindzaba bangaphasi kwencindzetelo yeLicembu Lemakomanisi LaseShayina," kwabhala yena.
Wengete ngelekutsi "linye lemaphephandzaba lamakhulu aseShayina ayaplkubalekela lokushicilela" i-athikili yakhe, nanoma-nje akazange asho kutsi nguliphi leliphephandzaba.

Njnegoba ema-Republican lamanyenti ayema avikele loyo lokhetfwe yiNkantolo Lephakeme Brett Kavanaugh lobukene netinsolo letinyenti tekulimata ngekwemacansi, bahlatisi bacaphelisa kutsi batawubona kuphendvula lokungasikahle, ikakhulu lokuvela kubomake, kulolukhetfo lolutako lethemu lesemkhatsini.
Imiva lephatselene naloku iphakmee kakhulu, futsi ema-Republican lamanyenti asevele abhalisiwe kukhombisa kutsi angeke achubeke nekuvota.
Leto tintfo leto atikwati kutsi tingabuyiselwa emuva," Grant Reeher, solwati wetesanyensi yetepolitiki weSyracuse University's Maxwell School watjela i-The Hill nge-athikili leyashicilelwa ngeLisontfo.
Reeher utsite uyakungabata kufuca ngemzuzu wekugcina kweMphunga Jeff Flake's (R-Arizona) mayela neluphenyo lwe-FBI kutsi lutawuba ngulolwenele kwehlisa lulaka lwebavoti labatfukutsele.

NgaLesihlanu ekusebi, babhikisha bebahlabela ticubulo "Lweti luyeta!" ngesikhatsi babhikisa ephaseji yeMphunga lapho ema-Republican lalawula Likomidi Letebulungiswa akhetsa kuya kuchubekelembili nekwenylwa kwaKavanaugh ngekunganaki bufakazi baDkt. Christine Blasey Ford, kwabika Mic.

Kwengeta, labangemaphesenti lange-38 batsite bacabanga kutsi Kavanaugh kungenteka kutsi ucambe emanga ngesikhatsi sebufakazi bakhe, knatsi labangemaphesenti lange-30 basho lokufananako nga-Ford.

Umsunguli weWebhu Yemhlaba Wonkhe Ihlela Kwenta I-inthanethi Lesha Letawucudzelana neGoogle ne-Facebook
Tim Berners-Lee, umsunguli weWebhu Yemhlaba Wonkhe, wetfula tinsaba letihlose kuvusetela i-Facebook, i-Amazon ne-Google.
Umklmao wakamuva walelichawe letetheknoloji, Ligalelo, yinkmpani leyakha inkhundla levulekile leCinile yaBerners-Lee.
I-Solid ivumela basebentisi kutsi bakhetse kutsi bafuna kutsi imininingwane yabo igcinwe kuphi nekutsi ngubaphi bafundzi labavunyelwe kufinyelela luphi lwatiso.
Kungcogcoluhlolo lekhetsekile ne-Fast Company, Berners-Lee wente lihlaya lekutsi le-nthanethi ngemuva kwe-Inrupt "yengamela umhlaba."
"Sifanele kutsi sikwente manje,"ukusho loko mayelana naletinsaba.
"Sikhatsi sencophamlandvo."
Le-app isebentisa itheknoloji yaSolid kuvumela bantfu kutsi batentele "sabo sitolo semininingwane saku-inthanethi’’ noma i-POD.
Singaba netinhlu lwetekuchumana, talokutawentiwa, ikhalenda, umtapolwati wemculo nalamanye emathulusi akho etebungcweti.
KunjengeGoogle Drive, i-Microsoft Outlook, i-Slack kanye ne-Spotify konkhe kukhona kubhrawuza yinye futsi konkhe ngesikhatsi sinye.
Lokukhetsekile ngalesitolo semininingwane saku-inthanethi kutsi konkhe kukumnikati longafinyelela nanoma nguluphi lwatiso lalufunako ngesikhatsi lasifunako.
Lenkampani ikubita ngekutsi "kutihlomisa ngemakhono ngekumininingwane."
Umbono we-Inrupt, ngekuya kwe-CEO yenkampani John Bruce,kutsi lenkampani iletse imitfombolusito, inchubo kanye nemakhono lafanele kwenta kutsi i-Solid itfolwe nguwonkhewonkhe.
Lenkampani kwamanje ine-Berners-Lee, Bruce, inkhundla yetekuvikelaka leletfwa yi-IBM, basebenti labacashelwe kusebenta kulomklamo, ummango wemavolontiya lalbhala ngemakhodi.
Kucala kuleliviki, batfutfukisi betetheknoloji emhlabeni wonkhe jikelele bangatakhela abo ema-app lasetindzaweni letehlukene basebentisa emathulu lakhona kuwebhu ye-Inrupt.
Berners-Lee utsite yena kanye nelicembu lakhe abakhulumisani ne-"Facebook ne-Google mayelana nekutsi bayingenis enoma bangayingenisi ingucuko lephelele lapho khona onkhe emamodeli emabhizinisi abo amiswe ngalokuphelele ngebusuku bunye.
"Asiceli imvume yabo."
Kulesinye sishicilelwa lesishicilelwe kuMedium ngeMgcibelo, Berners-Lee ubhalele kutsi imishini ye i-Inrupt's "kunikete i-eneji yetimakethe kanye nekusebentisana kwelekelela kuvikela sitfunti nebungibo balewebhu lensha leyakhelwe ku-Solid."
Nga-1994, Berners-Lee wantjintja i-inthanethi ngesikhatsi asungungula Inhlangano Yewebhu Yemave Emahlaba eSikhungweni Setetheknoloji aseMassachusetts.
Kuletinyanga, Berners-Lee unelivi lelinemtselela kunethi lesemkhatsini yedathabhesi.
Ngisho nangesikhatsi kwetfulwa i-Inrupt, Berners-Lee utawuchubeka nekuba nguMsunguli neMcondzisi weNhlangano yeWebhu Yemave Emahlaba, Sikhwama seWebhu kanye neSikhungu Sedatha Lesivulekile.
"Ngisetsemba kakhulu lesikhatsi lesitako sewebhu,"kwengeta Berners-Lee.
Bernard Vann: WW1 Victoria Cross umholi uyabungatwa
Lekungio kuphela Lisontfo laseNgilandi lelawina i-Victoria Cross ngeMphi Yemhlaba yekucala njengalo bekalwa emphini lobungatwa eveni lakubo iminyaka le-100 ngemuva kwaloko.
Lt Col Umfundisi Bernard Vann watfola umklomelo mhla tinge-29 Inyoini 1918 ekuhlaselweni eBellenglise naseLehaucourt.
Nanoma kunjalo, wabulawa lisotja lebelitifihlile ngemuv akwemalnaga lamane futsi akatange ati kutsi uwine umklomelo lomkhulukati waseBritain wekuhlonishwa mayelana netemphi.
Litje lakhe lesikhumbuto lavulwa batukulu bakhe labadvuna lababili kuphareyidi eRushden, eNorthamptonshire, ngeMgcibelo.
Munye wemadvodzana labatukulu bakhe, Michael Vann, watsi "kuluphawu loluhle kakhulu" lelitje litawuvetwa eminyakeni le-100-ngco kusukela ngesikhatsi sekuwin akwamkhulu wakhe.
Ngekuya kweGazeni yaseLandani, mhl atinge-29 Inyoni 1918 Lt Col Vann wachuba libutfo lemphi lewela umsele i-Canal dee Saint-Quentin "bahamba ngenkhungu lekhasa phasi futsi bahlaselwe yimililo yetibhamu netimbayimbayi."
Ekuhambeni kwesikhatsi waphutfumela egceni wekudubula futsi "ngekutimisela nekutetsemba lokukhulu" uchuba libutfo laya embili ngembi kwekutsi aphutfume imbayimbayi ngesandla sinye futsi wadubula ticheme temabutfo lamatsatfu tinamatseli.
Lt Col Vann wabulawa lisotha lelibhacile laseJalimane mhla ti-4 Imphala 1918 - sekusele inyanga yin-nje kutsi imphi iphele.
Michael Vann, lobekaneminyaka lenge-72, watsi tento tamkhulu wakhe "beyintfo lengatiko kutsi bengingeke ngiyimele kepha betiyintfo letfobisananko."
Yena kanye nemnakabo Dkt. James Vann baphindze babeka timbali ngemuva kwepharyidi, lebeyiholwa yi-Brentwood Imperial Youth Band.
Michael Vann watsi "utiva uhloniphekile kutsi adlale indzima kulephareyidi" waphindze futsi wengeta “kuba nesibiindzi lesikhulu ngembi kwengoti kwelichawe sibili kukhonjiswa kwesekelwa lokutawentiwa bantfu labanyenti."

""Peppa ingulube," yebo."

"Ngicabanga kutsi nangicabanga kuphindze futsi kudlalwe, ngicabanga kutsi loko mahlawumbe kungasebenta," kwasho Coker.
"Kepha lapho yinsimni ye-6 ekuseni ngeLisontfo futsi angeke sikwati kusebenta kute kube Lisontfo ngesikhatsi setfu, nguMsombuluko ngekwesikhatsi sabo.
Kepha sisetukwako siyakulungisa.
Ngikholwe, ngesikhatsi bantjintja bekunematheksthi lamanyenti labekaya emuva nasembili labekangasimahle.
Besetama kukulugisa, besicabanga kutsi bekumane kusihibe setebucwepheshe.
Kepha bekungasiso, bekuludzaba lwahulumende.
Ngiyakwetsembisa kutsi esikhatsini lesitako angeke kwenteke.
Sitakugcina kube tikhatsi tekulwa lesihlanu esikhundleni kwalasitfupha - njengobe sivamise kwenta -futsi setamile kwetfulela balandzeli ngalokwendlulele futsi sase siyagabadzela.
Simo lesilishwa."
I-Desert Island Discs: Tom Daley wativa angasilutfo ngetenkholleo yetebulili
Inlambi yete-Olympic Tom Daley utsi wakhula ativa angasilutfo kuwonkhe wonkhe ngenca yetebulili bakhe - kepha loko kwamkhutsata kutsi abe ngulophumelelako.
Lona loneminyaka lenge-24budzala watsi akatange abone kwate kwaba ngulapho asayofundza esikolweni emabanga laphakeme kutsi akutsi"akusiye wonkhe umuntfu lofanana naye."
Akhuluma emsakatweni wemoya i-Radio 4 Desert Island Discs leholwa nguLauren Laverne, wakhula ngemalungelo ebantfu labageyi kute kutsi anike labanye bantfu "litsemba."
Utsi futsi kuba ngumtali kwakhe kwamenta kutsi angakunaki kakhulu kuwina ema-Olympics.
Umsakati lowetayelekile wshowi lekukudzala ikhona, Kirsty Young, asatsatsa likhefu letiyanga letinyenti ngenca yekugula.
Avela njengalokhishwe inumbatana eluhlelweni lwekucala lwaLaverne, Daleywatsi wativa "amncane" kuwonkhe muntfu ngesikhatsi akhula ngobe "bekungemukeleki ngekwetenhlalo kutsandza bafana nemantfombatana."
Kwasho yena: "Kute kube ngulamuhla, leyo miva yekutiva amncane kunalabanye, nekutiva ehlukile, bekutintfo letifundvwako letinginike emandla nemfutfo wekutsi ngikwati kuphumelela."
Bekafuna kukhombisa kutsi "ulutfo," kwasho yena, kute kutsi angajabhisi wonkhemuntfu nabatfola ngebulili bakhe ekugcineni.
Lomwini lotfole emamedali e-bronze e-Olympic emahlandla lamabili sewube ngumkhankhasi lomkhulu we-LGBT waphindze futsi wasebentisa kuvela kwakhe Emidlalweni ye-Commonwealth e-Australia kucela emave lamanyenti kutsi ayekele kwenta kutandza kwebantfu bebulili lobufananako kutsi kube licala.
autsi wakhuluma ngoba bekativa anenhlanhla yekukhona kuphela ngalokukhululekile ngaphadle kwekukhulunywa kabi futsi bekafuna kunika labanye "litsemba."
Loshampeni wemhlaba lowawina emahlanlda lamatsatfu watsi kutsandzana nendvodza - somafilimu waseMelika Dustin Lance Black,lahlangana naye nga-2013 - "kwangimangalisa."
Daley sashada lomwini we-Oscar, lomdzala kunaye ngeminyaka lenge-20, kulomnyaka lophelile kepha utsite ligebe lemnyaka yebudzala alisiyo inkinga.
"Nawuhlangana netintfo letinyenti usesemncane kangaka" - waya kuma-Olympic akhe ekucala aneminyaka le-14 budzala futsi babe wakhe wabulawa sifo samdlavuta iminyaka lemitsatfu ngemuva kwaloko - watsi kumatima kutfol aumuntfu weminyaka lelingana neyakhe lohlangabetene netinkinga letifananako.
Laba labashadene baba batali ngeNhlaba, endvodzaneni yabo ligama layo lekunguRobert Ray Black-Daley, futsi Daley watsi "yonkhe indlela bekabuka ngayo tintfo" intjintjile.
"Kube bewubute kulomnyaka lophelile, konkhe bekumayelana nekutsi 'ngifuna kuwina imedali yeligolide'," kwasho yena.
"Uyati kutsini, kunetintfo letinkhulu kunemamedali eligolide le-Olympic.
Imedali yami yeligolide ye-Olympic nguRobbie."
Indvodzana yakhe ineligama lelifananako nelababe wakhe Robert, lowashona nga-2011 aneminyaka lenge-40 ngemuva kwekuhlolwa atfolakale anesifo samdlavuta.
Daley utsi uyise akazange akwemukele kutsi utwufa futsi yiny eyetintfo laticela kutsi nangabe banemathikithi ekuya elandani nga-2012 - ngoba bekafuna kuba semgceni wekucala.
"Angikhona kumtjela kutsi angeke ube khona kute uhlale emgceni longembili babe'," kwasho yena.
"Bengibambe sandla ngesikhatsi aphefumula kwekugcina futsi kwaba ngulapha ayekela kuphefumula futsi abesafile ngesikhatsi ngibona kutsi bekanemandla kakhulu kutsi angehluleka," kwaso yena.
Emnyakeni lolandzelako Daley wacudzelana kuma-Olympic anga-2012 futsi wawina i-bronze.
"Ngavele ngati-nje kutsi loku ngiko lebengiphupha ngako yonkhe iminyaka yekuphila kwami - kuntjweza ngembi kwetihlwele tasekhaya kuMidlalo yema-Olympic, bekute kutiva lokuncono kunaloko," kwasho yena.
Kwaphindze futsi kwashisekelisa likhetselo lebgoma yakhe yekucala - Ligcabho lehlatjela nguHeather Small - lebeyiloku ayiva ngekhatsi kwakhe ngemalungiselelo ema-Olympics futsi beyiloku imenta avele ematfutfumba.
I-Desert Island Discs ku-BBC Radio 4 ngeLisontfo nga-11:15 BST.
Mickelson lophumile endleleni lolunganiswa ne-Ryder Cup Saturday
Phil Mickelson waseMelika ucophe umlandvo ngeLisontfo ngesikhatsi adlala umdlalo wakhe webhola we-47 weNdzebe yeRyder, kepha kutaudzingeka kutsi antjintje indlela yakhe kute agweme kutsi ib eligcatsi lelingajabulisi.
Mickelson, adlala emkhosini webhiyenali welirekhodi lelihlandla le-12, wabekwa ebhentjini ngubuteni Jim Furyk wabekela emabhola lamane nalokunye lokune ngeMgcibelo.
Esikhundleni sekuba senkhabeni yemshukumo, njengobe bekahlala enta eMelika, lomwini lomkhulukati lowine emahlandla lasihlanu wehlukanisa lilanga lakhe emkhatsini kwekuba ngumholi lokutsatako kanye nekwenta umdlalo wakhe emkhakheni ngelitsemba lekutfola kutsi yini lemgulisako.
Kute ngisho namunye umchubi locinile losesicongweni semsebenti wakhe, lona loneminyaka lenge-48 budzala akasiye lofanele i-Le Golf National,lapho khona inhlalayenta lendze yehlulekile.
Futsi nangabe lomsebenti wona ngekwawo awucedzani emandla ngalokwenele, Mickelson, emdlalweni welishumi nemfica wangeLisontfo, utawubuka nashampeni lonembako Lovulekile waseBritain Francesco Molinari, lohlangene naTommy Fleetwood kuwina yonkhe imidlalo yomine kuleliviki.
Nangabe bantfu baseMelika, labanemaphuzu lamane labacala umdlalo wesingili lal-12, bacala ngendlela leshisako, umdlalo waMickelson ungakhombisa kubaluleka lokukhulu kakhulu.
Furyk ukhombise kuyetsemba lendvodza, hhayi kutsi kukhona lokunyenti bekangakusho.
"Bekayivisia ngalokuphelele lamuhla indzima bekayidlala, ungibubhudze ngemuva waphindze futsi wangigaca watsi utawube asalungele kusasa," kwaho Furyk
"Utetsemba kakhulu.
UnguLophumelelako futsi ufake lokukhulu kulamacembu esikhatsini lesendlulile, nakuleliviki leli.
Bengingamcabangi kutsi angadlala imidlalo lemibili.
Bengicabanga lokunyenti, kepha-ke nguyona ndlela lekube ngayo futsi nguna ndlela lesicabange kuhamba ngayo.
Ufuna kuba lapha, njengawonkhe muntfu."
Mickelson utawuphasa lirekhodi laNick Faldo emidlaeni lweminyenti yeNdzebe yeRyder ledlalwe ngeLisontfo.
Kungaba sephelo semsebenti weNdzebe yeRyder lengakate yahambisna ngalokuphelele nelizinga lelirekhodi lakhe.
Mickelson utfole emawini la-18, waba nekulahlekelwa lokunge-20 kanye nemahhafu lasikhombisa, nanoma Furyk atsite bukhona bakhe kuletse tintfo letibonakalako kulelicembu.
"Uyahlekisa, uyalutsana, uhlakaniphile, utsandza kwenta emahlaya ngebantfu, futsi ungumuntfu lokahle kuba naye egumbini lelicembu," kwachaza yena.
"Ngicabaga kutsi labadlali labasesebancane bakutfokotele kumeya, nabo, kuleliviki, lebekuyintfo lejabulisako kukubona.
Uniketa imali lenyenti kunekudlala-nje kuphela."
Kabuteni waseYurophu Thomas Bjorn uyati kutsi kuhola embili lokukhulu kungavele-nj ekuphele
Thomas Bjorn, kabuteni waseYurophu, uyati ngalahlangabetana nako kutsi kuhola lokusondzele kumasingili ekugcina eNdzebeni yeRyder kungavele-nje kalula kugucuke kube kabi.
LeDane yacopha umlandvo wayo emdlalweni wanga-1997 eValderrama, lapho khona kabuteni loseceleneni Seve Ballesteros waba meaphuzu lasihlanu labeka ebuhleni nakucatsaniswa nebaseMelika kepha bamane-nje bashaya intsambo ngetimphumulo tabo wawina kancane, batfola-14½-13½.
"Uphele kutikhumbuta kutsi besihola embili eValderrama; besihola embili eBrookline, lapho khona sadliwa, naseValderrama, lapho saphumelela khona, kepha-nje,"kwsho Bjorn, lowatsatfwa sitfombe, ngemuva kwekubuka Liklasi langa-2018 liwina-5-3 ngalesihlanu nayitolo kuhola-10-6 ku-Le Golf National.
Ngako-ke umlandvo utawukhombisa mine kanye nabo bonkhe lalbanye labakulethimu kutsi loku akukapheli.
Utawuhamba ngalokuphelele kusasa.
Phumela lapha ngaphandle wente tonkhe tintfo letifanele.
Loku akukapheli kut ekube ngulapho unemaphuzu ebhodini.
Sinemgomo, futsi loko kwetama kuwina lendzebe, futsi ngulapho-ke sigcile khona.
Bengiloku ngiso njalo kutsi, ngigcile kubadlali laba-12 labaseluhlangotsini lwetfu, kepha siyati kutsi yini lelindze ngakulolu loluny eluhlangotsi - badlali bemhlaba lalbakhulukati."
Ajabuliswe kutsi badlali bakhe badlale kanjani emdlalweni weligaluvu lomatima, kwenteta Bjorn: "Angeke ngitibeke embili kuloku.
Kusasa silwane lesehlukile.
Kusasa ngumdlalo wangamunye lotile, futsi loko-ke yintfo leyehlukile leyentiwako.
Kuyintfu lenkhulu kuba lapho ukanye nemlingani nangabe tintfo tihamba kahle, kepha nangabe ulapha wedvwana, likhono lakho-ke njengemdlali weligaluvu lehlolwa ngalokuphelele.
Loyo-ke ngumlayeto lofanele kutsi uwunike badlali, kutsi khipha onkhe emandla akho kusasa.
manje, ushiya umlingani wakhe ngemuva futsi ufanele kutsi ahambe ayotfola lokuhle kakhulu langatitfolela kona, futsi."
Ngalokufananako kuBjorn, inombolo lebukene naloko Jim Furyk utawuba afuna badlali bakhe kutsi badlale kancono ngamunye kunangesikhatsi babalingani, labakhetsekile nguJordan Spieth naJustin Thomas, labatfola emaphuzu lamatsatfu kulamane.
Furyk yena ngekwakhe bekasekupheleni kwetinhlangotsi totimbili talelo langa lelikhulu lekugcina, bekaloku ayincenye thelicembu leliphumelelako eBrookline ngembi kwekutsi agcine asehluleki lapho Iyurophu yaveta "Umlingo eMedinah."
"Ngikhumbula onkhe emagama ako lalibele," washo aphendvula ngesikhatsi abutwa kutsi Ben Crenshaw, kabuteni wanga-1999, wabakhutsata kanjani badlali bakhe nasekuyiwa ngaselangeni lekugcina.
"Kusasa sinemidlalo le-12 lebalulekile, kepha ungatsandza kucala masinyane njnegobe ubonile eBrookline, njnegobe ubonile eMedinah.
nasekuchutjekwa ngemandla ngendlela yinye, kuba nekucindzeteleka kumidlalo lesemkhatsini.
Sihlelembimbisa bafana betfu ngendlela lefanele futsi ngendlela lesibona ngayo, uyati setama kwenta umlingo kusasa."
Thomas unikwe umsebenti wekwetama kuhola kulwa futsi ubukene Rory McIlroy emdlalweni lomkhulu, naPaul Casey, Justin Rose, Jon Rahm, Tommy Fleetwood na-Ian Poulter laba labanye bantfu baseYurophu emlenteni lophakeme weluhlelo.
"Ngahamba nelicembu lalabafana ngalendlela lena ngoba ngicabanga kutsi ifanele konhe kute kuyofika ekugcineni," kwasho Bjorn welikhetselo lakhe lemasingili.
Umkhumbi lomusha wemphi waseJalimane uphindze futsi wahlehlisa
Imikhumbi lemisha yemphi yaseLwandle lenetikhali letehlukene yasJalimane beyifanele kutsi ikhishwe nga-2014 ingene esikhundleni semikhumbi legugile yeteMphi Yekushayisana Ngemoya Lobandzako, kepha angeke ibe lapho kute lokunani kube ngumnyaka lotako ngencha yetinchubo letingasebenti kahle netindleko letinkhulu, kwabik abetindzaba bendzawo.
Kukhishwa kwe"Rheinland-Pfalz," umkhumbi lohola embili lomusha weBaden-Wuerttemberg lenetikhali letihlanganisiwe, manje sewuhlehlisiwe kute kube sehhafini ya-2019, ngekuya kweliphephandzaba i-Die Zeit icaphuna umuntfu wetemphi.
Lomkhumbi bewufanele kutsi ngabe wajoyina leMphi yaselwandle nga-2014, kepha kwetfulwa kwakamuva kwabanga tinkinga kulomdlandla walomklamo.
Lemikhumbi lemine lesembili yeBaden-Wuerttemberg leyafunwa yiMphi yaseLwandle nga-2007 itawuta itotsatsa sikhundla semikhumbi legugile i-Bremen.
Kuvisisa kutsi batawufaka ikhanoni lenemandla kakhulu,imicibisholo leminyenti lelwa netinsizamshini nemikhumbi kanye netebucwepheshe lobushayela phansi, njengekunciphisa irada, tinkhomba tekukhanya lokubovu netemsindvo.
Letinye timphawu letibalulekile tifaka ekhatsi tikhatsi letindze tekulungisa - kufanele kutsi kukhoneke kukhipha lemikhumbu lemisha lenetikhali letihlangene iminyaka lemibile ingekho elugwini lwasekhaya.
Nanoma kunjalo, kwephuta lokuchubeka njalo kusho kutsi imikhumbi leyincalakuvela yemphi - kutsi yavumela Ijalimane kutsi ikhombise emandla emaveni langesheya kwetilwandle - itawube seyvele iphelelwe sikhatsi uma icala kusebenta, kwasho Die Zeit.
Umkhumbi wemphi lonetihali letihlananisiwe i-F125 icophe umlandvo kulomnyaka lophelile, ngesikhatsi Imphi yaseLwandle yaseGerman yala ngalokusemtsetfweni kukhipha lomkhumbi futsi yawubuyisela emuva emabaleni emikhumbi eBlohm naseVoss eHamburg.
Loku bekukwekucala kutsi Imphi yaseLwandle ibuyisele umkhumbi emuva kumakhi ngemuva sewetfuliwe.
Imbangela yaloko ayatiwa, kepha betindzaba basejalimane bakhomba lokunyenti lokungalungi "ngesakhiwo sangekhatsi nesakhiwo sangaphandle" lebekwenta lomkhumbi wemphi ube yintfo lengasebenti nangabe ungakhishwa uyolwa.
Kungeneli kwe-software bekubaluleke kakhulu ngobe imikhumbi i-Baden-Wuerttemberg itawuchutjwa libutfo lebachubi labange-120 - ihhafu yebantfu labasemkhumbini lomdzala i-Bremen.
Lokunye futsi, kwavela kutsi lomkhumbi bewunesisindvo lesikhulu kakhulu kuna leso lesilindzelekile llebekunciphisa likhono letemphi yaselwandle kutsi bawufake letinye tintfo letiwuphuculako.
"Le-Rheinland-Pfalz" lebeyingemathani la-7, 000 lekukholelwa kutsi beyesindza ngalokuphindzeke kabili kunemkhumbi lofana nayo lebewusetjentiswa ngeMajalimane eMphini Yemhlaba yesibili.
Ngaphandle kwesakhiwo sangaphandle lesingasebenti kahle,sigcebhezana sentsengo yawo wonkhe lomklamo -kufaka ekhatsi kuceceshwa kwelibutfo - nako sekuba yinkinga.
Kutsiwa yafika kutigidzigidzi leti- €3.1 ku- ($3.6bn) - kusuka kuyekucala tigidizgidzi leti- €2.2.
Tinkinga letihlasele lemikhumbi lemisha tiba nguletibalulekile ikakhulu njengobe kube netecwayiso tekutsi emandla etemphi yaselwandle yeJalimane ayehla.
Ekucaleni kwalomnyaka, Hans-Peter Bartels, sikhulu selikomidi letekuvikela lephalamende yaseJalimane, ukwemukele kutsi ecinisweni Temphi yaseLwandle "tiphelelwa yimikhumbi lengiyo lengakhishwa iyosebenta etindzaweni letitsite."
Lesikhulu sitsite lenkinga beyiloku ikhula ngekuhamba kwesikhatsi, ngoba imikhumbi lemidzala ayikhishwanga kepha futsi akutange kufakwe leminye etikhundleni tayo.
Wakhala ngekutsi kute namunye walemkhumbi lemisha ema-Baden-Wuerttemberg yakhona kujoyina Imphi yaseLwandle.
Ithrasti Yavelobkhe ihogela timfihlo temphilo yemalulwane
Lucwaningo lolusha lolwentiwa ku-estate eScottish Highlands luhlose kukhombisa kutsi emalulwane ayisebentisa kanjani indzawo kutingela kudla kwawo.
Kwetsenjwa kutsi loku lokutawutfolwa kutawuniketa lwatiso lolusha mayelana nendlela yekutiphatsa yaletilwane letimunyisako letindizako kanye nekwelekelela kukhombindlela imisebenti yekonga yesikhatsi lesikhatsi letitako.
Lucwaningo lolwentiwa bososayensi kuTrasti Yavelonkhe yeScotland lutawulandzela emalulwane lamadzala emhlaba kanye nemalulwane lansundvu lanetindlebe letindze nemalulwane ema-Daubenton e-Inverewe Gardens eWester Ross.
Kutawufakwa ticophamavi letikhetsekile etindzaweni letibalulekile letitawulandzelela lokwentiwa ngemalulwane kuso sonkhe sikhatsi.
Basebenti base-NHS nemavolontiya nabo batewenta luklayo basebentisa titfungatsi letiphatfwa ngesandla.
Bocwepheshe labahlatiya imisindvo yako konhe lokucoshiwe batawutfola emahlandla ekuchumana kwemalulwane nekutsi nguluphi luhlobo lolwenta loko.
kutawbese kukhishwa libalave lendzawo yekuhlala nembiko kwenta sikalo sendzawo lekhombisa lendlela yekutiphatsa.
Rob Dewar, umeluleki wetekongiswa kwemvelo we-NTS, wetsamba kutsi lemiphumela itawukhombisa ngutiphi tindzawo tekuhlala letibaluleke kakhulu kulamalulwane nekutsi luhlobo ngalunye lutisebentisa kanjani.
Lolwatiso lutawusita kutfola tinzuzo temsebenti wekulawula tindzawo tekuhlala njengekwakha tiganganekutsi tingana tingagcinwa kahle kanjani tigcinelwe emalulwane naletinye tinhlobo tetilwane.
Linani lemalulwane eScotland nase-UK lehle kakhulu kulomnyakalikhulu lowendlulile.
Asekusatjisweni ngenca yemisebenti yekwakha neyentfutfuko letsintsa tindzawo laho ahlangana khona kanye netindzawo tekuhlala.
Imishini yemoya nekukhanyisa nayo ingenta bungoti, njengetitsiyo tetimphungane kanye nemakhemikhali yetintfo tekwakha, kanye nekuhlaselwa ngemakati asendlini.
Ecinisweni emalulwane akasiwo timphumphutse.
Nanoma kunjalo, ngenca yemkhuba wawo wekutingela ebusuku emadlebe awo asebenta kakhulu kunemehlo awo nakuta eludzabeni lwekubamba tinyamatane.
Asebentiswa buciko bemsindvo lobucakile kukhomba tilokatana netihibe endleni letindiza kuyo.
I-NTS, lenguyona inakekela takhiwo tetemlandvo letingetulu kwaletinge-270, tingadze letibalulekile letinge-38 kanye nemahektha la-76,000 emhlaba kulo lonkhe lelive, kutsata emalulwane njengentfo lebalulekile.
Inetingcweti leticeceshiwe letilishumi, letivamise kwenta luklayo, kuhlola tindzawo lahlangana kuto futsi ngalesinye sikhatsi bayawatakula.
IScotland seyidzimate yasungula sichiwi eThreave estate eDumfries nase Galloway, lekulikhaya letinhlobo temalulwane letisiphohlongo taletilishumi aseScotland.
Umphatsi we-estate David Thompson utsi le-estate nguyona ndzawo yato lekahle kakhulu.
"Lapha eThreave sinandzawo lekahle kakhulu yemalulane," kwasho yena.
"Sinetakhiwo letindzala, tigaygayi tetihlahla nato tonkhe tindzawo letikahle.
Kodvwa kunyenti lokumayelana nemalulwane lokungatiwa, ngako-kel lomsbenti lesiwentako lapha nakuleti letinye tindzawo utasisita kutsi sivisise kabanti mayelana naloko lakudzinga kut ekutsi andlondlobale."
Kugcizelela indzaba yekubaluleka kwekuhlolwa kwemalulwane kucala ngembi kwekutsi kulungiswe leto tindzawo ngoba kungenteka kutsi ngekungati kumoshwe indzawo yekutala lekungabulala emalulwane lamasikati langaba nge-400 nebantfwana bawo, lokungabhubhisa cishe onkhe emalulwane lakhona.
Emalulwane avikelekile futsi kuwabulala akukho emtsetfweni, kuwahlukubeta noma kuwaphatamisa noma kubhidlita tindzawo tawolahlangan akuto.
Elisabeth Ferrell, sikhuli saseScotland seThrasti Yekongiwa Kwemalulwane, ukhutsate sive kutsi singene selekelele.
Kwasho yena: "Kusesekunyenti lesifanele kutsi sikufundze ngemalulwane etfu kanye naletinye tinhlotjana kutsi tichuba njani."
Ronaldo uyaticitsa tinslolo tekudlwengula njengobe bameli batsi batawubeka licala liphephandzaba laseJalimane
Cristiano Ronaldo utsi letinsolo tekudlwengula labeka tona "titindzaba letingesiwo emaciniso," utsi bantfu "bafuna kutiphakamisa" ngekusebentisa ligama lakhe.
Bameli bakhe batawumangalela liphephandza laseJalimane i-Der Spiegel,lelashicilela letinsolo.
LomPutukesi nemJuventus ibekwa licala lekudlwengula make waseMelika, ligama lekhe lekunguKathryn Mayorga, ehhotela eLas Vegas ekamelweni lelingunombolo-2009.
Kutsiwa umkhokhele-$375,000 kumvala umlomo kutsi angakhulumi ngalesihlakalo, kubike i-Der Spiegel ngaLesihlanu.
Akhuluma Bukhoma kuvidiyo ye-Instagram kubalandzeli bakhe labatigidzi leti-142 ngemuva kwekubikwa kwaletinsolo, Ronaldo, loneminyaka lenge-33 budzala, utsite lemibiko "itindzaba letingesiwo emaciniso."
"Cha, cha, cha, cha , cha.
Labakusho lamuhla, tindzaba letingesiwo emaciniso," kwasho Umwini wemahlandla lasihlanu kukhamera.
"Bafuna kutiphakamisa ngekusebentisa ligama lami.
Kwetayelekile.
bafuna kuba ngulabadvumile ngekusho ligama lami, kepha kuyincenye yemsebenti.
Ngiyindvodza lejabulile futsi konkhe kukahle," kwengeta lomdlali, amamatseka.
Bameli baRonaldo balunhgiselela kumangelela i-Der Spiegel mayelana naletinsolo, labakubite ngekutsi "kubika lokungeke kusetjentiswe njengebufakazi enkantolo lokusolwako kutangasese," ngekuya kweReuters.
Ummeli Christian Schertz utsite lomdlali utawufuna sincemphetelo "sekulinyatwa kwesitfunti sakhe lesilingana linani lebukhulu balokulinyatwa, lokunguyinye yetintfo letinkhulu kakhulu yekwephulwa kwelilungelo lebusense bemuntfu kuleminyaka."
Lesehlakalo lekutsiwa seneteka kutsi senteka ngeNhlaba 2009 ekamelweni eHhotela i-Palms neKhasino eLas Vegas.
Ngemuva kwekuhlangana eklabhini yasebusuku, Ronaldo naMayorga kutsiwa babuyela ekamelweni lalomdlali, lapho-ke amdlwengula khona amngena ngemuva emdzidzidzini, ngekuya kwemaphepha lafakwe eNkantolo yeSifundzai saseClark eNevada.
Mayorga utsi Ronaldo waguca ngemadvolo ngemuva kwalesehlakalo wamtjela kutsi ‘’ungumuntfu lotiphetse kahle’’ "ngemaphesenti lange-99" lowentelwa phasi "nguleliphesenti linye."
Lamadokhumenti atsi Ronaldo wacinisekisa kutsi laba lababili bayile emacansini, kepha loko kube sivumelwano.
Mayorga utsi waphindze futsi waya emaphoyiseni washuthwa titfombe talokulima kwakhe esibhedlela, kepha ngemuva kwesikhatsi wavuma kutsi loludzaba lusonjululwe ngaphandle kwenkantolo ngoba "bekesaba kutiphindzisela" futsi bekakhatsatekile "ngekungcunuleka emmangweni."
Lona loneminyaka lenge-34budzala utsi manje sewufuna kusigucula lesisombululo ngabe uyachubeka nekukhahlabeteka emoyeni mayelana nalesehlakalo.
Ronaldo bekasadvute nekujoyina licembu leReal Madrid esuka kuManchester United ngalesikhatsi saletinsolo tekulimata, futsi kulelihlobo ujoyine tichwaga tase-Ithali iJuve ngesivumelwane setigidzi leti-€100.
Brexit: I-UK itawuhlala itisola ngekulahlekwa bomakhi betimoto
I-UK "itawuhlala njalo itisola" nayingalahlekelwa lizinga layo lekuba ngumholi ekwakhiweni kwetimoto ngemuva kweBrexit, kwasho Mabhalane weTebhizinisi Greg Clark.
Wangena watsi "kuyakhatsatana" kutsi i-Toyota UK itjele i-BBC iBritain iphumile ku-EU ngaphandle kwedili itawumisa kwesikhashana imikhicto efekthri yayo eBurnaston, dvute neDerby.
"Sidzinga idili," kwasho Mnu. Clark.
Bomakhi betimoto baseJapan batsite lifutse lekwephuma eminyeleni nakwenteka kubabete idili neBrexit kungabangela kulahleka kwemisebenti.
Sakhiiti saseBurnaston - lesenta ema-Toyota Aurisnema-Avensis - sikhicite cishe timoto leti-150,000 kulomnyaka lophelile lapho khona-90% tatfunyelwa kuyo yonkhe INhlangano Yebunye BeYurophu.
"Imibono yami kutsi nangabe iBritain iyaphuma ku-EU ekupheleni kweNdlovulenkhulu sitawubon aumkhicito uma efekthri yetfu," kwasho Marvin Cooke, umphatsimcondzisi weToyota eBurnaston.
Labanye bakhiciti betimo base-UK bakhombisa kwesaba kwabo mayelana nekuphuma ku-EU ngaphdnle kwesivumelwane mayelana nekutsi luhwebelwano lwangaphandle kweminyele lutawusebenta kanjani, kufaka ekhatsi i-Honda, BMW neJaguar Land Rover.
I-BMW, sibonelo, itsi itawvala Sikhiciti sayo lesincanelant e-Oxford inyanga yinye ngemuva kweBrexit.
Kukhatsateka lokukhulu lokuphatselene naloku lokushiwo bakhiciti betimoto bungoti bekutsenga nakungenteka kubete sivumelwano seBrexit.
Kukhicita kweToyota kuyachubeka "ngesikhatsi lesifanele", futsi emaphatsi afika njalo ngemamitsi lange-37 avela kubatfulitinsita kukokubili i-UK neEU etimoto letentelwe kutsi ti-odwe.
Nangabe i-UK iyaphuma ku-EU ngaphandle kwesivumelwane mhla tinge-29 Indlovulenkhulu, kungenteka kube nekutsikameteka emnyeleni lapho khona imboni itsi kungaholela ekubalelekeni kwekufika kanye nekushoda kwemaphatsi.
Angeke kukhonakale kutsi iToyota ingema ngetulu kwelilanga linye neluhlu lolubalulekile esikhicitini sayo seDerbyshire, kwasho lenkampani, futsi kute kukhicita lokutawumiswa.
Mnu. Clark utsite isu laTheresa May Chequers letibudlwane bakusasa ne-EU "kwentelwa kutsi kugwemeke kuhlolwa emnyeleni."
"Sidzinga kutsi sibe nesivumelwano. Sifuna kuba nesivumelwane lesikahle kakhulu lesitawuvumela njnegobe ngisho-nje hhayi kuphela imphumelelo lekhona kwamanje kutsi ijatjulelwe kepha kitsi kutsi sibambe lelitfuba," watjela i-BBC Radio 4's eluhlelweni lwaNamuhla.
"Bufakazi hhayi-nje kuphela lobuvela kaToyota kepha nakulabanye bakhiciti kutsi sidzinga kutsi sikwati kuchubeka naloko lokuphumelele kakhulu lokuhlelwe yinchibo yekutsenga."
IToyota ayikhonanga kusho kutsi kukhicita kutawumiswa sikhatsi lesingakanani, kepha esikhatsini lesidze, yacaphelisa ngekutsi tindleko letengetiwe titawunciphisa kucudzelana futsi ekugcineni klahleke nemisebenti.
Peter Tsouvallaris, losebente eBurnaston iminyaka lenge-24 futsi ngulobita imihlagano yeNhlangano Lehlanganisako kusikhiciti, utsite emalunga akhe akhatsateke kakhulu: "Ngekwati kwami lemisebenti lena ingahamba ayiphindzi futsi ibuye.
Kwasho lokhulumela hulumende: "Sibeke lisu lelingilo futsi lelimangalisako lebudlelwane betfu besikhatsi lesitako ne-EU."
Umhlangano waTrump naRosenstein kungenteka futsi ubambelele, kwasho i-White House
Umhlangano waDonald Trump wetintfo lesengotini nelisekelammeli jikelele Rod Rosenstein "ungashicilelwa emuva ngalelinye liviki" lapho kuchubeka kulwela umnyulwa weNkantolo Lephakeme Brett Kavanaugh, kwasho i-White House nhgeLisontfo.
Rosenstein ubukene nemsebenti wemkhandlu lokhetsekile Robert Mueller, luphenya ngekufaka lunyawo lwengulube elukhetfweni lwaseRussia, emalinki emkhatsini waTrump abekwe eceleni bese kutsi iRussia nekuvimbeka lokungaba khona kwetebulungiswa ngumengameli.
Noma Trump uyamcosha noma akamscoshi lommeli jikelele, futsi ngaleyo ufaka engotini kutimela kwaMueller, sikubhebhetsekisa inhlebo yeWashington inyanga yonkhe.
Ekucaleni kwalenyanga, iNew York Times ibike kutsi Rosenstein ukhulume ngekufaka luhwayela kute acophe inkhulumo yarump kanye nekwenteka kususa mengameli ngesichibelo se-25.
Rosenstein uwuphikile lombiko.
Kepha ngeMsombuluko lwendlulile i-White House, nanoma kunemibiko bekasadvuute nekwesula esikhundleni.
Esikhundleni saloko, umhlangao naTrump, lobekakaMhlabuhlangene eNew York, kwamenyekela ngLesine.
Trump utsite "unconota" kungamcoshi Rosenstein kepha-ke umhlangano wabambeleleka kugwema kungcubutana likomidi lebasekeli belijaji leTimphunga kuva kutsi Kavanaugh nalomunye wabomake labamsolo ngekutiphatsa kabi ngekwemacansi, Dkt. Christine Blasey Ford, bobabili betfule bufakazi.
NgaLesihlanu, Trump ukhiphe umyalo weluphenyo lweliviki lwe-FBI mayelana naKavanaugh, lokubambelele ngalokuchubekako kuvota lokuphelele kweTimphunga.
Mabhala waTrump webetindzaba, Sarah Sanders, uvele kuFox News ngeLisontfo.
Abutwa mayelana nemhlangano waRosenstein, watsi: "Lusuku lwaloko lusengakabekwa, ngiyabona kutsi kuhlehlisa ngalelinye liviki nakubukwa tonkhe letintfo letinye letichubekako enkantolo lephakeme.
Kepha-ke sitawubona futsi siyatsandza kuhlala satisa betindzaba."
Labanye babiki batawuphikisana ngaloko: Sanders akate asebe nemhlangao webetindzaba we-White Housekusukela ngeNyoni mhla ti-10.
Host Chris Wallace wabuta kutsi kungani kunjalo.
Sanderswatsi kungabi khona kwemihlangano lemincane kungenca yekungatsandzi babiki be-TV "kutiphakamisa," nanoma-nje atsi: "Angikuvumi kutsi bayatiphakamisa."
Wabese ubeka umbono wekutsi kuchumana-ngco emkhatsini waTrumpnebetindzaba kutawukhula.
"Mengameli unemaseshini lamanyenti eMibuto Netimphendvulo kunabo bonkhe bomengameli baphambilini," utsite, engeta ngaphdnle kwekuniketa bufakazi: "Siwabukile lawo manani."
Tinkhulumo tekwatisa tisatawentiwa, kwasho Sanders, kepha "nangabe betindzaba banelitfuba lekubuta mengameli waseMelika-ngco imibuto, loko kuncono kakhulu kunekukhuluma.
Setama kwenta loko kakhulu futsi nisibonile senta njalo kakhulu kulamaviki lambalwa lendlulile fusi loko kusatawenta etinkhulumeni tekwatisa tebetindzaba lapho nitawukhuluma namengameli waseMelika."
Trump uvamise kuphendvula imibuto nakesuka e-White House noma ahlanganyele kumaseshini lavulekile noma kunkhomfa yebetindzaba lenalabakhulu labavakashile.
Tinkhomfa tebentindzaba tamunye tiyindlala.
ENew York kuleliviki mengameli mhlawumbe ukhombise kutsi kungani, kuvelenje uchamuke kubetindzaba bangakakulindzeli.
Mabhalane weTemphilo ubhalela basebenti be-EU eNHS Scotland mayelana nekwesaba iBrexit
Mabhalane weTemphilo ubhalele basebenti be-EU labasebenta kubetindzaba beNHS yaeScotland kuvakalisa kubonga kwalelive nekubafisela kutsi bahlale kuloku bekukadz kuyiBrexit.
Jeane Freeman MSP watfumela incwadzi sekusele tinyanga letisitfupha kutsi i-UK iphume ku-EU.
Hulmende waseScotland sweuvele itinikele kuhlangabetgana netindleko tekufaka ticelo tekuhlala tetakhamuti te-EU letisebenta kutetinsita tahulumende lobhidlitiwe.
Ekugcineni, Mk. Freeman wabhala watsi: "Kulelihlobo, tinkhulumswano emkhatsini we-UK ne-EU mayelana nekuphuma tiyachubeka, ticondze esincumeni lesilindzelekile kulelikwindla.
Kepha ne-UK nayo iloku itilungiselela kancono yentela kutsi umanga ngab ekuyenteka kubabete sivumelwane.
Ngitayi kutsi lesi sikhatsi sekungatintiseki kini nonkhe.
Kungako-ke bengifuna kugcizelela manje kutsi ngilitfokotela kangakanani ligalelo lawonkhewonkhe lolilunga lebasebenti, ngekungakhatsali ngebuve babo.
Balingani ngekwemsebenti lenivela ku-EU,nekwendlul alapho, nita nesipiliyoni nemakhono labalulekile lacinisa aphuindze futsi ente kancono umsebenti wetemphilo, futsi lokuzuzisa tingulane nemmango lesiwusebnetelako.
IScotland likhaya lenu ngalokuphelele futsi siyavuna kakhulu kutsi nihlale."
Christion Abercrombie Uhlindvwa Ngalokuphutfumako Ngemuva Kwekulimala Enhloko
Tennessee State Tigers linebacker Christion Abercrombie uhlindvwe ngalokuphutfumako ngemuva kwekulima enhloko ngeMgcibelo ngemuva kwekwehlula nga-31-27 i-Vanderbilt Commodores, kwabika Mike Organ waseTennesse.
Umceceshi lomkhulu weTennessee State Rod Reed utjele tintsatseli kutsi lokulimala kwenteke masinyane -nje kungapheli ihhafu yesiwombe.
"Ute uceleni wavele wadzimuleka phasi khona lapho," kwasho Reed.
Baceceshi kanye netemphilo banike Aercrombie umoyamphilo khona lapho emaceleni ngembi kwekutsi bamfake eluhlakeni baphidze futsi bamahambisa kute kutsi ahlolwe.
Sikhulu saseTennessee State sitjele Chris Harris wase- WSMV eNashville, Tennessee,kutsi Abercrombie bekasacedzile kuhlindvwa eVanderbilt Medical Center.
Harris wengete ngekutsi kusete "imininingwane mayelana neluhlobo/bubanti balokulimala" kwanyalo futsi iTennessee State isetama kutfola kutsi lokulimala kwenteke nini.
Abercrombie, losesesigabeni lesiphasi, ukusizini yakhe yekucala eTennessee State ngemuva kwekuphuma ku-Illinois.
Ube nesamba sekuhlasela lesisihlanu ngeMgcibelo ngembi kwekuphuma kulomdlalo, lokufake kusizini yakhe kuhlasela loku-18.
batsengi bakulamanye emave batawukhokhiswa umtselo wesitembu nangabe batsenga tindlu e-UK
Batsengi bakulamanye emave batawukhokhiswa umtselo lonkhulu wesitembu nangabe batsenga tindlu e-UK bese kutsi imali lengukheshi leyengetekile isetjentiselwa basita labo labete emakhaya ngaphasi kwelisu lelisha leTory
Loku kutawusita kwehlisa lizinga lekushuba lemphumelelo yemkhankhaso waCorbyn wekuheha bavoti labasesebasha
Lokukhuphuka kwemtselo wesitembu utawukhokhiswa labo labangakhokhi umtselo e-UK
Temafa tilindzele kukhula kwawo kufike kutigidzi leti-£120 ngemnyaka kute kusitwe labo labete emakhaya
Batsengi bakulamanye emave batawukhokhisa umtselo wesitembu lomkhulu nabatsenga tindlu e-UK - bese kutsi imali lengukheshi leyengetiwe isetjentiselwa kusita labo labete emakhaya, Theresa May utawumemetela loku lamuhla.
Lesento lesi sitawubekeka njengemitama yekwehlisa lizing alekushuba lemphumelelo yemkhankhaso waCorbyn wekuheha bavoti labasesebasha ngekufunga kutsi kutawuniketwa tindlu letinyenti letingabiti kakhulu futsi kuhloswe labo labahola kakhulu.
Lomtselo wesitembu utawukhokhiswa bantfu kanye nemafemu langatseli e-UK, bese kutsi imali lengukheshi leyengetiwe itawufukula umkhankhaso waHulumende wekulwa nekungalali kahle.
Lomtselo lowengetiwe - lowengetwa kulona lokhona wesitembu, kufaka ekhatsi emazinga laphakeme langeniswe eminyakeni lemibili leyendlulile emakhaya esibili kanye nekutsengela kucashisa - kungaba ngemaphesenti lamatsatfu.
Temafa tilindzele kutsi lesento sitfole tigidzi leti-£120 ngemnyaka.
Njengoba kulinganiselwe emaphesenti la-13 ekwakhiwa lokusha kwemakhaya aseLondon atsengwa bahlali base-UK, lokukhuphula tintsengo bese kwenta kutsi kube matima kutsenga kulabo labatsenga kwekucala kute tsatfol etindlu.
Tindzawo letinyenti talelive letinjingile - ikakhulu edolobheni lelikhulu - "atisenamuntfu" ngenca yelinani lelikhulu lebatsengi bakulamanye emave labahlala sikhatsi sabo lesinyenti bangaphandle kwalelive.
Lenchubomgomo lensha ivela-nje ngemuva kwemavikana Boris Johnson amemetele sabele semtselo wesitembu kusita bantfu labasha kutsi babe nemakhaya.
Usole emafemu lamakhulu etekwakha ngekukhulisa tintsengo tetindlu ngekutsatsa umhlaba kodvwa angawusebentisi, waphindze futsi wacela Nkkt. May kutsi ayekele ema-quotas emakhaya latsengekako kut ekutsi kulungiswe “lihlazo letindlu” laseBritain.
Mnu. Corbyn umemetele luchugechunge loluhle loluhlongotwako lwekulungiswa kwetindlu, kufaka ekhatsi kulawulwa kwerenti kanye nekucedza kukhishwa kwebantfu etindzaweni ngendluzula "ngaphandle kweliphutsa".
Ufuna futsi kunika imikhandlu emandla lamakhulu ekwakha emakhaya.
Nkkt. May utsite: "Kulomnyaka lophelile ngitsite ngitawusebentisa bundvunankhulu bami bekubuyisela liphupho laseBritish esimeni salo - kitsi imphilo ifanele kutsi ibe ncono kusitukulwane lesisha ngasinye.
Futsi loko kusho kulungisa imkethe yetfu ylengasikahle yetindlu.
IBritain itawuhlala ivulekele bantfu labafuna kuphila, kusebenta kanye nekwakha imphilo lapha.
Nanoma kunjalo, akusiyo intfo lekahle kutsi kulula kulabanye bantfu labangahlali lapha e-UK, kanye nakutinkampani takulamanye emave, kutsi batsenge emakhaya njengebahlali labasebenta ngekutikhandla.
Kubantfu labanyenti liphupho lekuba nemakhaya selibe yintfo lekhashane nabo, futsi nekungcunuleka setfunti ngenca yekungalali kahle yintfo lekhona mbamba."
Jack Ross: Tikhwepha tami tekugcina kutsi ngilawule iScotland'
Sunderland boss Jack Ross utsi "tikhwepha tekugcina" kutsi abe ngumphatsi weScotland esigabei lesitsite.
Scot, 42, ulangatelela insayeya yekuvusetela iklabhu North-East, lekwamanje ihleti endzaweni yesitsatfu yeLeague One, emaphuzu lamatsatfu etulu.
Waya eNkhundleni Yetemdlalo yeKukhanya kulelihlobo ngemuva kwekukhombindlela i-St Mirren wabuyela kuScottish Premiership kulesizini lephelile.
"Bengifuna kudalela live lakitsi njengemdlali.
Ngatfola B futsi ngiko loko," Ross watjela i-BBC Scotland's Sportsound.
"Kepha ngakhula ngibukela kakhulu iScotland eHampden ngikanye nababe wami ngesikhatsi ngisesemncane, futsi kutintfo lbeyisolo iloku ingibuyesela emuva.
Lelo tfuba litawufika kuphela, nangabe, ngiyaphumelela ekulawuleni leklabhu."
Bahambiphambili lababaphatsi beSunderland bafaka ekhatsi Dick Advocaat, David Moyes, Sam Allardyce, Martin O'Neill, Roy Keane, Gus Poyet naPaulo Di Canio.
Loyo bekangumphatsi we-Alloa Athletic bekangesabi kulandzela lamagama lamakhulu kuleklabhu lenkhulu, ngemuva kwekwala tingeniso talokukhulu letivela eBarnsley naseDolobheni i-Ipswich.
"Imphumelelo kimi itawukalwa kutsi 'ngingayibuyisela yini leklabhu kuPremier League?'
Ngenca yesakhiwo netisetjentiswa letikuleklabhu lena, akungabateki kutsi ngeyePremier League," kwasho yena.
"Akusiwo umsebenti lolula kufika lapho, kepha ngitawubona kutsi ngiyaphumelela lapha uma ngingakhona kubiyisela leklabhu lapho."
Ross uneminyaka lemitsatfu akulomsebenti wakhe, ngemuva kwesihatsi sekuba ngumsiti wemphatsi eDumbarton kanye netinyanga leti-15 tekucecesha basebenti be-Hearts.
Wabese usita i-Alloa kutsi ivuke ekubeni semlenteni wesitsatfu, waphindze wantjintja i-St Mirren ekubeni semngcengcemeni welizinga leliphasi lekuwina kuba nguShampeni kusizini lelandzelako.
Futsi Ross utsi utiva ukhululeke kakhulu manje ngendlela langakate asakhululeke ngayo phambilini emsebentini wakhe wekuba ngumdlali eClyde, Hartlepool, Falkirk, St Mirren naseHamilton Academical.
"Bekusemphambanandlela mbamba,"washo akhumbula, nangitsandza tindzambo tekuhola i-Alloa.
"Bengikholelwa mbamba ekutsini kuphatsa bekuyintfo lengifanele, kakhulu kunekudlala.
Kuvakala sengatsi yintfo lemangalisako ngoba ngenta kahle, ngatiphilisa kahle ngako, futsi ngatfokotela netintfo letisezingeni leliphakeme.
Kodvwa kudlala kungaba yintfo lematima.
Kunetintfo letinyenti lewufanele kutsi wendlule kuto njalo ngelivi.
Namanje ngisendlula kuloko mayelana nekucindzeteleka nencindzetelo yemsebenti kodvwa kuphatsa kuvakala kuyintfo elkahle.
Bengihlala njalo ngifuna kuphatsa futsi manje sengiphetse, kuvakala kuyintfo lengenta ngikhululeke ngalendlela lengingiyo yonkhe imphilo yami yebudzala."
Ungalalela ingcoco lephelele ku-Sportsound ngeLisontfo, mhla tinge-30 Inyoni, ku-Radio Scotland emkhatsini wensimbi ye12:00 emini neye-13:00 BST ntsambama
Sikhatsi lesikahle kakhulu seliphayindzi yinsimbi ye-5.30 ntsambama ngeMgcibelo, luklayo lutfole kanjalo
Ligagasi lekushisa kwasehlobo likhuphule lizinga lekunatsa kumaphabhu aseBritain lanebumatima futsi kwavaka kucindzeteleka lokukhulu etindzaweni tekudlela.
Emacembu emaphambu nemabhala abone kukhuphuka lizinga lekutsenga ngemaphesenti langu- 2.7 ngaKholwane - kepha etindzaweni tekudlela lehle ngemaphesenti la-4.8, tibalo letikhishiwe.
Peter Martin, webhizinisi yebunjingalwati i-CGA, leyahlanganisa lamanani, utsite: "Kuchubeka kwekukhanya kwelilanga ekuhlanganyeleni kweNgilandi lokudze kwendlula loko bekulindzelwe eNdzebeni Yemhlaba kusho kutsi Kholwane ulandzele iphethini lefanananko neyenyanga yeNhlaba leyendlulile, ngesikhatsi emaphabhu bekasetulu ngemaphesenti langu-2.8, ngaphandle kwekutsi tindzawo tekudlela tashayeka kakhulu kunakucalar.
Kwehla ngemasenti langu-1.8 kutekuhwebelana kwetindzawo tekudlela ngeNhlaba kwaba kubi kakhulu ngaKholwane.
Emaphabhu laholwa kunatsa tjwala kanye nemabhala asebenta kahle kakhulu kunetindzawo tekudlela.
Emaphabhu laholwa kudla nawo alinyatwa lilanga, nanoma-nje akufanananga nebachubi betindzawo tekudlela.
Kubonakala sengatsi bantfu bebafuna kuhamba bayonatsa.
Kuwo onkhe emabhaphu lalawulwako nasemabhaleni lizinga lakutsenga lakhuphuka ngemaphesenti la-6.6 ngaleyo nyanga, kwatsi kudla kona kwehla ngemaphesenti lamatsatfu."
Paul Newman, weluhlatiyo lwetekungcebeleka nekukhibika we-RSM utsite: "Lemiphumela lena ichubeka nendlelakwenta lesiyibone kusukela ekupheleni kwaMabasa.
Simo selitulu nelifutse lemidlalo lemikhulu yetenhlalo liyachubeka nekutsi yimbangela lenkhulu mayelana neliziunga lekutsenga emakethe lengaphandle kwasekhaya.
Kuyintfo lemangalisananko kutsi emacembu etindzawo tekudlela ayachubeka nekuba nebumatima, nanoma-nje lizinga lekutsenga likhuphuke ngemaphesento la-4.8 ngemnyaka kutawuba yintfo lebuhlungu eukwencindzetelo lechubekako.
Lelihlobo lelidze lelishisako lifike ngesikhatsi lesibi kulabasebenta ngekudla futsi kutawukhuluma sikhatsi mayelana nekutsi tio telitulu letisemkhatsini lesihlangabetene nato ngenyanga yeNgci kutawuniketa sikhashana lesidzingeka kakhulu."
Linani lelizinga lekutsengisa kuwo onkhe emaphabhu netindzawo tekudlela, kufaka ekhatsi lokusha lokuvuliwe, bekungemaphesenti la-2.7 ngaKholwane, lokukhombisa kuhamba kancane kwekukhishwa kwetinhlobo.
Umlandzeleli welizinga lemboni lekutsenga i-Coffer Peach Tracker lemkhakha wephabhu,libhala nendzawo yekudlela yase-UK, uyagcogca aphindze ahlatiye imininingwane yekusebenta emacenjini lasebentako lange-47, ngembuyiselo lehlanganisiwe lengetulu kwetigidzi leti-£9, futsi kusikalo semboni lesimeme.
Umntfwana munye kulabasihlanu unema-akhawunti etinkhundla tekuchumana lawafihlela batali bakhe
Umntfwana munye kulabasihlanu - labanye babancane baneminyaka le-11 - banema-akhawunti etinkhundla tekuchumana labawafihlela batali babo nabothishela babo, luklayo lukhombisa kanjalo
Luklayo lwebantfwana besikolwa bemabanga laphakeme laba-20,000 lukhombise kukhula kwemakhasi "e-Insta mbumbulu"
letindzaba tiphakamise kwesaba kutsi kushicilelwa tintfo tetemacansi
Bantfwana besikolwa labangemaphesenti langemashumi lamabili batsite bane-akhawunti "lenguyona yona" labayikhombisa batali babo
Umntfwana munye kulaba labasihlanu - labanye babancane baneminyaka le-11 budzala - benta ema-akhawunti etindlela tekuchumana labagcina ayimfinhlo bawafihlele batali babo.
Luklayo lwebantfwana besikolwa bemabanga laphakeme langange-20,000 lukhombise lizinga lelikhula ngemandla lema-akhawunti "-Insta mbumbulu" - emasayithi ekwabelana ngetitfombe e-Instagram.
Letindzaba leti tikhulise lizinga lekwesaba kutsi kushicilelwa tintfo tetemacansi.
Bnatfwana besikolwa labangemaphesenti langemashumi lamabili batsi bachuba i-akhawunti "lenguyona yona" llehlobile kukhombisa batali, babe futsi banema-akhawunti layimfihlo.
Lomunye make lowatikhandza akusayithi leyimfihlo yendvodzakati yakhe leneminyaka le-13 watfola lomunye umuntfu lomusha acela labanye atsi "ngidlwenguleni."
Lucwaningo, lolwentiwe yi-Digital Awareness UK neNkhomfa yaboThishelanhloko Labadvuna" kanye naBothishelanhloko Lababomake" (i-HMC) betikolwa letitimele,batfola emaphesenti lange-40 ebnatfwana labaneminya le-11 kuya kule-18 budzala bebanemaphrofayili lamabili, futsi ihhafu yabo bavuma kutsi banema-akhawunti angasense.
Sikhulu se-HMC Mike Buchanan watsi: "Kuyaphazamisa kutsi lusha lolunyneti lwakha ema-akhwunti ku-inthanethi lapho khona batali nabothishela bangeke babatfole."
Eilidh Doyle utawuba "livi lema-athilethi" kubhodi yeMa-athilethi YaseScotland
Eilidh Doyle ukhetfwe kuba kubhodi yeMa-athilethi YaseScotland njengemcondzisi longekho kusigungu lesiphetse emhlanganweni wemtimba lophetse wemnyaka.
Doyle longumu-athilethi waseScotland' wemzila lohlotjisiwe newendzima futsi sihlalo Ian Beattie uchaze loku njengelitfuba lelikhulu lalalbo labakhombindlela temidlalo kutsi bazuze kubukadzebona bakho lobubanti ezingeni lemave emhlaba kulomnyakalishumi lowendlulile.
"Eilidh uhlonishwa kakhulu emmangweni wema-athilethi waseScotland, e-UK nasemhlabeni futsi sinesiciniseko sekutsi tema-athilethi eScotland titawuzuza kakhulu ngekutsi bamfake kubhodi,"kwasho Beattie.
Doyle watsi: "Nginemdlandla wekusebenta njegelivi lema-athilethi futsi nginelitsemba lekutsi ngingafaka ligalelo ngiphindze futsi ngisite ngicondzise lomhlalo eScotland."

Sikhangiso sephampu yemabele lesicatsanisa bomake netinkhomo sehlukanisa ekhatsi imibono ku-inthanethi
Inkampani yemaphampu emabambela inembono lohlukene ekhatsi ku-inthanethi ngenca yesikhangiso lesicatsanisa bomake labamunyisako netikhomo natisengwa.
Kwetfula loku lokutsiwa "yiphampu yemhlaba lethulile legcokekako," inkampani yebatsengi yetebucwephshe i-Elvie ikhiphe sikhangiso sevidiyo yemculo yekucaphela lokushiwokokukhombisa inkhululeko lephampu lensha leyinika bomake labamunyisako.
Bomake mbamba labane badansa esibayeni sekudla kwetinkhomo badansela ingoma lefaka ekhatsi emagama lafana nalawa: "Yebo, ngiyatisenga mine ngekwami, kepha kute umsila lowubonako" nalatsi "Mhlawumbe awukacapheli lena akusiyo imibele, ngemabele ami."
lelikhorasi liyachubeka litsi: "Phampa ulukhiphe, phampa ulukhiphe, ngondla bantfwana, luphampe ulukhiphe, luphampe ulukhiphe, ngisenga bafati bami."
Nanoma kunjalo,lesikhangiso, lesishicilelwe ekhasini le-Facebook lalenkampani, sibange kuphikisana lokukhulu ku-inthanethi.
Ngemibono le-77,000 netiphakamiso letingemakhulukhulu, levidiyo itfole timphendvulo leticubene kubabukeli, lapho linyenti litsi itsatsela phansi "lusizi lolukhulu" lwemboni yetelubisi.
"Sincumo lesibi kabi sekusebentisa tinkhomo kukhangisa lomkhicito.
Njengatsi didzinga kwemitsa bese tiyatala kute kutsi tikhiphe lubisi, ngaphandle kwekutsi ematfole ato ayantjontjwa kuto kungapheli malanga mangaki tiwatele," kwabhala lomunye.

Linani lebantfwana lababachamuki labatokisiwe selikhule kakhulu nanoma-nj etinhlalo tekwewela umnyele tichubeka nekungagucuki, ngalokuyincenye ngoba tinchubomgomo letifananako naletimatima letingeniswe lulawulo lwaTrump lukwente kwaba matima kubeka bantfwana kubasiti.
Ngalokwetayelekile,basiti labanyenti babachamuki labangakabhaliswa bona ngekwabo, futsi besaba kumosha kuchubeka nekuhlala kulelive kwabo ngekutsi baphumele ebaleni batsatse labantfwana.
Lobungoti bakhula ngeNhlaba, ngesikhatsi tiphatsimandla tenhlangano timemetela kutsi labo labangaba basiti kanye nemalunga emindeni yabo bafanele kutsi bangenise tinyatseliso teminwe yabo, nekutsi futsi leyo mininingwane kutawabelwana ngayo netiphatsimandla tebachamuki.

Ekuhambeni kwesikhatsi le-ejensi icinisekise kutsi lababoshiwe labangemaphesenti lange-70 bebete emarekhodi ebugebengu aphambilini.
"Cishe emaphesenti lange-80 ebantfu lababasiti noma emalunga emindeni yebasiti bakulelive ngalokungekho emtsetfweni futsi linyenti labo batigebengu.
Ngako-ke siyachubeka nekulandzelela labo bantfu," kwasho Mnu. Albence.
Ngekufuna kwenta inchubo yalabantfwana masinyane, tikhulu tangenisa umtsetfomgomo lomusha lotawudzinga kutsi labanye babo bavele enknatolo kungakapheli inyanga batokisiwe, kunekutsi kube ngemuva kwemalanga lange-60, lebekukadze kulizing alaphambilini, ngekuya kwebasebneti betindzawo tekukhosela.

ISyria itjela umkhosi wemphi waseMelika, eFulansi newaseTurky kutsi uphume masinyane lapho ukanekise khona
Akhulume Emhlnganweni Lowetayelekile we-UN, Indvuna yeTetebudlelwano Nekubambisana Kwemave Emhlaba Walid al-Moualem uphindze watjela bakhoseli baseSyria kutsi babuye ekhaya, nanoma-nje imphi yalelive nyawo isemnyakeni wayo wesiphohlongo.
Moualem, lophindze futsi abe lisekelandvu nakhulu, lemikhosi yemphi yalamanye emave isemhlabeni weSyrian ngalokungekho emtsetfweni, ngaphasi kwelekutsi balwa nebuphekulasikhuni, futsi "kutawubukwana nabo ngalokufanele."
"Bafanele kutsi baphume masinyane futsi ngaphandle kwetincabekelwane," watjela lomhlangano.
Moualem waphikelela watsi "kulwa nebuphekulasikhuni sekucishe kufike ekugcineni" eSyria, lapho khona sekushone bantfu labangetulu kwalaba-360,000 pekusukela nga-2011, lapho khona tigidzi letinyenti tikhishiwe emakhaya ato.
Watsi Damascus utawuchubeka "alwe lemphi engcwele kut ekube ngulapho sicedza onkhe emaphekulasikhuni aseSyria "kokubili emacembu ekwesabisa kanye "nanoma ngubuphi bukhona bebuchamuki."
Imelika inemasotja emphi la-2,000 eSyria, ikakhulu laceceshako naleluleka imikhosi yemphi yemaKurdish nema-Arabhu aseSyrian lamelene neMengameli Bashar al-Assad.
Ifulansi inemasotja emphi yaphasi langetulu kwala-1,000 kulelive levitsitwe yimphi.
Mayelana neludzaba lwebakhoseli, Moualem watsi timo tilungile kutsi bangabuya, waphindze futsi wasola "lamanye emave asenshonalanga" ngekutsi "abhebhetsekise kwesaba lokungenasizatfu" lokwente bakhoseli kutsi bangabuyi.
"Sicele ummango wemave emhlaba kanye netinhlangano letibakekela bantfu kutsi tichubo loludzaba lwekubuya,"kwasho yena.
"Benta ludzaba lwetekunakekelwa kwebantfu kutsi lube ludzaba lwetepolitiki."
Imelika neNhlangano Yebunye BeYurophu bacaphelise ngekutsi angeke lubekhona lusito lwekwakha kabusha lweSyria kute kuba ngulapho kunekuvumelana kwetepolitiki emkhatsi wa-Assad nalaphakisako kuya ekupheleni kwemphi.
Emancusa e-UN atsi sivumelwane lesisandza kwentiwa emkhatsi weRussia neTurkey sekutsi kwentiwe indzawo lesemkhatsini endzaweni lenkhulu yemaphekulasikhuni ase-Idlib sekwente litfuba lekuchubeka netingcoco tetepolitiki.
Sivumelwane seRussia neTurky savimba kulinyatwa lokukhula kweRussia lobekucgutjwa ngumbutfo wemphi waseSyria kulesifundza, lapho kuhlala khona bantfu labatigidzi letintsatfu.
Moualem nanoma kunjalo wagcizelela kutsi lesivumelwane "besinemincamulajucu lecacile " waphindze wavakalisa litsemba lekutsi sinyatselo setemphi sitawucondza ema-jihads kufaka ekhatsi tilwi letivela e-Al-Qaeda-linked Nusra Front, "lelitawubhujiswa."
Lincusa le-UN Staffan de Mistura letsemba kutsi masinyane-nje litawubita umhlangano wekucala welikomidi lelisha lokufaka ekhatsi hulumende kanye nemalunga elicembu leliphikisako kutsi kubhalwe inchubomgomo yangemuva kwemphi yeSyria bese kuvulwa indlela leya elukhetfweni.
Moualem wabeka tincabekelwana tekuhlanganyela kwahulumende waseSyria kulelikomidi, watsi umsebenti wephaneli ufanele kutsi ubekelwe umkhawulo "wekubuyeketa ema-athikili emtsetfosisekelo lokhona kwamanje," waphindze wacaphilisa ngekufakw akwelunyawo lwengulube.

Imelika Weighed Penalizing El Salvador Over Support for China, Then Backed Off
Emancusa abona kutsi iDominican Republic nePanama had besebavele bayemukele iBeijing, ngekusiphalata lokuncane kweWashington.
Mnu.Trump waba nemhlangano lomuhle neMengameli Juan Carlos Varela of Panama ngeNhlaba-2017futsi bekanelihhotela ePanama kwate kwaba ngulapho balingani bacosha licembu lelilawula Inhalnagno yaTrump.
Tikhulu telitiko lembuso lancuma kubita tikhulu temishini teMelika kutsi tibuye tisuka e-El Salvador, iDominican Republic nePanama mayelana "netincumo letisandza kutsatfwa tekutsi kungasanakwa iTaiwan," Heather Nauert,make lokhulumela litiko, washo kusitatimende nakusuka lenyanga.
Kepha tinhlawulo tacondziswa ku-El Salvador,leyatfola tigidzi letilinganiselwe leti- $140 telusito lweMelika nga-2017, kufaka ekhatsi yekulawula tidzakamiva, kutfutfukisa kanye nekwesekela umnotfo.
Letinhlawulo letiphakanyisiwe, lebetifaka ekhatsi kuncishiswa kwelusito lwetimali kanye nemikhawulo yemavisa, bekutawuba yintfo lebuhlungu yeNkhaba yeMelika kanye netilinganiso tekubate imisebenti nekubulalana.
lapho imihlangano yangekhatsi ichubekela embili, tikhulu teNyakatfo yeMelika neNkhaba yeMelika bahlelhlisa tinkhomfa telizinga leliphakeme tagcila kutekuphepha nekundlondlobala kwetemnotfo kulandzela imibutano yalolo luhlobo yemnyaka lophelile kwabonakala njengesinyatselo lesiya embili emitameni yekuvimbela bachamuki kutsi bangayi eMelika.
Kepha kwatsi emkhatsini weNyoni, tikhulu letinkhulu letilawulako takucacisa kutsi tifuna lenkhomfa kutsi ichubeke, ngemphumelelo kucedvwe konkhe kucabanga ngekuhlawulisa i-El Salvador.

Sebenta kanye nemeluleki wakho nemndeni wakho nikhulumisane ngekutsi utawunakekelwa kanjnai futsi kuphi, ngoba leto tincumo tingaba yintfo lebalulekile ekuncumeni tindleko.

Kutamatama kwemhlana nematsunamis e-Indonesia
Lokungenani kushone bantfu lange-384 babulawa kutamatama kwemhlaba lokunemandla kanye netsunami leshaye lidolobhakati lase-Indonesia iPalu ngaLesihlanu, kwasho tikhulu, futsi kulindzeleke kutsi linani lalabashonako likhuphuke.
Njengoba tindlela tekuchumana tincamukile, tikhulu tekuhhamula betingakhoni kutfolwa lwatiso ku-ejendi yeDonggala, indzawo lesenyakato yePalu letfute kakhulu nenkhaba yelidolobha lapho kwenteke khona umonakalo wekutamatama kwemhlaba lokunemandla la-7.5.
EPalu, bantfu labangetulu kwala ba-16,000 bakhishwa ngesikhatsi kwenteka lenhlekelele.
Nati tintfo letibalulekile ngePalu neDonggala, esichiwini saseSulawesi:
IPalu iyinhlokodolobha yeNkhaba yesifundza iSulawesi, lesekugcineni yelugu loluncane elugwini lolusenshonalanga yesichiwei iSulawes, lenelinanibantfu lelilinganiselwa ku-379,800 nga-2017.
Lelidolobhakati beligubha umkhosi weminyaka lenge-40 ngesikhatsi lihlaselwa kutamatama kwemhlaba kanye netsunami.
Donggalayindzawo leyelule ngalokungetulu kwe-300 km (emamayela la-180) elusentse lwelugu ngasengakatfonshonalanga yesichiwi iSulawesi.
lendzawo,sigodzi selulawulo lesingaphasi lwesifundza, besinelinanibantfu lelilinganisela ku-299,200 nga-2017.
Kudweba tinhlanti kanye nekulima ngutona tintfo letinkhulu temnotfo walesifundza lesiyiNkhaba yeSulawesi, ikakhulu sigodzi lesingaselwandle seDonggala.
Kumbiwa we-Nickel kupgindze kube ngulenye intfo lebalulekile kulesifundza, kodvwa itfolakala kakhulu eMorowali, elugwini lolubukene neSulawesi.
IPalu neDonggala kuhlaselwe ngematsunamis emahlandla lamanyenti kuleminyaka le-100 leyendlulile, ngekuya kwe-Ejensi Yekunciphisa Tinhlekelele yase-Indonesia.
Nga-1938,itsunami yabulala bantfu labangetulu kwalabange-200 people yaphindze futsi yabhubhisa tindlu letingemakhulukhulu eDonggala.
Itsunami yaphindze futsi yahlasela inshonalanga yeDonggala nga-1996, yabulala bantfu labayimfica.
I-Indonesia ihleti endzaweni leyindingilizi Yemlilo we-Pacific letsandvwa kuhlalela kutamatama kwemhlaba njalo-nje.
Naku lokunye kutamatama kwemhlaba kanye nematsunami lamakhulu aleminyaka lesandza kwendlula:
2004: Kutamatama kwemhlaba lokukhulu ngaselugwini lwasenshonalanga esifundzeni se-Indonesia i-Aceh ngasenyakatfo Sumatra ngeNgongoni mhla tinge-26 lokwacubula itsunami leyahlasela emave la-14, yabulala bantfu laba-226,000 elusentseni lweLwandle LwaseNdiya, futsi labangetulu kwehhafu base-Aceh.
2005: Luchungechunge lwekutamatama kwemhlaba lokunemandla kwahlasela lugu lwangasenshonalanga yeSumatra ngasekupheleni kweNdlovulenkhulu nakusuka mabasa.
Emakhulukhulu ahona eNias Island, ngaselugwini lweSumatra.
2006: Lokunemandla la-6.8 kwahlasela inshonalanga yeJava, sichiwi sase-Indonesia lesinebantfu labanyenti, lokwacubula itsunami leyashaya elugwini lolungaseningisimi, labulala bantfu labange-700.
2009: Kutamatama kwemhlaba lokunemandla la-7.6 kwashaya dvute nelidolobhakati iPadang, inhlokodolobha yesifundza seNshonalanga yeSumatra.
Kwafa bantfu labangetulu kwalaba-1,100.
2010: Kutamatama kwemhlaba lokunemandla la-7.5 yashaya sinye setichiwi teMentawai, eSumatra, kwacubula itsunami lebeyingafika kumamitha la-10 lebhubhisa emadazini emimango yaphindze futsi yabulala bantfu labalinganiselwa kulabange-300.
2016: Kutamatama kwemhlaba lokuncane kwashaya iPidie Jaya e-Aceh, kwabanga umonakala nekwetfuka ngoba bantfu bakhumbula kukhateka lokukhulukati kwekutamatama kwemhlaba netsunami yanga-2004 leyabulala bantfu labanyenti.
Kute itsunami leyacubuleka, kodvwa kwafa bantfu labangetulu kwalaba-100 lalbagcotjwa takhiwo letadzilika.
2018: Kutamatama lokukhulukati kushaye sichiwi setivakashi sase-Indonesia saseLombok, kwafa bantfu labangetulu kwalabange-500, ikakhulu ngaseluhlangotsini lwesichiwi lesisenyakatfo.
Lokutamatama kwemhlaba kwabhubhisa tinkhulungwane netinkhulungwane tetindlu futsi tivakashi tasala tindzindza.

Bashushisi beFederal bafuna sigwebo sentsambo lesngakavami semsolwa wesidlamlilo wase-NYC
Bashushisi beFederal eNew York bafuna sigwebo sentsambo saSayfullo Saipov, losolwa ngekuhlaselwa ngekwebudlamlilo kweNew York City lokubulele bantfu labasiphohlongo -- sijeziso lesingakavami lebesiniketwa nglelive mayelana nemacala ebufederali kusukela nga-1953.
Saipov, loneminyaka lenge-30, usolwa kutsi wasebentisa imoto yakaHome Depot lerentiwe kute achube luhlaselo endleleni yetidududu eMgwacweni Longutselwa Wayekela eWest Side eLower Manhattan, ashayisa labahamba ngetinyawo nalabagibele emabhayisikili ngeMphela.
Kute kutsi kwesekelwe sigwebo sakhe sentsambo, bashoshisi bafanel ekutsi banikete bufakazi bekutsi Saipov wabulala labahlaselwa labasiphohlongo "ngenhloso" waphindze futsi walimata kabuhlungu "ngenhloso", ngekuya kwalesatiso senhloso yekutfola sigwebo sentsambo, sicelo sase lesifakwe eSifundzeni saseNingizimu saseNew York.
Omabili lawo macala ngewesigwebo sentsambo, ngekuya kwemadokhumenti asenkantolo.
Emaviki ngemuva kwaloluhlaselo, basiti belijaji labakhulu befederali bashaye Saipov ngemacala labhalwe phasi lange-22 labekafaka ekhatsi ekubulawa kwebantfu labasiphohlongo ngenloso yekukhwaphanisa, lokuvamise kwentiwa bashushisi befederali emcaleni lahleliwe, kanye nelicala lebudlova nekumosha imoto.
Lokuhlasela kudzinge "kuhlela lokukhulu nekucabanga phambilini,"kwasho bashushisi, bachaza lendlela Saipov lenta ngalo lelicala "lelibi kakhulu, nelunya lekungabi nesimilo."
"Sayfullo Habibullaevic Saipov wabangela kulimala, ingoti, nekulahlekewal kwalemindeni nebangani baDiego Enrique Angelini, Nicholas Cleves, Ann-Laure Decadt, Darren Drake, Ariel Erlij, Hernan Ferruchi, Hernan Diego Mendoza, kanye na-Alejandro Damian Pagnucco," kwasho satiso senhloso.
Labasihlanu balabahlaselwa bekutivakashi tase-Argentina.
Sekuphele iminyaka lelishumi Sifundza saseNingizimu saseNew Yorksagcina kushushisa licala lentsambo.
Umbekwacala, Khalid Barnes, ulahlwe licala lekubulala batsengisi betidzakamiva lababili kodvwa wagcina agwetjwe kudzilikelwa lijele ngeNyoni 2009.
Kugwetjwa intsambo kwekugcina lokwentiwa eNew York ecaleni lefederali bekungu-1953 kwaJulius na-Ethel Rosenberg, labebashadene bajutjwa ngemuva kwekulahlwa licala lekuba tinhloli teSoviet Union ngesikhatsi seMphi Yekubukana kabi iminyaka lemibili ngembi kwaloko.
Bobabili boRosenbergs babulawa ngekuhlaliswa esitulweni sagezi ngeNhlaba mhla ti-19, 1953.
Saipov, longumsinsi wekumbelwa wase-Uzbekistan, wakhombisa kungadzabuki ngetento takhe emalangeni nasetuinyangeni ngemuva kwalokuhlasela kwakhe, ngekuya kwemaadokhumenti asenkantolo.
Watjela emaphoyisa kutsi utiva ukahle ngaloko lakwentile, kwasho emaphoyisa.
Saipov utsi watfola inshisekelo yekubulala ngemuva kwekubukela ividiyo ye-ISIS elucingweni lwakhe, ngekuya kwemadokhumenti elicala.
Waphindze futsi wacela kukhangisa ngemjeka we-ISIS egumbini lakhe lasesibhedlela, kwasho emaphoyisa.
Akawavumanga emacala akhe lange-22 kulamadokhumenti asenkantolo.
David Patton, lomunye webavikeli bemmange befederali lomelele Saipov, watsi "baphocekile sibili" ngesincume sekushushiswa.
"Sicabanga kutsi sincumo sekufuna sigwebo sentsambo kunekutsi emukele licala adzilikelwe lijele lokute litfuba lekutsi angakhululwa kutawudvosa kukhahlabeteka kwengcondvo kwalehlakalo kuwo wonkhe lotsintsekako," kwasho Patton.
Licembu lelivikela Saipov ekucaleni belicele bashushisi kutsi bangasifuni sigwebo sentsambo.

Sifuna kutishayela yetfu imitsetfo eveni letfu.'

Inkampani yetindizamshini lebeyichuba inidzamshini lephahlateke elwandle iPacific eMicronesia itsi manje kukhona indvodza lelahlekile, ngemuva kwkeutsi itsi bonkhe bagebeli lange-47 nelibutfo lebasebenti bayitakule ngalokuphephile lendizamshini lebeyicwila.
Inkampani Yetindizamshini yakaNiugini itsite kusukela ngeMgcibelo emini, beyingakwati kutilandze ngemgibeli lomdvuna.
Lenkampani yetindizamshini itsite isebenta netiphatsimandla tendzawo, tibhedlela nebaphenyi kutsi betame kuyitfola lendvodza.
Lenkampani yetindizamshini ayikaphendvuli masinye kulesicelo semininingwane leminyenti mayelana nalomgibeli, njengeminyaka yayo yebudzala nebuve bayo.
Tikebhe tendzawo tisitile kutakula laba labanye bagibeli nelibutfo lebasebenti ngemuva kwekutsi lendizamshini itsintse emanti ngesikhatsi yetama kuhlala esikhumulweni setindizamshini seSichiwi iChuuk.

Kushushiswa kwemisa licala lako ngeMgcibelo ecaleni lendvodza lebekwe licala lekushisa umfati waseMississippi aphila nga-2014.
Imelika Umhlatiyi Welitiko Letebulungiswa laseMelika Paul Rowlett wetfula bufakazi ema-awa lamanyenti njengafakazi loyingcweti emkhakheni wetekuhlatiya temshoshaphansi.
Wendlale libandla lebasiti belijaji kutsi wawasebentisa kanjani emarekhodi amakhalekhikhini kuhlanganisa kuhamba kwemmangalelwa loneminyaka lenge-29 budzala Quinton Tellis nemhlukunyetwa leneminyaka le-19 budzala, Jessica Chambers, ngebusuku lashona ngabo.

Sanford wagibla ebhokisini ngeMgcibelo wafakaza kutsi yena bekangekho edolobheni ngalelo langa.
Ngesiskhatsi bashushisi babuta kutsi ingabe Tellis bekakhuluma liciniso yini ngesikhatsi atsi bekasemotweni yaSanford ngalobo busuku, Sanford watsi "bekacamba emanga, ngoba lemoto beyiseNashville."
Lokunye lebekungacondzi kutsi Tellis watsi besekucishe kungemaviki lamabili atana naChambers ngesikhatsi afa.
Emarekhodi amakhalekhikhini akhombise kutsi bekuliviki linye batana.
Rowlett ngesikhatsi lesitsite ngemuva kwekushona kwaChambers, Tellis wasusa elucingweni lwakhe ematheksti, emarekhodi ekusahayelwa lucingo kanye nemininingwane yekutsintsana yaChambers.

Labatsatfu bemculo we-hip hop bafuna kuneketa umcondvo longasimuhle insayeya mayelana naloluhlobo lwemculo ngekutsi umculo wabo bawugcwalise ngemilayeto leyakhako.

Lomunye umuntfu lomnyama?!
Umgadzi webantfwana wase-NY imangalela umfati nedvodza ngemuva kwekumcosha ngemuva kwetheksti "lebandlulula ngwekwebuhlanga"
Umgadzi webantfwana waseNew York umangalela umfati nendvodza ngekumcosha ngalokubandlululako ngemuva kwekutsi itheksti lephambukile levela kumake wemntfwana akhonona ngekutsi "ngulomunye umuntfu lomnyama."
Lomfati nalendvodza bayaphika kutsi babandlulula ngekwebuhlanga, bafananasisa lokumangalelwa "njengekuntjontjelwa imali."
Lynsey Plasco-Flaxman, make webantfwana lababili,ukhombise kumangala nakatfola kutsi lomgadzi webantfwana lomusha, Giselle Maurice, ngumuntfu lomnyama ngelilanga lakhe lekucala nakefika emsebentini nga-2016.
"HHAYI BOOOOOOOOOOOO UMUNTFU LOMNYAMA FUTSI," kwabhala Nkkt. Plasco-Flaxman abhalela indvodza yakhe umlayeto.
Nanoma kunjalo, esikhundleni sekutsi awutfumele indvodza yakhe, wawutfumela kuMk. Maurice, kabili .
Utsite nakabona kutsi wente liphutsa,Plasco-Flaxman "lobekangahlaliseki" wabese ucosha Mk. Maurice, watsi lomnakekeli webantfwana lohambile, lobekanguMelika wase-Afrika, bekente umsebenti lomubi nekutsi futsi bekalindzele umuntfu longumFilipino, ngekuya kweNew York Post.
Mk. Maurice wakhokhelwa imali yakhe yelilanga linye wabe uyiswa ekhaya nge-Uber.
Manje, Maurice umangalela lmake nendvodza yakhe kute kutsi bamncephetele ngalokumcosha kwabo, futsi ufuna sincephelo se-$350 ngelilanga tinyanga letisitfupha, kuhlala emsebentini labekacashelwe kona, kodvwa ngaphandle kwekontileka.
"Ngifuna kubakhombisa, buka, awuyenti intfo lefana naleyo," watjela i-Post ngaLesihlanu, engeta ngekutsi "ngiyati kutsi kubandlulula."
Lomake nalendvodza batiphendvulele ngelekutsi abasibe babandlululi, batsi kuncamula ikontileka yaMaurice bekuyintfo lelungile kuyenta, besaba kutsi abakwati kumetsemba ngemuva kwekumtfukutselisa.
"Umfati wami utfumele intfo labekangacondzi kuyisho.
Akasiye umbandlululi.
Asisibo bantfu lababandlulanako,"indvodza Joel Plasco watjela i-Post.
"Kodvwa bantfwana bakho ungabashiya yini etandleni temuntfu lobe luhlata kuye, ngisho noma ngabe loko kwenteke ngeliphutsa?
Umntfwana wakho losandza kutalwa?
Cabanga."
Afananasisa lokumangelelwa “njengekuntjontjelwa," Plasco watsi umkakhe unetinyanga letimbili abelekile futsi "bekasesimeni lesimatima."
"Utawenta loko kumuntfu?
Loko akusiyo intfo lenhle kuyenta," kwangeta sobhange welutjalomali.
Lapho lelicala letemtsetfo lisachubeka, inkantolo yemibono yemmango isheshile kucitsa lomfati nalelndvondza etinkhundleni tekuchumana, bangevani ngekutiphatsa kwabo nendlela labacabanga ngayo.

Indvodzakati yaBond Karen Jankel, lowatalwa masinyane-nje ngemuva kwekutsi lencwadzi ivunywe, watsi mayelana nalencwadzi: "Kumatima kutifaka eticatfulweni talomunye umuntfu kuyifundza kwekucala ngembi kwkeutsi ishicilelwe.

Atsi babe wakhe losebente njengemtfwebuli wetitfombe ka-BBC ngembi kwekutsi abe nenshisekelo yekubhala incwadzi yebantfwana yelithoyisi lelibhele lelincane,bekatawube acabanga ngekwaliwa kwemsebenti wakhe,waphindze futsi wengeta kutsi umkhosi wekugubha kushicilelwa kwalencwandzi we-60 "wayintfo lebuhlungu nalemnandzi" ngemuva kwekushona kwakhe kulomnyaka lophelile.
Mayelana naPaddington, lochazwa ngekutsi "lilunga lemndeni lelibaluleke kahulu,"wengeta ngelekutsi babe wakhe bekatigcabha ngalokuthulile mayelana nemphumelelo yakhe.
"Bekayindvodza lethulile, futsi bekangasiyo indvodza letikhukhumetako," kwasho yena.

Ngicabanga kutsi wabuka imohumelelo yaPaddington ngaleyo ndlela.
Nanoma-nje bekukucamba kwakhe nekucabanga kwakhe, bakavamisa kunika Paddington ludvumo."

Bebavamisa kutsi kumamatseka kwakhe kukhanyisa ligumbi lonkhe."

Mk. Davis wakha lamakhati, "kwatisa bantfu kutsi kukhona bantfu longaya kubo ukhulume nabo, ngisho noma ngabe ngumngani.
Ungahlali uthule -ufanele kutsi ukhulume."

"Akazange asho kutsi uva umoya wakhe ushona phasi noma yiva ukhahlabetekile noma yini,"kwasho yena.
"Ngemalanga lambalwa ngembi kwaKhisimusi sacaphela ingcuko kusimongcondvo sakhe.
Bekasafike ekugcineni ngeLilanga laKhimusi - ngesikhatsi bantfwana bamnika tipho akazange ababuke emehlweni noma abuke lokunye."

Kusidzabula ekhatsi.

Linani lebantfu baseNyakatfo Korea labashiye live labo bawele ngaphasi kwaKim
Linani lebantfu baseNorth Korea labashiye live labo baya eNingizimu Korea bawile kusukela ngesiskhatsi Kim Jong-un atsatsa sihlalo eminyakeni lesikhombisa leyendlulile, njengekusha kwebagwayimitsetfo baseNingizimu Korea.
Park Byeong-seug, acaphuna kumininingwane yeministri yekuhlanganisa yaseNingizimu, utsite kube khona lashiye live labo laba-1,127 kulomnyaka lophelile - nakucatsaniswa ne-2,706 nga-2011.
Mnu. Park utsite kulawulwa kweminyele emkhatsini weNyankatfo Korea neShayina kanye natilinganiso letisetulu letikhokhiswa bantfu labafihla bantfu tintfo letibalulekile.
Pyongyang kute kuphawula lakwentile esiveni.
Linyenti lalabantfu labashiye live labo lnyakatfo bagcina banikwa bakhamuti baseNingizimu Korea.
Seoul utsi bangetulu kwe-30,000 bantfu baseNyakatfo Korean labawele iminyele ngalokungekho emtsefweni kusukela kwaphela Imphi yaseKorea nga-1953.
Linyenti libaleka lendlule eShayina, lenemnyele lomudze kakhulu kantsi eNyakatfo Korea kweweleka kalula kune Demilitarised Zone (DMZ) levikeleke kakhulu lesemkhatsini walamaKorea lamabili.
ishayini itsi labantfu labashiya live labo bachamuki labangekho emtstfweni kunekutsi bakhoseli futsi ivamise kubabuyisela emuva ngenkhani.
Buhlobo emkhatsi weNyakatfo neNingizimu - lokusalwa - sebube ncono kakhulu kuletinyanga letisandza kwendlula.
Ekucaleni kwalenyanga, baholi balamave lamabili bahlangene ePyongyang mayelana netinkhulumo nekususa inuzi.
Loku kuvele ngemuv akwemhlangano wangeNhlaba lobowusemkhatsini waMengameli waseMelika Donald Trump naKim Jong-un eSingapore, lapho bavumele khona ngemibandela lebanti kutsi basebentela kutsi indzawo yaseKorea letungeletwe ngemanti ibete inuzi.

"Kute lokunye bengingakwenta ngaphandle kwekucabanga kuts nangane umfati ente ngalendlela, batakusho 'ngesibibitfwane,'" kwasho Pelosi ngendlela labukene ngayo nebufakazi baKavanaugh ngembi kweLikomidi Letebulungiswa Letimphunga ngaLesine.

Imphi yetekuhwebelana neMelika neShayina ingaba yintfo lenhle kuBeijing
Kuvula kwetikhali temphi yetekuhwebelana emkhatsini weMelika neShayina bekukubi kkahulu, futsi lapho lemphi isesekhashane kakhulu nekuphela, umkhatsi emkhatsini walamave unga yinzuzo kuBeijing esikhatsini lesidze, kwsho ingcweti.
Donald Trump, Mengameli waseMelika, ukhiphe secwayiso sekucala ekucaleni kwalomnyaka ngekutsi atselise imikhicto lebalulekile levela eShayina kufaka ekahsti emaphaneli agezi welilanga, insimbi ne-aluminiyamu.
Kubhebhetseka lokukhulu kakhulu kuphume kuleliviki lapho khona ematharifu lamasha latsintsa tigidzi letinge-$200 (tigidzi letinge-£150) wetintfo, lokugcine kutseliswa ihhafu netimphahla letingena eMelika tisuka eShayina.
